## 中药(藥)
---
## traditional Chinese medicine
### zhōng yào
---
- **traditional:** 中藥
- **definition:** traditional Chinese medicine
- **pinyin:** zhōng yào
- **components:**
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle; central
  - 药(藥)
    - yào
    - medicine; cure; drug
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 中 (zhōng, "middle; central") refers to both the geographical and cultural centrality of China. 藥 (yào, "medicine") means medicine and is used in the context of treatment or healing.
  - **interpretation:** The term 中 (zhōng, "middle; central") connects to China's geographic and cultural position as a central and ancient civilization with a long history of medicinal practices. 藥 (yào, "medicine") signifies substances used for healing. Together, 中藥 (zhōngyào, "traditional Chinese medicine") refers to the traditional medicinal practices and substances developed within Chinese culture. This combination emphasizes the concept of Chinese medicine as originating from and central to China's cultural and historical identity.
- **examples:**
  - 中药(藥)有几(幾)千年的历(歷)史。
    - Zhōng yào yǒu jǐ qiān nián de lìshǐ.
    - Traditional Chinese medicine has a history of thousands of years.
  - 她在学(學)习(習)中药(藥)，希望帮(幫)助更多的人。
    - Tā zài xuéxí zhōng yào, xīwàng bāngzhù gèng duō de rén.
    - She is studying traditional Chinese medicine, hoping to help more people.
  - 医(醫)生给(給)我开(開)了几(幾)副中药(藥)，来(來)治我的感冒。
    - Yīshēng gěi wǒ kāi le jǐ fù zhōng yào, lái zhì wǒ de gǎnmào.
    - The doctor prescribed me some traditional Chinese medicine to treat my cold.
### 中药(藥) → 中
- **definition:** middle; central
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)
### 中药(藥) → 药(藥)
- **traditional:** 藥
- **definition:** medicine; cure; drug
- **pinyin:** yào
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 樂
    - lè
    - music
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (grass) + phonetic 樂 (sound) ->
    - medicine
  - **interpretation:** The character 藥 (yào, "medicine") combines the semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass") indicating herbs, traditionally used for medicinal purposes, with the phonetic 樂 (lè, "music") contributing the sound. This suggests the harmonious preparation of herbal remedies.
  - **simplification:** 藥 simplified to 药 with the 艹 (艹) component retained and simplification of the phonetic 樂 (樂) to simplify writing.
- **examples:**
  - 医(醫)生给(給)我开(開)了药(藥)。
    - Yīshēng gěi wǒ kāile yào.
    - The doctor prescribed medicine for me.
  - 如果你不舒服，记(記)得吃药(藥)。
    - Rúguǒ nǐ bù shūfú, jìdé chī yào.
    - If you're not feeling well, remember to take medicine.
  - 这(這)药(藥)很苦，但很有效。
    - Zhè yào hěn kǔ, dàn hěn yǒuxiào.
    - This medicine is bitter but very effective.
### 中药(藥) → 药(藥) → 艹
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他写(寫)字时(時)用艹作草字的偏旁。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春天到来(來)时(時)，艹生长(長)得很快。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.
### 中药(藥) → 药(藥) → 樂
- **definition:** music
- **pinyin:** lè
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - string
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 白
    - bái
    - white
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 糸 (mì, "string") + 木 (mù, "wood") =
    - strings on a piece of wood ->
    - wooden musical instrument
  - **interpretation:** The character 樂 (lè, "music") originally represents strings attached to a wooden frame, depicting a musical instrument. The addition of 白 (bái) in bronze inscriptions likely represents either the thumb in playing motion or serves as a phonetic component. Over time, it became associated with music and by extension, happiness.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜歡聽樂。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān tīng lè.
    - I like listening to music.
  - 他在音樂會上欣賞樂，感受文化魅力。
    - Tā zài yīnyuèhuì shàng xīnshǎng lè, gǎnshòu wénhuà mèilì.
    - He appreciates music at the concert and experiences the charm of culture.
  - 書房中傳來樂，令人心情愉悅。
    - Shūfáng zhōng chuán lái lè, lìngrén xīnqíng yúyuè.
    - Music comes from the study, making people feel delighted.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 樂](@media/glyph6a02.png)
### 中药(藥) → 药(藥) → 樂 → 糸
- **definition:** string
- **pinyin:** mì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她手工制(製)作了一条(條)漂亮的丝(絲)巾。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)图(圖)必须(須)用细(細)糸画(畫)出来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我们(們)参(參)观(觀)了古代的织(織)布技术(術)，对(對)丝(絲)绸(綢)制(製)作产(產)生了兴(興)趣。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 糸](@media/glyph7cf8.png)
### 中药(藥) → 药(藥) → 樂 → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 中药(藥) → 药(藥) → 樂 → 白
- **definition:** white
- **pinyin:** bái
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an acorn ->
    - white from the color of acorn's inside
  - **interpretation:** The character 白(bái, "white") is thought to depict an acorn, as suggested by its use in words related to oak and acorns. The character's meaning of "white" is likely derived from the white color of an acorn's interior.
- **examples:**
  - 白色是我最喜欢(歡)的颜(顏)色。
    - Báisè shì wǒ zuì xǐhuān de yánsè.
    - White is my favorite color.
  - 他的头(頭)发(髮)已经(經)全白了。
    - Tā de tóufà yǐjīng quán bái le.
    - His hair has turned completely white.
  - 在阳(陽)光下，白沙滩(灘)显(顯)得格外美丽(麗)。
    - Zài yángguāng xià, bái shātān xiǎnde géwài měilì.
    - In the sunlight, the white sandy beach looks especially beautiful.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 白](@media/glyph767d.png)

## 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋)
---
## Cungen Gai Old Style Hot Pot
### cún gēn gài · bù gǎi lǎo huǒ guō
---
- **traditional:** 存根蓋不改老火鍋
- **definition:** Cungen Gai Old Style Hot Pot
- **pinyin:** cún gēn gài · bù gǎi lǎo huǒ guō
- **components:**
  - 存根
    - cún gēn
    - store root; receipt stub
  - 蓋
    - gài
    - cover; lid
  - 不改
    - bù gǎi
    - not change
  - 老火鍋
    - lǎo huǒ guō
    - old-style hot pot
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** The phrase is a specific name and should be understood as such without a breakdown that provides further meaning. However, each part involves morphemes with distinct roles. 存 (cún, 'exist; store') suggests preservation, 根 (gēn, 'root; origin') hints at foundational aspects; together 存根 stores foundational essence. 蓋 (gài, 'cover; lid') literally refers to a cover. 不改 (bù gǎi, 'not change') implies consistency. 老 (lǎo, 'old; experienced') suggests traditional or authentic. 火鍋(锅) (huǒ guō, 'hot pot') indicates a type of meal involving cooking at the table.
  - **interpretation:** The phrase 存根蓋不改老火鍋 can be understood as a name indicating a hot pot house that prides itself on retaining traditional or original recipes. 存根(gēn) emphasizes maintaining foundational aspects of the food. 不改 (bù gǎi) suggests an unwavering adherence to tradition, while 老火鍋 (lǎo huǒ guō) specifies the type of cuisine, known for its warming, communal dining nature.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)家餐厅(廳)叫存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng jiào cún gēn gài bù gǎi lǎo huǒ guō.
    - This restaurant is called Cungen Gai Old Style Hot Pot.
  - 我们(們)晚上去存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋)，人很多。
    - Wǒmen wǎnshàng qù cún gēn gài bù gǎi lǎo huǒ guō, rén hěn duō.
    - We went to Cungen Gai Old Style Hot Pot in the evening, and there were many people.
  - 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋)的牛肉非常好吃。
    - Cún gēn gài bù gǎi lǎo huǒ guō de niúròu fēicháng hàochī.
    - The beef at Cungen Gai Old Style Hot Pot is extremely delicious.
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 存根
- **definition:** store root; receipt stub
- **pinyin:** cún gēn
- **components:**
  - 存
    - cún
    - preserve; keep; save
  - 根
    - gēn
    - root; base; origin
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 存 (cún, "preserve") + 根 (gēn, "root")
  - **interpretation:** 存根 (cún gēn, "preserved root") traditionally refers to a part that remains as a record or proof, such as the stub of a receipt. The concept aligns with something being kept ('preserved') as a foundation ('root').
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)妥善保管这(這)张(張)存根。
    - Qǐng tuǒshàn bǎoguǎn zhè zhāng cún gēn.
    - Please keep this receipt stub carefully.
  - 银(銀)行开(開)具了存根，作为(為)交易凭(憑)证(證)。
    - Yínháng kāijù le cún gēn, zuòwéi jiāoyì píngzhèng.
    - The bank issued a receipt stub as proof of the transaction.
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 存根 → 存
- **definition:** preserve; keep; save
- **pinyin:** cún
- **components:**
  - 才
    - cái
    - talent
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 才 (cái, "talent") + Semantic: 子 (zǐ, "child") =
    - combination symbolizing preservation or continuation ->
    - preserve
  - **interpretation:** In 存 (cún, "preserve"), 才 (cái, "talent") functions as the phonetic element, while 子 (zǐ, "child") provides a semantic suggestion of nurturing or preserving, which aligns with the idea of keeping or saving.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)把珍贵(貴)的信件存入保险(險)柜(櫃)。
    - Qǐng bǎ zhēnguì de xìn jiàn cún rù bǎoxiǎn guì.
    - Please store the precious letters in the safe.
  - 他把时(時)间(間)存起来(來)，为(為)了未来(來)计(計)划(劃)。
    - Tā bǎ shíjiān cún qǐlái, wèi le wèilái jìhuà.
    - He saved up time for his future plans.
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 存根 → 存 → 才
- **definition:** talent
- **pinyin:** cái
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a sharp peg ->
    - originally referred to pegs used in board games ->
    - conceptually extended to 'talent' as skill pegs straight into a task
  - **interpretation:** The character 才 (cái) initially depicted a sharp peg, which was associated with playing board games that required skill. This sense of skill was then extended metaphorically to mean 'talent'. The leap to 'only then' likely comes from the notion that one's capabilities are unlocked or recognized through achievement, akin to placing the right peg in the right spot.
- **examples:**
  - 他的音乐(樂)才华(華)令人惊(驚)叹(嘆)。
    - Tā de yīnyuè cáihuá lìngrén jīngtàn.
    - His musical talent is astonishing.
  - 我刚(剛)刚(剛)才知道这(這)个(個)消息。
    - Wǒ gānggāng cái zhīdào zhège xiāoxi.
    - I just now found out about this news.
  - 只有努力工作才能取得成功。
    - Zhǐyǒu nǔlì gōngzuò cái néng qǔdé chénggōng.
    - Only by working hard can one achieve success.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 才](@media/glyph624d.png)
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 存根 → 存 → 子
- **definition:** child
- **pinyin:** zǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a baby with a large head and spread arms, with legs wrapped in a blanket
  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)小子很调(調)皮。
    - Zhè xiǎo zǐ hěn tiáopí.
    - This kid is very naughty.
  - 他的小子爱(愛)打篮(籃)球，每天都锻(鍛)炼(煉)身体(體)。
    - Tā de xiǎo zǐ ài dǎ lánqiú, měitiān dōu duànliàn shēntǐ.
    - His child loves playing basketball, and practices every day.
  - 孤独(獨)的子需要关(關)爱(愛)。
    - Gūdú de zǐ xūyào guān'ài.
    - A lonely child needs care.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 子](@media/glyph5b50.png)
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 存根 → 根
- **definition:** root; base; origin
- **pinyin:** gēn
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 艮
    - gēn
    - obstinate
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 木 (mù, 'wood') + phonetic: 艮 (gēn, 'obstinate') =
    - root of a tree or plant ->
    - 'root; base; origin'
  - **interpretation:** The 木 (mù, 'wood') component indicates the connection to trees or plants, while the 艮 (gēn, 'obstinate') provides the sound element and suggests a firm and stable foundation, similar to how roots anchor a plant.
- **examples:**
  - 每棵树(樹)都有根。
    - Měi kē shù dōu yǒu gēn.
    - Every tree has roots.
  - 历(歷)史是文化的根，传(傳)统(統)给(給)予我们(們)智慧。
    - Lìshǐ shì wénhuà de gēn, chuántǒng jǐyǔ wǒmen zhìhuì.
    - History is the root of culture, and tradition gives us wisdom.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 根](@media/glyph6839.png)

- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 存根 → 根 → 艮
- **definition:** obstinate
- **pinyin:** gēn
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 目 (mù, 'eye') + 人 (rén, 'person') =
    - a person looking back ->
    - concept of disobedience or limit
  - **interpretation:** The character 艮(gěn) depicts a person turning around to look back, symbolizing hesitation or obstruction. The association with stopping or limiting arises from the act of looking back as a check on forward movement.
- **examples:**
  - 火车(車)在车(車)站艮停。
    - huǒchē zài chēzhàn gěn tíng.
    - The train is stopping at the station.
  - 他前行至半途便艮住。
    - tā qiánxíng zhì bàntú biàn gěn zhù.
    - He stopped halfway through his journey.
  - 研究易经(經)时(時)，学(學)者发(發)现(現)艮象寓意着(著)停止。
    - yánjiū yìjīng shí, xuézhě fāxiàn gěn xiàng yùyì zhe tíngzhǐ.
    - While studying the I Ching, scholars discovered that the image of Gèn implies stopping.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 艮](@media/glyph826e.png)
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 存根 → 根 → 艮 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 存根 → 根 → 艮 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 蓋
- **definition:** cover; lid
- **pinyin:** gài
- **components:**
  - 艸
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 盍
    - hé
    - why not
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 艸 (cǎo, "grass") as semantic + 盍 (hé, "why not") as phonetic =
    - thatch representing cover ->
    - expanded to "cover; lid; top"
  - **interpretation:** The character 蓋(gài) originally depicted a thatch made from grass, used for covering structures. The phonetic component 盍 (hé, "why not") was initially the original character for 'cover,' which later extended the semantic scope of 蓋(gài) as it was borrowed to also ask "why not."
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 蓋 is simplified to 盖 by adopting a more streamlined form in mainland China.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)把锅(鍋)的盖(蓋)盖(蓋)好。
    - Qǐng bǎ guō de gài gài hǎo.
    - Please properly cover the pot.
  - 我找不到水瓶的盖(蓋)，因为(為)它太小了。
    - Wǒ zhǎo bù dào shuǐpíng de gài, yīnwèi tā tài xiǎo le.
    - I can't find the lid of the water bottle because it is too small.
  - 桌子上的盖(蓋)盖(蓋)住了杂(雜)乱(亂)的书(書)本。
    - Zhuōzi shàng de gài gài zhù le záluàn de shūběn.
    - The lid on the table covers the messy stack of books.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 蓋](@media/glyph84cb.png)
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 蓋 → 艸
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - grass
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts grass blades ->
    - duplication of 屮 (chè, 'grass') ->
    - grass imagery
  - **interpretation:** The character 艸(cǎo, 'grass') is a pictorial representation of grass blades. It is essentially a duplication of the character 屮 (chè, 'grass'), visually suggesting the appearance of grass tufts through repetition, emphasizing the concept of grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 公园(園)里(裡)绿(綠)艸茵茵。
    - Gōngyuán lǐ lǜ cǎo yīn yīn.
    - The park is filled with lush grass.
  - 晨露滋润(潤)艸丛(叢)，微风(風)使它们(們)起舞。
    - Chénlù zīrùn cǎo cóng, wēifēng shǐ tāmen qǐwǔ.
    - The morning dew nourishes the cluster of grass, and the breeze makes them dance.
  - 秋天时(時)艸变(變)黄(黃)，冬天它又枯萎。
    - Qiūtiān shí cǎo biàn huáng, dōngtiān tā yòu kūwěi.
    - In autumn, the grass turns yellow, and in winter, it withers.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 艸](@media/glyph8278.png)
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 蓋 → 艸 → 屮
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润(潤)后(後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 蓋 → 盍
- **definition:** why not
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - A container and its lid ->
    - indicates the concept of 'cover'
  - **interpretation:** 盍 (hé, "why not") depicts a container with a lid, symbolizing the action of covering. Originally, it is the graphic representation of a covered object, which later influenced its role in forming other characters with related meanings such as 蓋 (gài, "cover"). The character's modern usage extends metaphorically to form questions and imperatives that imply a proactive suggestion, similar to asking 'why not do something?'

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改
- **definition:** not change
- **pinyin:** bù gǎi
- **components:**
  - 不
    - bù
    - not; no
  - 改
    - gǎi
    - change; alter
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 不 (bù, "not") negates the action of 改 (gǎi, "change"). Combining them conveys the meaning of maintaining consistency or staying the same.
  - **interpretation:** 不 (bù, "not") negates the component it's paired with. 改 (gǎi, "change") indicates the idea of alteration or modification. Therefore, 不改 conveys the concept of stopping any change from occurring, reinforcing constancy or the decision to keep something as it is.
- **examples:**
  - 无(無)论(論)发(發)生什么(麼)，他的决(決)定不改。
    - Wúlùn fāshēng shénme, tā de juédìng bù gǎi.
    - No matter what happens, his decision does not change.
  - 他对(對)原则(則)不改，始终(終)如一。
    - Tā duì yuánzé bù gǎi, shǐzhōngrúyī.
    - He does not change his principles and remains consistent.
  - 虽(雖)然环(環)境变(變)了，她的态(態)度不改。
    - Suīrán huánjìng biàn le, tā de tàidù bù gǎi.
    - Although the environment has changed, her attitude does not change.
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改 → 不
- **definition:** not; no
- **pinyin:** bù
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 否
    - fǒu
    - no
  - 柎
    - fū
    - calyx
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a calyx of a flower ->
    - used phono-semantically in 否 (fǒu, "no") with 口 (kǒu, "mouth") to express negation ->
    - borrowed back as synonym for 否 to mean "not"
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted a calyx, the character 不 was used phonosemantically in 否 (fǒu, "no") to convey negation by combining with 口 (kǒu, "mouth"). This negation concept spread back to 不, shifting its meaning to "not". The calyx meaning is now expressed by 柎.
- **examples:**
  - 我不是医(醫)生。
    - Wǒ bú shì yīshēng.
    - I am not a doctor.
  - 他不想去公园(園)。
    - Tā bù xiǎng qù gōngyuán.
    - He doesn't want to go to the park.
  - 天气(氣)不太好，所以我们(們)待在家里(裡)。
    - Tiānqì bù tài hǎo, suǒyǐ wǒmen dāi zài jiālǐ.
    - The weather is not very good, so we stayed at home.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 不](@media/glyph4e0d.png)
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改 → 不 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改 → 不 → 否
- **definition:** no
- **pinyin:** fǒu
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 不
    - bù
    - not
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 不 (bù, "not") ->
    - represent denial or negation
  - **interpretation:** The character 否(pǐ, "no") combines the semantic element 口 (kǒu, "mouth") with the phonetic element 不 (bù, "not"). The mouth is associated with speech, and when combined with 'not', it conveys the idea of refusal or denial, which aligns with the meaning 'no'.
- **examples:**
  - 你去不去学(學)校？
    - Nǐ qù bù qù xuéxiào?
    - Are you going to school or not?
  - 这(這)个(個)答案是对(對)的还(還)是错(錯)的？
    - Zhège dá'àn shì duì de háishì cuò de?
    - Is this answer right or wrong?
  - 他是否知道这(這)个(個)消息？
    - Tā shìfǒu zhīdào zhège xiāoxi?
    - Does he know this news or not?

  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 付
    - fù
    - to pay
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "wood") + phonetic 付 (fù) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** 柎(fū, "calyx") combines 木 (mù, "wood"), which highlights the botanical context related to plants and flowers, with 付 (fù), which provides the phonetic component. The structure suggests a part of a plant, specifically the calyx, which is wooden or firm like 木 (mù, "wood").

  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.

    - yòu

  - 寸
    - cùn
    - hand

  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**

    - person giving with hand ->
    - to deliver, hand over
  - **interpretation:** The character 付 (fù, "hand over") combines 亻(人) (rén, "person") with a hand component. It visually represents the action of a person handing something over to another, emphasizing the act of giving or delivering.
- **examples:**

- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Stylization of 人 (rén, "person") as a side radical to depict a person
  - **interpretation:** 亻 is a stylized form of 人 (rén, "person") used to indicate human-related meanings when combined with other components in characters as a radical. It visually represents a standing person, maintaining the core meaning of 'person' while facilitating the construction of complex characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一个(個)热(熱)心的人。

    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu mèngxiǎng.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改 → 不 → 柎 → 付 → 又

  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.

    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改 → 不 → 柎 → 付 → 寸
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布每一寸都是精心制(製)作。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用卷尺量一寸，每一寸数(數)据(據)都准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.

  - **interpretation:** The character combines 攴 (pū, 'rap'), which resembles a hand holding a stick, with 己 (jǐ), which serves as the phonetic component. The semantic part, depicting a form of correction or enforcement, aligns with the concept of change as a correction or amendment, while 己 contributes the sound.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改 → 改 → 攴
- **definition:** rap
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩鼓面，传(傳)递(遞)出节(節)奏的信号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了一下门(門)，唤(喚)起了室内(內)的安静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改 → 改 → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 不改 → 改 → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.

    - silk; thread

    - jǐ
    - self

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 老火鍋
- **definition:** old-style hot pot
- **pinyin:** lǎo huǒ guō
- **components:**
  - 老
    - lǎo
    - old; venerable; experienced
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire; hot; fierce; urgent
  - 鍋
    - guō
    - pot; pan; cauldron; wok
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** The word 老火鍋(lǎo huǒ guō, "old-style hot pot") combines the concepts of 老 (lǎo, "old"), 火 (huǒ, "fire; hot"), and 鍋 (guō, "pot"). Together, it refers to a type of hot pot that is traditional or follows an old method of preparation.
  - **interpretation:** 老 (lǎo, "old") suggests something ancient or traditional, indicating a method or style passed down through generations. 火 (huǒ, "fire; hot") emphasizes cooking with direct heat, apt for the communal boiling method of a hot pot. 鍋 (guō, "pot") explicitly refers to the cooking vessel used. Combined, it conveys the image of a time-honored dining experience using hot pots, popular for gatherings across time.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)今晚去吃老火锅(鍋)。
    - Wǒmen jīnwǎn qù chī lǎo huǒ guō.
    - We are going to eat old-style hot pot tonight.
  - 在冬天，吃一顿(頓)热(熱)腾(騰)腾(騰)的老火锅(鍋)感觉(覺)很棒。
    - Zài dōngtiān, chī yī dùn rè téng téng de lǎo huǒ guō gǎnjué hěn bàng.
    - In winter, eating a steaming old-style hot pot feels great.
  - 许(許)多人喜欢(歡)老火锅(鍋)的独(獨)特味道。
    - Xǔduō rén xǐhuān lǎo huǒ guō de dútè wèidào.
    - Many people enjoy the unique taste of old-style hot pot.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 老火鍋 → 鍋 → 金

- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 士
    - shì

  - 呂
    - lǚ
    - two blocks of metal
  - 亼
    - jí
    - open mouth upside down

    - original pronunciation; no earth pictogram in ancient forms ->

  - **interpretation:** Initially representing copper, due to its use in the Copper Age, the character 金 (jīn, "metal") evolved to refer broadly to metal as technological progress made various metals crucial in society. The extension to gold reflects its value and prominence. The phonetic 亼 indicates the character's pronunciation, with semantic elements showing early associations with precious materials.

- **definition:** upside-down ritual axe
- **pinyin:** shì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a ritual axe, possibly made of jade ->
    - symbolized soldier ->
    - intellectual or officer over time
  - **interpretation:** The character 士(shì, 'scholar') originally depicted a ritual axe used in ceremonies, implying a person of a certain rank or status who could wield such symbols. This connection to ceremonial authority evolved to mean 'soldier' and later 'intellectual' or 'officer', roles associated with leadership and knowledge in societal hierarchies.
- **examples:**

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 老火鍋 → 鍋 → 金 → 呂
- **definition:** two blocks of metal
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two disconnected blocks of metal, later connected in seal script ->
    - Original form of 鋁 (lǚ, 'ingot') ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'spine' and 'music notes'
  - **interpretation:** The character 呂(lǚ) ('two blocks of metal') visually represents two separate blocks aligned vertically. In its earliest forms, these blocks were disconnected, symbolizing distinct metal segments, which aligns with its early use for 'ingot'. Over time, as seen in seal script, a connecting line was added to form the modern appearance. This visual interpretation supports its original meaning related to metal. It was later phonetically borrowed to convey concepts like 'spine' and 'music notes', where no direct semantic link exists with metal, but the sound similarity allowed its reuse in these contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 他用两(兩)个(個)大的金属(屬)块(塊)铸(鑄)造了一个(個)雕像。
    - Tā yòng liǎng gè dà de jīnshǔ kuài zhùzào le yī gè diāoxiàng.
    - He cast a statue using two large blocks of metal.

    - Xiàndài gōngyè zhōng, jīnshǔ kuài cháng yòng yú zhìzào zhòngxíng shèbèi.
    - In modern industry, metal blocks are often used for manufacturing heavy equipment.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)师(師)用金属(屬)块(塊)建造了一个(個)现(現)代化建筑(築)。
    - Zhège shèjì shī yòng jīnshǔ kuài jiànzào le yī gè xiàndàihuà jiànzhù.
    - The designer built a modern structure using metal blocks.

  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 老火鍋 → 鍋 → 金 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今天的天气(氣)不错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在是吃晚饭(飯)的时(時)候。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她今天特别(別)忙，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 老火鍋 → 鍋 → 咼
- **definition:** crooked, bent
- **pinyin:** guō
- **components:**
  - 冎
    - guā
    - a type of ancient vessel
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 冎 (guā, "a type of ancient vessel") + semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") ->
    - crooked; bent
  - **interpretation:** The character 咼 (guō, "crooked, bent") combines the phonetic component 冎 (guā, "a type of ancient vessel"), which suggests the sound, with the semantic component 口 (kǒu, "mouth"), indicating aspects related to opening or shape. Together, these components infer an image of something that does not maintain a straight line, thus producing the meaning "crooked, bent."
- **historical forms:**

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 老火鍋 → 鍋 → 咼 → 冎

- **pinyin:** guā
- **components:**
  - 骨
    - gǔ

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts bones ->
    - original form of 骨 (gǔ, "bone")
  - **interpretation:** The character 冎 is a pictogram representing bones and serves as the original form of 骨 (gǔ, "bone"). Its depiction captures the outline of bones, highlighting its usage in ancient scripts. It also appears in other characters as a component, maintaining its essence related to structure and form.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)汉(漢)字由偏旁和冎构(構)成，其中冎提供了语(語)音线(線)索。

    - This character is composed of radicals and guǒ, wherein guǒ provides a phonetic clue.
  - 在古代造字过(過)程中，冎常作为(為)声(聲)旁使用。
    - Zài gǔdài zàozì guòchéng zhōng, guǒ cháng zuòwéi shēngpáng shǐyòng.
    - In the process of character creation in ancient times, guǒ was often used as a phonetic component.
  - 冎是一种(種)发(發)音提示符。
    - Guǒ shì yī zhǒng fāyīn tíshì fú.
    - Guǒ is a phonetic indicator.

### 存根盖(蓋)不改老火锅(鍋) → 老火鍋 → 鍋 → 咼 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**

    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

## 孙(孫)子兵法
---
## The Art of War by Sun Tzu
### Sūnzǐ Bīngfǎ
---
- **traditional:** 孫子兵法
- **definition:** The Art of War by Sun Tzu
- **pinyin:** Sūnzǐ Bīngfǎ
- **components:**
  - 孫子
    - Sūnzǐ
    - Master Sun
  - 兵法
    - bīngfǎ
    - military methods
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** The term 孫子兵法 (Sūnzǐ Bīngfǎ) refers to 'The Art of War,' an ancient Chinese military treatise. It was traditionally attributed to the military strategist 孫 (Sūn, "surname Sun") 子 (zǐ, "master; son") whose name collectively forms 孫子 (Sūnzǐ, "Master Sun"). The surname 孫 (Sūn, "surname Sun") connects him to his lineage, while 子 (zǐ, "master") conveys reverence and mastery. 兵 (bīng, "soldier; military") emphasizes the military focus of his teachings. 法 (fǎ, "method; law") indicates a comprehensive systematic methodology, reflecting the structured and strategic nature of the text.
  - **interpretation:** The name 孫子 (Sūnzǐ, "Master Sun") acknowledges Sun Tzu's status as a venerated figure in military strategy. 兵法 (bīngfǎ, "military methods") signifies the strategic doctrines and tactics explained in the text, making it an authoritative guide on warfare. 'Master Sun's Military Methods' highlights the treatise's focus on strategic principles employed by military leaders.
- **examples:**
  - 孙(孫)子兵法是一部著名的兵书(書)。
    - Sūnzǐ Bīngfǎ shì yī bù zhùmíng de bīngshū.
    - The Art of War is a famous military treatise.
  - 许(許)多商界领(領)袖都从(從)孙(孫)子兵法中获(獲)得灵(靈)感。
    - Xǔduō shāngjiè lǐngxiù dōu cóng Sūnzǐ Bīngfǎ zhōng huòdé línggǎn.
    - Many business leaders draw inspiration from The Art of War.
  - 读(讀)孙(孫)子兵法能提高我们(們)的战(戰)略思维(維)。
    - Dú Sūnzǐ Bīngfǎ néng tígāo wǒmen de zhànlüè sīwéi.
    - Reading The Art of War can enhance our strategic thinking.
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 孫子
- **definition:** Master Sun
- **pinyin:** Sūnzǐ
- **components:**
  - 孫
    - sūn
    - grandson
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - master; child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 孫 (sūn, "grandson") + 子 (zǐ, "master; child"): The term can refer to Sun Tzu (Sūnzǐ, "Master Sun"), the author of The Art of War, an ancient Chinese military treatise.
  - **interpretation:** Sun Tzu, historically known as Sūnzǐ (孫子), amalgamates the meaning of 'descendant' or 'grandson' (孫) implying lineage and heritage, with 'master' (子), denoting his revered status and intellectual stature in military strategy. The combination suggests not only lineage but also implies respect, similar to calling someone 'Master Smith' in English. In full, it marks Sun Tzu as an esteemed figure in Chinese culture.
- **examples:**
  - 孫子兵法是一本关(關)于(於)战(戰)争(爭)策略的书(書)。
    - Sūnzǐ Bīngfǎ shì yī běn guānyú zhànzhēng cèlüè de shū.
    - The Art of War by Master Sun is a book about military strategy.
  - 很多人认(認)为(為)孫子的智慧，仍然适(適)用于(於)现(現)代社会(會)。
    - Hěn duō rén rènwéi Sūnzǐ de zhìhuì, réngrán shìyòng yú xiàndài shèhuì.
    - Many people believe that the wisdom of Master Sun is still applicable in modern society.
  - 孫子是一位古代的军(軍)事战(戰)略家。
    - Sūnzǐ shì yī wèi gǔdài de jūnshì zhànlüèjiā.
    - Master Sun was an ancient military strategist.
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 孫子 → 孫
- **definition:** grandson
- **pinyin:** sūn
- **components:**
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - son
  - 系
    - xì
    - continue
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 子 (zǐ, "son") + 系 (xì, "continue") =
    - offspring that continues the family line ->
    - grandson
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 子 (zǐ, "son") and 系 (xì, "continue") to represent the idea of a descendant who continues the family line, specifically a grandson.
  - **simplification:** Simplified to 孙 by changing 系 to 小 to reduce complexity.
- **examples:**
  - 他的孙(孫)子每天放学(學)后(後)都会(會)来(來)找他。
    - Tā de sūnzi měitiān fàngxué hòu dōu huì lái zhǎo tā.
    - His grandson comes to find him every day after school.
  - 孙(孫)悟空是《西游记(記)》中的一个(個)角色。
    - Sūn Wùkōng shì 《Xīyóujì》 zhōng de yī gè juésè.
    - Sun Wukong is a character in 'Journey to the West'.
  - 他已经(經)有三个(個)孙(孫)子了。
    - Tā yǐjīng yǒu sān gè sūnzi le.
    - He already has three grandsons.
- **historical forms:**

### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 孫子 → 孫 → 子
- **definition:** son
- **pinyin:** zǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a baby with a large head and spread arms, with legs wrapped in a blanket
  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)小子很调(調)皮。
    - Zhè xiǎo zǐ hěn tiáopí.
    - This kid is very naughty.
  - 他的小子爱(愛)打篮(籃)球，每天都锻(鍛)炼(煉)身体(體)。
    - Tā de xiǎo zǐ ài dǎ lánqiú, měitiān dōu duànliàn shēntǐ.
    - His child loves playing basketball, and practices every day.
  - 孤独(獨)的子需要关(關)爱(愛)。
    - Gūdú de zǐ xūyào guān'ài.
    - A lonely child needs care.

### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 孫子 → 孫 → 系
- **definition:** continue
- **pinyin:** xì
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - abbreviated 手 (shǒu, "hand") + 糸 (mì, "silk") =
    - hand manipulating thread ->
    - simplified ->
    - used as simplified form of 繫 (xì, "connect")
  - **interpretation:** The character 系 (xì, "continue") combines 手 (shǒu, "hand") and 糸 (mì, "silk"), depicting a hand weaving or tying thread, symbolizing continuity or connection. It simplifies the more complex 繫 (xì, "connect") by merging the elements concisely.
  - **simplification:** Simplified by merging components into a unified character, omitting 人 (rén, "person") and retaining essential elements from related forms like 繫 (xì, "connect") and 係 (xì, "relate").
- **examples:**
  - 课(課)程系进(進)行到下学(學)期。
    - Kèchéng xì jìnxíng dào xià xuéqī.
    - The course continues into the next semester.
  - 旅程系向未知方向展开(開)。
    - Lǚchéng xì xiàng wèizhī fāngxiàng zhǎnkāi.
    - The journey continues unfolding in an unknown direction.
  - 讨(討)论(論)系持续(續)深入。
    - Tǎolùn xì chíxù shēnrù.
    - The discussion continues to delve deeper.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 系](@media/glyph7cfb.png)
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 孫子 → 孫 → 系 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

  - **type:** pictogram

- **examples:**
  - 她手工制(製)作了一条(條)漂亮的丝(絲)巾。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.

    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.

    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.

### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法
- **definition:** military methods
- **pinyin:** bīngfǎ
- **components:**
  - 兵
    - bīng
    - soldier; weapon
  - 法
    - fǎ
    - method; rule; law
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 兵 (bīng, "soldier; weapon") refers to soldiers or warfare, encompassing everything related to military matters. 法 (fǎ, "method; rule; law") denotes a method or doctrine, indicating a set of structured practices or principles.
  - **interpretation:** 兵 (bīng, "soldier; weapon") implies the entire scope of military operations, while 法 (fǎ, "method; rule; law") suggests a formalized system or set of techniques. Together, they signify the structured methods and principles essential to conducting warfare, encapsulating the strategic and tactical doctrines that guide military operations.
- **examples:**
  - 孙(孫)子兵法是一本著名的古代军(軍)事著作。
    - Sūnzǐ Bīngfǎ shì yī běn zhùmíng de gǔdài jūnshì zhùzuò.
    - The Art of War by Sun Tzu is a famous ancient military work.
  - 他精通兵法，可以在战(戰)场(場)上灵(靈)活应(應)对(對)。
    - Tā jīngtōng bīngfǎ, kěyǐ zài zhànchǎng shàng línghuó yìngduì.
    - He is well-versed in military methods and can adapt flexibly on the battlefield.
  - 了解各种(種)兵法，有助于(於)提高战(戰)略思维(維)。
    - Liǎojiě gèzhǒng bīngfǎ, yǒuzhù yú tígāo zhànlüè sīwéi.
    - Understanding various military methods helps in enhancing strategic thinking.
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法 → 兵
- **definition:** soldier; weapon
- **pinyin:** bīng
- **components:**
  - 斤
    - jīn
    - a short axe
  - 廾
    - gǒng
    - two hands
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 斤 (axe) + 廾 (two hands) =
    - hands holding a weapon ->
    - soldier; military
  - **interpretation:** The character 兵 (bīng, "soldier; military") is composed of 斤 (jīn, "a short axe"), representing a weapon, and 廾 (gǒng, "two hands"), depicting a pair of hands gripping the weapon. This combination intuitively symbolizes a person equipped with a weapon, directly leading to the meanings of "soldier" and "military."
- **examples:**
  - 他的梦(夢)想是当(當)一名优(優)秀的兵。
    - Tā de mèngxiǎng shì dāng yī míng yōuxiù de bīng.
    - His dream is to become an excellent soldier.
  - 兵营(營)里(裡)的生活很有纪(紀)律。
    - Bīngyíng lǐ de shēnghuó hěn yǒu jìlǜ.
    - Life in the barracks is very disciplined.
  - 军(軍)队(隊)集结(結)完毕(畢)，准(準)备(備)出发(發)。
    - Jūnduì jíjié wánbì, zhǔnbèi chūfā.
    - The troops have assembled and are ready to depart.

### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法 → 兵 → 廾 → 𠂇 → 又
- **definition:** again
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法 → 法
- **definition:** method; rule; law
- **pinyin:** fǎ
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 去
    - qù
    - go
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵 (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic 去 (qù, "go") ->
    - method
  - **interpretation:** The character 法(fǎ, "method; law") combines the semantic component 氵 (shuǐ, "water") suggesting flow or enactment with the phonetic component 去 (qù, "go"), which provides the sound. The concept of water implies a guiding principle or natural flow, which together with the action of 'going', forms the idea of following a prescribed path or method, hence 'law' or 'method'.
  - **simplification:** Originally simplified from 灋, resulting in 法 by retaining key phonetic and semantic elements and omitting structurally non-essential components.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)方法很有效。
    - Zhège fāngfǎ hěn yǒuxiào.
    - This method is very effective.
  - 学(學)习(習)法律是一个(個)挑战(戰)。
    - Xuéxí fǎlǜ shì yī gè tiǎozhàn.
    - Studying law is a challenge.
  - 我们(們)需要找到更好的解决(決)办(辦)法。
    - Wǒmen xūyào zhǎodào gèng hǎo de jiějué bànfǎ.
    - We need to find a better solution.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 法](@media/glyph6cd5.png)
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法 → 法 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字中偏旁氵，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快戏(戲)水。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法 → 法 → 去
- **definition:** go
- **pinyin:** qù
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth, object
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 大 (dà, "big") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth, object") =
    - originally depicted a man departing from a cave or city ->
    - meaning "go"
  - **interpretation:** The original form illustrated a man leaving a place, possibly a city or a cave, suggesting the concept of going away or departing. This imagery naturally leads to the modern meaning of "go."
- **examples:**
  - 我要去学(學)校。
    - Wǒ yào qù xuéxiào.
    - I want to go to school.
  - 她去商店，买(買)了一些水果。
    - Tā qù shāngdiàn, mǎile yīxiē shuǐguǒ.
    - She went to the shop and bought some fruits.
  - 明年我打算去法国(國)。
    - Míngnián wǒ dǎsuàn qù Fǎguó.
    - I plan to go to France next year.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 去](@media/glyph53bb.png)
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法 → 法 → 去 → 大
- **definition:** big
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)房子很大。
    - Zhè ge fángzi hěn dà.
    - This house is very big.
  - 大海波涛(濤)汹(洶)涌(湧)，展现(現)出大自然的力量。
    - Dàhǎi bōtāo xiōngyǒng, zhǎnxiàn chū dàzìrán de lìliàng.
    - The vast ocean waves surge, showcasing the power of nature.
  - 大人物登场(場)，留下传(傳)奇。
    - Dà rénwù dēngchǎng, liúxià chuánqí.
    - Great figures make an appearance, leaving behind legends.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 大](@media/glyph5927.png)
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法 → 法 → 去 → 大 → 夫
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a variant form of 大 (dà, "big") representing an adult man with a hairpin ->
    - became associated with 夫 (fū, "man").
  - **interpretation:** 夫 (fū, "man") was visually similar to 大 (dà, "big") and was originally interchangeable. The addition of the horizontal stroke was interpreted as a hairpin, symbolizing adulthood for men.
- **examples:**
  - 此夫心怀(懷)大志。
    - Cǐ fū xīn huái dà zhì.
    - This man has lofty aspirations.
  - 他勤劳(勞)努力，堪称(稱)良夫。
    - Tā qín láo nǔ lì, kān chēng liáng fū.
    - He works diligently and is regarded as an exemplary man.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夫](@media/glyph592b.png)
### 孙(孫)子兵法 → 兵法 → 法 → 去 → 口
- **definition:** mouth, object
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)

## The Art of War by Sun Tzu

## 岭(嶺)南
---
## Lingnan region
### lǐng nán
---
- **traditional:** 嶺南
- **definition:** Lingnan region
- **pinyin:** lǐng nán
- **components:**
  - 岭(嶺)
    - lǐng
    - mountain ridge; peak
  - 南
    - nán
    - south; southern part of country
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 岭(嶺) (lǐng, "mountain ridge") is used to describe a series of connected mountains forming a continuous elevated crest. 南 (nán, "south") indicates the direction towards the south. Together, these characters describe the geographic region south of the mountain range, particularly referring to the area south of the Nanling Mountains in southern China.
  - **interpretation:** 岭(嶺) (lǐng, "mountain ridge") visually depicts a path or crest between heights, signaling a droplet-like shape, which naturally signifies a high, narrow point. 南 (nán, "south") culturally aligns with directions, land divisions, and cardinality essential in Chinese climatology and geography, indicating the region beneath the mountain ridges. Hence, 岭(嶺)南 describes the geographical area lying south of these natural barriers, famously known as the region south of the Nanling mountain ranges, with historical implications of being a culturally distinctive and economically significant space within southern China.
- **examples:**
  - 岭(嶺)南地区(區)以其独(獨)特的文化而闻(聞)名。
    - Lǐngnán dìqū yǐ qí dútè de wénhuà ér wénmíng.
    - The Lingnan area is famous for its unique culture.
  - 许(許)多岭(嶺)南菜肴(餚)在全国(國)各地都很受欢(歡)迎。
    - Xǔduō lǐngnán càiyáo zài quánguó gèdì dōu hěn shòu huānyíng.
    - Many Lingnan dishes are very popular across the country.
  - 他打算去岭(嶺)南旅游(遊)。
    - Tā dǎsuàn qù lǐngnán lǚyóu.
    - He plans to travel to Lingnan.
### 岭(嶺)南 → 岭(嶺)
- **traditional:** 嶺
- **definition:** mountain ridge; peak
- **pinyin:** lǐng
- **components:**
  - 山
    - shān
    - mountain
  - 領
    - lǐng
    - neck; collar
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 山 (shān, "mountain") + phonetic 領 (lǐng, "neck; collar") ->
    - ridge
  - **interpretation:** In the character 嶺 (lǐng, "ridge"), the semantic component 山 (shān, "mountain") suggests the geographical feature, while the phonetic component 領 (lǐng) provides the sound. The character evokes the image of a mountain's ridge or crest, akin to the line of a neck, which it resembles in shape, leading logically to the meaning "ridge" or "mountain range."
  - **simplification:** 嶺 was simplified to 岭 by replacing the semantic component 領 (lǐng, "neck; collar") with 领, retaining phonetic similarity while reducing complexity.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)早晨爬上了高高的山岭(嶺)。
    - Wǒmen zǎochén pá shàng le gāogāo de shānlǐng.
    - We climbed the high mountain ridge in the morning.
  - 这(這)条(條)山岭(嶺)横(橫)跨整个(個)地区(區)。
    - Zhè tiáo shānlǐng héngkuà zhěnggè dìqū.
    - This mountain range spans the entire region.
  - 云(雲)层(層)遮住了山岭(嶺)的顶(頂)峰。
    - Yúncéng zhē zhù le shānlǐng de dǐngfēng.
    - The cloud layer obscured the mountain ridge's peak.
### 岭(嶺)南 → 岭(嶺) → 山
- **definition:** mountain
- **pinyin:** shān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three mountain peaks
  - **interpretation:** The character 山(shān, "mountain") visually represents the concept of a mountain using three vertical lines that suggest peaks. This depiction is consistent with early forms found in Oracle Bone Script, emphasizing the notion of natural elevation associated with mountains.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)去爬山。
    - Wǒmen qù pá shān.
    - We go climb the mountain.
  - 那座大山让(讓)人惊(驚)叹(嘆)。
    - Nà zuò dà shān ràng rén jīngtàn.
    - That mountain astonishes people.
  - 远(遠)处(處)的山隐(隱)约(約)在云(雲)中，令人心旷(曠)神怡。
    - Yuǎnchù de shān yǐnyuē zài yún zhōng, lìng rén xīnkuàng shényí.
    - The distant mountain fades into the clouds, leaving one in a state of peace.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 山](@media/glyph5c71.png)
### 岭(嶺)南 → 岭(嶺) → 領
- **definition:** neck; collar
- **pinyin:** lǐng
- **components:**
  - 頁
    - yè
    - head
  - 令
    - lìng
    - order
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 頁 (yè, "head") + phonetic 令 (lìng) ->
    - related to the neck or collar
  - **interpretation:** The semantic component 頁 (yè, "head") suggests a connection to parts of the body close to the head, while the phonetic component 令 (lìng) provides the sound. This combination relates to the neck or collar, areas near the head.
  - **simplification:** Simplified by replacing 頁 with 页 to reduce strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他的衣服有一个(個)黑色的领(領)子。
    - Tā de yīfú yǒu yīgè hēisè de lǐngzi.
    - His shirt has a black collar.
  - 她戴着(著)一条(條)珍珠项(項)链(鏈)在脖子上，看起来(來)非常优(優)雅。
    - Tā dàizhe yītiáo zhēnzhū xiàngliàn zài bózi shàng, kànqǐlái fēicháng yōuyǎ.
    - She is wearing a pearl necklace on her neck, and it looks very elegant.
  - 这(這)件衬(襯)衫的领(領)特别(別)舒服。
    - Zhè jiàn chènshān de lǐng tèbié shūfú.
    - The collar of this shirt is particularly comfortable.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 領](@media/glyph9818.png)
### 岭(嶺)南 → 岭(嶺) → 領 → 頁
- **definition:** head
- **pinyin:** yè
- **components:**
  - 首
    - shǒu
    - head; first
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 首 (head/face) + 卩 (kneeling person) ->
    - depicts a person's head and body
  - **interpretation:** Originally represented a head and its body in a kneeling posture, emphasizing “head”. The depiction was extended semantically to represent a 'page', as pages bear leading information like a head does for a body. The concept of 'head' is also reflected in its modern usage as a radical in characters related to parts of the head or face.
  - **simplification:** 页 is a cursive shorthand of the traditional 頁, simplifying the structure while maintaining the core shape of a head.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)打开(開)书(書)的第十页(頁)。
    - Qǐng dǎkāi shū de dì shí yè.
    - Please open to page ten of the book.
  - 这(這)本书(書)每一页(頁)都有插图(圖)。
    - Zhè běn shū měi yī yè dōu yǒu chātú.
    - Every page of this book has illustrations.
  - 我昨天晚上读(讀)了三十页(頁)。
    - Wǒ zuótiān wǎnshang dúle sānshí yè.
    - I read thirty pages last night.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 頁](@media/glyph9801.png)
### 岭(嶺)南 → 岭(嶺) → 領 → 頁 → 首
- **definition:** head; first
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of an animal with a long mouth and horns, often shown with or without hair ( 巛) ->
    - perpetuated as 𩠐 (form with hair) ->
    - streamlined to 首
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts the head of an animal, with prominent features like a long mouth and horns, emphasizing the notion of a 'head' both physically and symbolically as the foremost part.
- **examples:**
  - 他是这(這)个(個)团(團)队(隊)的首领(領)。
    - Tā shì zhège tuánduì de shǒulǐng.
    - He is the head of this team.
  - 这(這)首歌是我最喜欢(歡)的歌曲。
    - Zhè shǒu gē shì wǒ zuì xǐhuān de gēqǔ.
    - This song is my favorite track.
  - 他抬起头(頭)，看向远(遠)方的山。
    - Tā tái qǐ tóu, kàn xiàng yuǎnfāng de shān.
    - He raised his head and looked towards the distant mountains.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 首](@media/glyph9996.png)
### 岭(嶺)南 → 岭(嶺) → 領 → 頁 → 卩
- **definition:** kneeling person
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式中，卩象征(徵)着(著)内(內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卩](@media/glyph5369.png)
### 岭(嶺)南 → 岭(嶺) → 領 → 令
- **definition:** order
- **pinyin:** lìng
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 卩
    - jié
    - seal
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 卩 (jié, "seal") =
    - person with seal ->
    - issuing orders or commands
  - **interpretation:** The character 令 (lǐng, "order") combines 人 (rén, "person") and 卩 (jié, "seal") to depict someone with a seal or authority, signifying the power to issue orders or commands.
- **examples:**
  - 将(將)军(軍)令部队(隊)保持警戒，士兵严(嚴)格服从(從)。
    - jiāngjūn lǐng bùduì bǎochí jǐngjiè, shìbīng yángé fúcóng.
    - The general orders the troops to maintain vigilance, and the soldiers strictly obey.
  - 老师(師)令学(學)生认(認)真听(聽)讲(講)。
    - lǎoshī lǐng xuéshēng rènzhēn tīngjiǎng.
    - The teacher orders the students to listen attentively.
  - 国(國)王令大臣速速筹(籌)备(備)，迎接远(遠)方使节(節)。
    - guówáng lǐng dàchén sùsù chóubèi, yíngjiē yuǎnfāng shǐjié.
    - The king orders his ministers to quickly make preparations to welcome the foreign envoy.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 令](@media/glyph4ee4.png)
### 岭(嶺)南 → 岭(嶺) → 領 → 令 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 岭(嶺)南 → 南
- **definition:** south; southern part of country
- **pinyin:** nán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hanging percussion instrument (bell) ->
    - Phonetically borrowed for 'south'
  - **interpretation:** 南 originally depicted a bell, indicating hanging percussion instruments, and was later borrowed for its sound to mean 'south'. This borrowing is based on phonetic resemblance rather than a direct conceptual link with directionality.
- **examples:**
  - 南方的天气(氣)很温(溫)暖。
    - Nánfāng de tiānqì hěn wēnnuǎn.
    - The weather in the south is very warm.
  - 我们(們)计(計)划(劃)去南部旅行。
    - Wǒmen jìhuà qù nánbù lǚxíng.
    - We plan to travel to the south.
  - 他住在城市的南边(邊)。
    - Tā zhù zài chéngshì de nánbiān.
    - He lives on the south side of the city.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 南](@media/glyph5357.png)

## 春风(風)手作
---
## Chun Feng handmade
### chūn fēng shǒu zuò
---
- **traditional:** 春風手作
- **definition:** Chun Feng handmade
- **pinyin:** chūn fēng shǒu zuò
- **components:**
  - 春風
    - chūnfēng
    - spring wind
  - 手作
    - shǒuzuò
    - handmade
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** The word 春风手作 (春風手作) is a compound word combining the elements 春风(風) (chūnfēng, "spring wind") and 手作 (shǒuzuò, "handmade").
  - **interpretation:** 春风(風) (chūnfēng, "spring wind") symbolizes the beginning or renewal as spring represents growth and new life. The gentle and refreshing qualities of 春风(風) (chūnfēng, "spring wind") metaphorically convey a sense of creativity and rejuvenation found in handmade crafts. 手作 (shǒuzuò, "handmade") directly indicates something crafted by hand, emphasizing personal touch and uniqueness. Together, the phrase implies crafting items with the refreshing, renewing energy of spring, suggesting creativity and artistry.
- **examples:**
  - 春风(風)手作的产(產)品很受欢(歡)迎。
    - Chūn fēng shǒu zuò de chǎnpǐn hěn shòu huānyíng.
    - Chun Feng handmade products are very popular.
  - 我喜欢(歡)春风(風)手作的设(設)计(計)。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chūn fēng shǒu zuò de shèjì.
    - I like the design of Chun Feng handmade.
  - 春风(風)手作每件作品都很独(獨)特。
    - Chūn fēng shǒu zuò měi jiàn zuòpǐn dōu hěn dútè.
    - Every piece from Chun Feng handmade is unique.
### 春风(風)手作 → 春風
- **definition:** spring wind
- **pinyin:** chūnfēng
- **components:**
  - 春
    - chūn
    - spring
  - 風
    - fēng
    - wind; breeze
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 春 (chūn, "spring") + 風 (fēng, "wind") =
    - spring breeze
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 春 (chūn, "spring") and 風 (fēng, "wind") creates an evocative image of the gentle, refreshing winds associated with the spring season. In Chinese culture, spring is often symbolic of renewal, growth, and hope, and the spring breeze represents these themes.
- **examples:**
  - 春风(風)拂面。
    - chūn fēng fú miàn.
    - The spring breeze caresses the face.
  - 春风(風)轻(輕)拂万(萬)物，唤(喚)来(來)温(溫)暖阳(陽)光。
    - chūn fēng qīng fú wànwù, huàn lái wēn nuǎn yángguāng.
    - The spring breeze gently brushes all living things, summoning warm sunshine.
### 春风(風)手作 → 春風 → 春
- **definition:** spring
- **pinyin:** chūn
- **components:**
  - ⾠(艸)
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 屯
    - zhūn
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - ⾠(艸) (cǎo, "grass") + 日 (rì, "sun") + 屯 (zhūn, "sprout") =
    - sun shining on grass with sprouts ->
    - spring
  - **interpretation:** The character 春 (chūn, "spring") involves elements representing natural growth and revival: grass, sun, and sprouts together illustrate the vibrant growth occurring in springtime.
- **examples:**
  - 春天来(來)了。
    - Chūntiān láile.
    - Spring has arrived.
  - 春天来(來)了，万(萬)物复(復)苏(蘇)。
    - Chūntiān láile, wànwù fùsū.
    - Spring has arrived, and all things are reviving.
  - 春光明媚，人们(們)心情愉快。
    - Chūnguāng míngmèi, rénmen xīnqíng yúkuài.
    - The spring light is bright, and people feel joyful.
- **historical forms:**

### 春风(風)手作 → 春風 → 春 → ⾠
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a kind of agricultural tool used for tilling fields ->
    - original form of removing weeds ->
    - possibly related to tools or a person holding onto a cliff
  - **interpretation:** The character ⾠ initially represented a tool used for agricultural purposes, possibly related to removing weeds, symbolizing labor and cultivation. Alternatively, it is seen as depicting a person holding onto a cliff, illustrating support and elevation.

### 春风(風)手作 → 春風 → 春 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 春风(風)手作 → 春風 → 春 → 屯
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** zhūn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a plant sprout (屮) with a middle emphasis line ->
    - emphasizes sprout
  - **interpretation:** The character 屯(tún, 'station') originally depicts a plant sprout with an added line to emphasize its growth. This imagery reflects the concept of development or establishment, leading to the sense of 'station' as a place where something is established or set up.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)附近有一个(個)储(儲)备(備)粮(糧)的屯。
    - Zhè fùjìn yǒu yīgè chǔbèi liáng de tún.
    - There is a grain storage station nearby.
  - 他们(們)准(準)备(備)在此地设(設)立一个(個)新的军(軍)事屯。
    - Tāmen zhǔnbèi zài cǐdì shèlì yīgè xīn de jūnshì tún.
    - They plan to establish a new military station at this location.
  - 村民们(們)在屯里(裡)储(儲)存了大量的粮(糧)食。
    - Cūnmín men zài tún lǐ chǔcún le dàliàng de liángshí.
    - The villagers have stored a large amount of grain in the station.

### 春风(風)手作 → 春風 → 風
- **definition:** wind; breeze
- **pinyin:** fēng
- **components:**
  - 鳳
    - fèng
    - fenghuang
  - 凡
    - fán
    - ordinary
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** jiajie
  - **description:**
    - 鳳 (fèng, 'fenghuang') borrowed for sound ->
    - 凡 (fan, 'ordinary') phonetic + depiction of fenghuang tail 'fur' ->
    - 風
  - **interpretation:** Originally a borrowing of 鳳 (fèng, 'fenghuang') for its sound to mean 'wind'. The character's structure was influenced by early forms depicting feathers or fur on a fenghuang's tail, with later simplifications resulting in the final form.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 風 was simplified to 风 by replacing 䖝 with 㐅, streamlining the depiction of wind.
- **examples:**
  - 今天的风(風)很大。
    - Jīntiān de fēng hěn dà.
    - The wind is strong today.
  - 风(風)轻(輕)轻(輕)地吹过(過)树(樹)叶(葉)。
    - Fēng qīngqīng de chuī guò shù yè.
    - The breeze gently blows through the leaves.
  - 他喜欢(歡)在风(風)中散步。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài fēng zhōng sànbù.
    - He likes to take walks in the wind.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 風](@media/glyph98a8.png)
### 春风(風)手作 → 春風 → 風 → 鳳
- **definition:** fenghuang
- **pinyin:** fèng
- **components:**
  - 鳥
    - niǎo
    - bird
  - 凡
    - fán
    - ordinary
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") + phonetic 凡 (fán) ->
    - mythical bird
  - **interpretation:** The character 鳳 combines 鳥 (niǎo, "bird"), indicating its connection to the avian world, with 凡 (fán) as a phonetic component, hinting at its pronunciation. This construction symbolizes the mythical phoenix, often associated with auspicious omens and revered in various cultural myths. Its use draws from the elegant and rare nature attributed to this legendary bird.
  - **simplification:** 凤(鳳): The component 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") was replaced with 又 (yòu, "again"), simplifying the strokes necessary to write the character.
- **examples:**
  - 凤(鳳)凰涅槃重生。
    - Fènghuáng nièpán chóngshēng.
    - The phoenix rises from the ashes to be reborn.
  - 这(這)是传(傳)说(說)中的凤(鳳)凰。
    - Zhè shì chuánshuō zhōng de fènghuáng.
    - This is the legendary phoenix.
  - 凤(鳳)舞九天，象征(徵)着(著)自由和力量。
    - Fèng wǔ jiǔ tiān, xiàngzhēng zhe zìyóu hé lìliàng.
    - The phoenix dances in the sky, symbolizing freedom and strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 鳳](@media/glyph9cf3.png)

- **pinyin:** niǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bird with a prominent beak and tail feathers
  - **interpretation:** The character 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") visually represents a bird, featuring distinct elements such as a beak and tail feathers, capturing its essence through its graphical form.
- **examples:**
  - 花园(園)里(裡)有许(許)多鸟(鳥)，在空中翱翔。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu xǔduō niǎo, zài kōngzhōng áoxiáng.
    - Many birds soar in the garden.
  - 树(樹)林中有一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，在枝头(頭)跳跃(躍)。

    - A bird hops on a branch in the forest.

### 春风(風)手作 → 春風 → 風 → 鳳 → 凡
- **definition:** ordinary
- **pinyin:** fán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a plate or flat dish ->
    - borrowed for abstract meanings ->
    - unrelated to 几(幾) (jī, 'small table')
  - **interpretation:** 凡 (fán, 'ordinary') originally depicted a flat dish or plate. Over time, it expanded to encompass broader abstract meanings and is unrelated to the character 几(幾) which represents a small table.
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)平凡的人。
    - tā shì gè píngfán de rén.
    - He is an ordinary person.
  - 凡人都可能犯错(錯)，从(從)错(錯)误(誤)中成长(長)。
    - fán rén dōu kěnéng fàncuò, cóng cuòwù zhōng chéngzhǎng.
    - Ordinary people may make mistakes, and grow from them.
  - 他凡去旅行，总(總)能发(發)现(現)新的风(風)景。
    - tā fán qù lǚxíng, zǒng néng fāxiàn xīn de fēngjǐng.
