### 春风(風)手作 → 手作
- **definition:** handmade
- **pinyin:** shǒuzuò
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 作
    - zuò
    - make; work; act
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 手 (shǒu, "hand") + 作 (zuò, "make; work") combine to form 手作, meaning "handmade".
  - **interpretation:** 手 (shǒu, "hand") refers to the direct involvement of the hands in creating something, emphasizing the manual aspect of the process. 作 (zuò, "make; work") indicates the act of producing or crafting. Together, 手作 implies creating something by hand, highlighting the traditional or artisanal nature of the work, as opposed to machine-made products.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)手作的礼(禮)物。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān shǒu zuò de lǐwù.
    - I like handmade gifts.
  - 市场(場)上展示了许(許)多精美的手作饰(飾)品。
    - Shìchǎng shàng zhǎnshìle xǔduō jīngměi de shǒu zuò shìpǐn.
    - The market showcased many exquisite handmade accessories.
  - 她在周(週)末开(開)设(設)了一个(個)手作工作坊。
    - Tā zài zhōumò kāishèle yī gè shǒu zuò gōngzuòfāng.
    - She started a handmade workshop on the weekend.
### 春风(風)手作 → 手作 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

  - 亻(人)
    - rén
    - person
  - 乍
    - zhà
    - sudden
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 亻(人) (rén, "person") + phonetic 乍 (zhà) ->
    - make; create; do; work
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 亻(人) (rén, "person") indicating human involvement or action with 乍 (zhà) for its phonetic sound. This results in the meaning of acting or creating, as it involves a person performing an action or task.
- **examples:**
  - 他每天都要工作。
    - Tā měitiān dōu yào gōngzuò.
    - He has to work every day.
  - 我正在创(創)作一首新歌。

### 春风(風)手作 → 手作 → 作 → 亻
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Stylization of 人 (rén, "person") as a side radical to depict a person
  - **interpretation:** 亻 is a stylized form of 人 (rén, "person") used to indicate human-related meanings when combined with other components in characters as a radical. It visually represents a standing person, maintaining the core meaning of 'person' while facilitating the construction of complex characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一个(個)热(熱)心的人。
    - Tā shì yī gè rèxīn de rén.

    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu mèngxiǎng.
    - Everyone has dreams.

  - **interpretation:** This character combines the semantic 木 (mù, "tree"), indicating that it is a type of tree, with the phonetic component 昨 (zuó), which suggests the pronunciation. The core meaning of "oak" likely stems from its reference as a specific type of tree.

## 有位子吗(嗎)
---
## Is there a seat available?
### yǒu wèi zi ma
---
- **traditional:** 有位子嗎
- **definition:** Is there a seat available?
- **pinyin:** yǒu wèi zi ma
- **components:**
  - 有
    - yǒu
    - have; there is
  - 位子
    - wèi zi
    - seat
  - 嗎
    - ma
    - question particle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 有 (yǒu, "have; there is"), 位 (wèi, "position; seat"), 子 (zi, "noun suffix"), 嗎 (ma, "question particle")
  - **interpretation:** 有 (yǒu, "have; there is") suggests possession or existence, implying the presence of something. 位 (wèi, "position; seat") denotes a specific location or available spot, often related to seating or rank. 子 (zi, "noun suffix") creates a noun phrase, finalizing the concept of a 'seat.' 嗎 (ma, "question particle") turns the phrase into a question, asking whether such a seat exists.
- **examples:**
  - 餐厅(廳)里(裡)的人很多，你可以问一下有位子吗(嗎)？
    - Cāntīng lǐ de rén hěn duō, nǐ kěyǐ wèn yīxià yǒu wèi zi ma?
    - There are many people in the restaurant, can you ask if there is a seat available?
  - 请(請)问(問)这(這)里(裡)有位子吗(嗎)？
    - Qǐng wèn zhèlǐ yǒu wèi zi ma?
    - Excuse me, is there a seat available here?
  - 如果你去电影院，你应该先查有位子吗(嗎)？
    - Rúguǒ nǐ qù diànyǐngyuàn, nǐ yīnggāi xiān chá yǒu wèi zi ma?
    - If you go to the cinema, you should check first if there is a seat available.
### 有位子吗(嗎) → 有
- **definition:** have; there is
- **pinyin:** yǒu
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - ⺼(肉)
    - ròu
    - meat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic 又(yòu, 'hand') + Semantic ⺼(肉, 'meat') ->
    - abstracted form ->
    - meaning: possess, exist
  - **interpretation:** The character 有(yǒu, 'have') combines the form of a hand holding something, represented by 又(yòu, 'hand'), with the semantic idea of possession or content rooted in 肉(ròu, 'meat'). This symbolically implies having or being in possession of something. Although the original script does not explicitly show meat, the abstracted form represents the concept of existence or possession.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一本书(書)。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī běn shū.
    - I have a book.
  - 花园(園)里(裡)有许(許)多美丽(麗)的花，小鸟(鳥)也在唱歌。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu xǔduō měilì de huā, xiǎo niǎo yě zài chànggē.
    - There are many beautiful flowers in the garden, and the little bird is also singing.
  - 桌上有一杯水。
    - Zhuō shàng yǒu yī bēi shuǐ.
    - There is a glass of water on the table.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 有](@media/glyph6709.png)
### 有位子吗(嗎) → 有 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 有位子吗(嗎) → 有 → ⺼(肉)
- **traditional:** 肉
- **definition:** meat
- **pinyin:** ròu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts ribs of an animal's torso ->
    - physical representation of a slice of meat
  - **interpretation:** The character 肉 (ròu, 'meat') visually represents the structure of ribs or flesh, making its meaning clear and direct in relation to its shape. Over time, its form was stylized into other component shapes like 月 when combined with phonetic elements.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)吃肉。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī ròu.
    - I like to eat meat.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)做了一道红(紅)烧(燒)肉，味道鲜(鮮)美无(無)比。
    - Māmā zuòle yīdào hóngshāo ròu, wèidào xiānměi wúbǐ.
    - Mom prepared a dish of braised meat, and its flavor is extraordinarily delicious.
  - 聚会(會)时(時)，我点(點)了一份烤肉，大家都赞(讚)不绝(絕)口。
    - Jùhuì shí, wǒ diǎnle yī fèn kǎo ròu, dàjiā dōu zàn bù jué kǒu.
    - During the party, I ordered a portion of grilled meat, and everyone couldn't stop praising it.
### 有位子吗(嗎) → 位子
- **definition:** seat
- **pinyin:** wèi zi
- **components:**
  - 位
    - wèi
    - position; place; stand
  - 子
    - zi
    - child; seed; noun suffix
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 位 (wèi, "position") refers to a place or status, often used to specify a particular location in space. The concept of "position" naturally includes the idea of a seat, as it is a specific location meant for someone to occupy. 子 (zi, "child; noun suffix") originally means "child" but in this context, it serves as a noun suffix that doesn't alter the inherent meaning significantly but emphasizes the substantive aspect of the term.
  - **interpretation:** 位 (wèi, "position") provides the core sense of a specific location designated for an individual, which directly translates to the idea of a 'seat' as a particular space reserved for sitting. 子 (zi, "child; noun suffix") acts as a functional suffix that classifies 位 (wèi, "position") clearly as a noun, reinforcing the substantive meaning without altering the fundamental concept of a specified place for someone. The result is a natural intuition of a defined spot meant for occupation by a person, thus, a 'seat'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)电(電)影的位子很好。
    - Zhè ge diànyǐng de wèi zi hěn hǎo.
    - This seat at the movie is very good.
  - 请(請)问(問)这(這)里(裡)有空位子吗(嗎)？
    - Qǐng wèn zhèlǐ yǒu kōng wèi zi ma?
    - Excuse me, is there an available seat here?
  - 我们(們)需要预(預)订(訂)位子，因为(為)餐厅(廳)很忙。
    - Wǒmen xūyào yùdìng wèi zi, yīnwèi cāntīng hěn máng.
    - We need to book a seat because the restaurant is busy.
### 有位子吗(嗎) → 位子 → 位
- **definition:** position; place; stand
- **pinyin:** wèi
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 立
    - lì
    - stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 人 (rén, "person") + phonetic: 立 (lì, "stand") =
    - person standing ->
    - position, rank
  - **interpretation:** The character 位 (wèi, "position") combines 人 (rén, "person") to signify a person and 立 (lì, "stand") to indicate the act of standing or taking a position. This reflects the idea of assuming a role or status.
- **examples:**
  - 他坐在第一位。
    - Tā zuò zài dì yī wèi.
    - He sits in the first position.
  - 老师(師)点(點)名时(時)，这(這)位学(學)生总(總)是表现(現)出色。
    - Lǎoshī diǎnmíng shí, zhè wèi xuéshēng zǒng shì biǎoxiàn chūsè.
    - When the teacher calls roll, this student always performs outstandingly.
  - 在会(會)议(議)上，他占(佔)据(據)了重要的一位。
    - Zài huìyì shàng, tā zhànjù le zhòngyào de yī wèi.
    - During the meeting, he occupied an important position.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 位](@media/glyph4f4d.png)
### 有位子吗(嗎) → 位子 → 位 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.

### 有位子吗(嗎) → 位子 → 位 → 立

- **pinyin:** lì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a person standing on the ground
  - **interpretation:** The character 立 (lì, 'stand') intuitively represents the concept of standing by depicting a person in an upright position, emphasizing the posture.
- **examples:**
  - 小王立在窗前，等待朋友到来(來)。
    - Xiǎo Wáng lì zài chuāng qián, děngdài péngyǒu dàolái.
    - Xiao Wang stands at the window, waiting for his friend to arrive.
  - 园(園)中雕像静(靜)立于(於)石台(臺)上。
    - Yuán zhōng diāoxiàng jìng lì yú shí tái shàng.
    - The statue in the garden stands quietly on the stone platform.
  - 士兵集合后(後)，整齐(齊)地立定阵(陣)型。
    - Shìbīng jíhé hòu, zhěngqí de lì dìng zhènxíng.
    - After the soldiers assemble, they stand in formation neatly.

### 有位子吗(嗎) → 位子 → 子
- **definition:** child; seed; noun suffix
- **pinyin:** zi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a baby with a large head and spread arms, with legs wrapped in a blanket
  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)小子很调(調)皮。
    - Zhè xiǎo zǐ hěn tiáopí.
    - This kid is very naughty.
  - 他的小子爱(愛)打篮(籃)球，每天都锻(鍛)炼(煉)身体(體)。
    - Tā de xiǎo zǐ ài dǎ lánqiú, měitiān dōu duànliàn shēntǐ.
    - His child loves playing basketball, and practices every day.
  - 孤独(獨)的子需要关(關)爱(愛)。
    - Gūdú de zǐ xūyào guān'ài.
    - A lonely child needs care.

### 有位子吗(嗎) → 嗎
- **definition:** question particle
- **pinyin:** ma
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 馬
    - mǎ
    - horse
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 馬 (mǎ, "horse") ->
    - question particle
  - **interpretation:** The character 嗎 (ma, "question particle") combines the semantic component 口 (kǒu, "mouth") indicating speech or communication, with the phonetic component 馬 (mǎ, "horse") to provide the sound. This creates the character used to indicate a question when speaking.
- **examples:**
  - 你今天好吗(嗎)？
    - Nǐ jīntiān hǎo ma?
    - How are you today?
  - 你会(會)说(說)中文吗(嗎)？
    - Nǐ huì shuō Zhōngwén ma?
    - Can you speak Chinese?
  - 今天天气(氣)很好，对(對)吗(嗎)？
    - Jīntiān tiānqì hěn hǎo, duì ma?
    - The weather is great today, isn't it?
### 有位子吗(嗎) → 嗎 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 有位子吗(嗎) → 嗎 → 馬
- **definition:** horse
- **pinyin:** mǎ
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 灬
    - huǒ
    - four dots
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horse with head left, flowing mane ->
    - head simplified to 目 (mù, "eye"); legs to 灬 (huǒ, "four dots")
  - **interpretation:** The character 馬 (mǎ, "horse") pictorially represents a horse with a flowing mane and simplified features: the head as an eye and legs as dots. It clearly conveys the image of a horse.
  - **simplification:** 马(馬): simplified by adopting a cursive script form.
- **examples:**
  - 那匹马(馬)在草原上奔跑。
    - Nà pǐ mǎ zài cǎoyuán shàng bēnpǎo.
    - That horse runs on the grassland.
  - 农(農)夫牵(牽)着马(馬)，走向村庄(莊)。
    - Nóngfū qiānzhe mǎ, zǒuxiàng cūnzhuāng.
    - The farmer leads the horse, walking towards the village.
  - 小女孩骑(騎)着马(馬)，在花园(園)里玩耍。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái qízhe mǎ, zài huāyuán lǐ wánshuǎ.

### 有位子吗(嗎) → 嗎 → 馬 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.

### 有位子吗(嗎) → 嗎 → 馬 → 灬
- **definition:** four dots
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames or fire at the bottom of a character
  - **interpretation:** The character 灬(biāo, 'fire') visually resembles flames and is used to represent fire-related concepts, especially as a radical component in many Chinese characters.
- **examples:**
  - 灬是燃烧(燒)的象征(徵)。
    - biāo shì ránshāo de xiàngzhēng.
    - Fire is a symbol of burning.
  - 夜幕降临(臨)时(時)，灬映出温(溫)暖的光芒。
    - yè mù jiàng lín shí, biāo yìng chū wēnnuǎn de guāngmáng.
    - When night falls, fire radiates a warm glow.
  - 狂风(風)暴雨后(後)，灬象征(徵)重生。
    - kuáng fēng bào yǔ hòu, biāo xiàngzhēng chóngshēng.
    - After the storm, fire symbolizes rebirth.

## 李旭婷
---
## Chinese personal name
### Lǐ Xùtíng
---
- **definition:** Chinese personal name
- **pinyin:** Lǐ Xùtíng
- **components:**
  - 李
    - Lǐ
    - a common Chinese surname
  - 旭
    - xù
    - dawn; rising sun
  - 婷
    - tíng
    - graceful; elegant; attractive
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** A Chinese personal name, typically consisting of a family name followed by two given names.
  - **interpretation:** 李 (Lǐ, "a common Chinese surname") is one of the most common Chinese surnames, originating from the plum tree. 旭 (xù, "dawn; rising sun") represents the rising sun and often symbolizes new beginnings or hope. 婷 (tíng, "graceful; elegant; attractive") suggests grace and elegance. Together, the name 李旭婷 (Lǐ Xùtíng) combines the common surname 李 with a given name evoking the hopeful beauty of a new dawn and grace, typical for personal names that reflect positive attributes or aspirations for the individual.
- **examples:**
  - 李旭婷是我的好朋友。
    - Lǐ Xùtíng shì wǒ de hǎo péngyǒu.
    - Li Xuting is my good friend.
  - 我昨天见(見)到了李旭婷，她看起来(來)很开(開)心。
    - Wǒ zuótiān jiàn dào le Lǐ Xùtíng, tā kàn qǐlái hěn kāixīn.
    - I met Li Xuting yesterday, she looked very happy.
  - 李旭婷喜欢(歡)旅行，她去过(過)很多国(國)家。
    - Lǐ Xùtíng xǐhuān lǚxíng, tā qù guò hěn duō guójiā.
    - Li Xuting likes traveling, she has visited many countries.
### 李旭婷 → 李
- **definition:** a common Chinese surname
- **pinyin:** Lǐ
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 來 (lái, originally representing 'wheat') became corrupted to 木 (mù, 'tree') + semantic 子 (zǐ, 'child') ->
    - 李
  - **interpretation:** Originally a phono-semantic compound with 來 (lái, originally 'wheat') providing sound and 子 (zǐ, 'child') lending meaning. Over time, 來 was corrupted to 木 (mù, 'tree'), suggesting a 'plum tree', which is also associated with the surname Li, well-known in Chinese culture.
- **examples:**
  - 李老师(師)是我们(們)的数(數)学(學)老师(師)。
    - Lǐ lǎoshī shì wǒmen de shùxué lǎoshī.
    - Mr. Li is our math teacher.
  - 李先生邀请(請)我们(們)去他的茶馆(館)。
    - Lǐ xiānshēng yāoqǐng wǒmen qù tā de cháguǎn.
    - Mr. Li invited us to his tea house.
  - 我常常和李小姐去公园(園)散步。
    - Wǒ chángcháng hé Lǐ xiǎojiě qù gōngyuán sànbù.
    - I often go for walks in the park with Miss Li.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 李](@media/glyph674e.png)
### 李旭婷 → 李 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 李旭婷 → 李 → 子
- **definition:** child
- **pinyin:** zǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a baby with a large head and spread arms, with legs wrapped in a blanket
  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)小子很调(調)皮。
    - Zhè xiǎo zǐ hěn tiáopí.
    - This kid is very naughty.
  - 他的小子爱(愛)打篮(籃)球，每天都锻(鍛)炼(煉)身体(體)。
    - Tā de xiǎo zǐ ài dǎ lánqiú, měitiān dōu duànliàn shēntǐ.
    - His child loves playing basketball, and practices every day.
  - 孤独(獨)的子需要关(關)爱(愛)。
    - Gūdú de zǐ xūyào guān'ài.
    - A lonely child needs care.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 子](@media/glyph5b50.png)
### 李旭婷 → 旭
- **definition:** dawn; rising sun
- **pinyin:** xù
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 九
    - jiǔ
    - nine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 日 (rì, "sun") + phonetic 九 (jiǔ) ->
    - rising sun
  - **interpretation:** The character 旭(xù, "rising sun; dawn") combines the semantic component 日 (rì, "sun"), suggesting brightness or a celestial body, with the phonetic component 九 (jiǔ), which contributes the sound. This combination conveys the sense of the sun rising, signifying dawn or the early morning.
- **examples:**
  - 天边(邊)露出了旭日，空气(氣)显(顯)得特别(別)清新。
    - Tiānbiān lùchūle xùrì, kōngqì xiǎnde tèbié qīngxīn.
    - The rising sun appeared on the horizon, and the air felt especially fresh.
  - 旭光渐(漸)渐(漸)照亮了大地。
    - Xù guāng jiànjiàn zhàoliàngle dàdì.
    - The light of the rising sun gradually illuminated the land.
  - 每天清晨，我们(們)都会(會)沐浴在旭日的光辉(輝)中。
    - Měitiān qīngchén, wǒmen dōu huì mùyù zài xù rì de guānghuī zhōng.
    - Every morning, we bathe in the glory of the rising sun.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 旭](@media/glyph65ed.png)
### 李旭婷 → 旭 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 李旭婷 → 旭 → 九
- **definition:** nine
- **pinyin:** jiǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized hand with bent wrist ->
    - original 'elbow' 肘 (zhǒu) meaning ->
    - associated with nine as metaphorical bumping up against ten
  - **interpretation:** 九 originally depicted the elbow, symbolizing movement akin to pulling back in momentum, which culturally reflects nearing a complete cycle at ten. Later, 九 came to symbolize the number nine, a fist bumping up against ten, the last count on one's fingers.
- **examples:**
  - 今天是九号(號)。
    - Jīntiān shì jiǔ hào.
    - Today is the ninth.
  - 她有九个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Tā yǒu jiǔ gè píngguǒ.
    - She has nine apples.
  - 我们(們)九点(點)钟(鐘)出发(發)，去探望朋友。
    - Wǒmen jiǔ diǎn zhōng chūfā, qù tànwàng péngyǒu.
    - We will leave at nine o'clock to visit a friend.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 九](@media/glyph4e5d.png)
### 李旭婷 → 婷
- **definition:** graceful; elegant; attractive
- **pinyin:** tíng
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 亭
    - tíng
    - pavilion
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 女 (nǚ, "woman") + phonetic 亭 (tíng) ->
    - graceful, elegant
  - **interpretation:** The character uses 女 (nǚ, "woman") as its semantic component, indicating qualities typically associated with femininity, such as grace and elegance. 亭 (tíng) provides the phonetic component, contributing its sound to the character.
- **examples:**
  - 她的舞姿非常优(優)雅，如同一朵轻(輕)盈的莲(蓮)花。
    - Tā de wǔzī fēicháng yōuyǎ, rútóng yī duǒ qīngyíng de liánhuā.
    - Her dance moves are very graceful, like a light lotus flower.
  - 这(這)个(個)花园(園)设(設)计(計)得很精致(緻)，充满(滿)了优(優)雅的气(氣)息。
    - Zhège huāyuán shèjì de hěn jīngzhì, chōngmǎn le yōuyǎ de qìxī.
    - This garden is designed meticulously and is filled with an elegant ambiance.
  - 她散发(發)着(著)一种(種)自然的美丽(麗)，令人赞(讚)叹(嘆)不已。
    - Tā sànfā zhe yī zhǒng zìrán de měilì, lìngrén zàntàn bùyǐ.
    - She exudes a natural beauty that leaves people in awe.
### 李旭婷 → 婷 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.

### 李旭婷 → 婷 → 亭
- **definition:** pavilion
- **pinyin:** tíng
- **components:**
  - 京
    - jīng
    - capital
  - 丁
    - dīng
    - nail
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** semantic 京 (jīng, 'capital') variant, stylized as tower + phonetic 丁 (dīng, 'nail')
  - **interpretation:** The character 亭(tíng, 'pavilion') combines a variant of 京 (jīng, 'capital city'), stylized to resemble a tower or platform, with 丁 (dīng, 'nail') as the phonetic component. This representation suggests a small, fixed structure such as a pavilion, where the 'tower-like' form conveys the sense of an elevated, ornamental building.
- **examples:**
  - 在公园(園)里(裡)有一个(個)漂亮的亭子。
    - Zài gōngyuán lǐ yǒu yī gè piàoliang de tíngzi.

  - 我们(們)坐在亭里(裡)，欣赏(賞)周围(圍)的风(風)景。
    - Wǒmen zuò zài tíng lǐ, xīnshǎng zhōuwéi de fēngjǐng.
    - We sit in the pavilion, enjoying the surrounding scenery.
  - 亭子的屋顶(頂)是用传(傳)统(統)的瓦片做的。
    - Tíngzi de wūdǐng shì yòng chuántǒng de wǎpiàn zuò de.
    - The roof of the pavilion is made with traditional tiles.

### 李旭婷 → 婷 → 亭 → 京
- **definition:** capital
- **pinyin:** jīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tall building or tower
  - **interpretation:** The character 京 (jīng, "tower") is a pictogram representing a tall building or a tower. Its form directly illustrates the concept of height and grandeur associated with a prominent structure.
- **examples:**
  - 故宫(宮)的塔楼(樓)很高。
    - Gùgōng de tǎlóu hěn gāo.
    - The tower of the Forbidden City is very tall.
  - 在北京，你可以看到许(許)多高楼(樓)大厦(廈)。
    - Zài Běijīng, nǐ kěyǐ kàn dào xǔduō gāolóu dàshà.
    - In Beijing, you can see many tall buildings.
  - 古代的建筑(築)中常常能见(見)到高耸(聳)的塔顶(頂)。
    - Gǔdài de jiànzhú zhōng chángcháng néng jiàn dào gāosǒng de tǎdǐng.

### 李旭婷 → 婷 → 亭 → 丁
- **definition:** nail
- **pinyin:** dīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of a nail ->
    - 丁
  - **interpretation:** The character 丁 originally depicted the head of a nail, emphasizing simplicity and directness. While it has developed other interpretations over time, such as a head or city wall, these relate to similar shapes and functions. Today, 釘 (dīng, 'nail') reflects this meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 工人熟练(練)地把丁敲进(進)了墙(牆)壁。
    - Gōngrén shúliàn de bǎ dīng qiāng jìnle qiángbì.
    - The worker skillfully hammered the nail into the wall.

    - Tā jīngxīn tiāoxuǎnle tiě zhì dīng, quèbǎo jiājù wěngù.
    - He carefully selected the iron nail to ensure the furniture was stable.
  - 请(請)把散落的丁收好。
    - Qǐng bǎ sànluò de dīng shōuhǎo.
    - Please gather the scattered nails.

## 松茸
---
## matsutake mushroom
### sōng róng
---
- **definition:** matsutake mushroom
- **pinyin:** sōng róng
- **components:**
  - 松
    - sōng
    - pine
  - 茸
    - róng
    - mushroom; fungi; soft growth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 松 (sōng, "pine") refers to the tree species and is often associated with natural or wild environments. 茸 (róng, "mushroom") is used to denote soft, downy growths or fungi such as mushrooms.
  - **interpretation:** 松茸 (sōngróng, "matsutake mushroom") refers to a type of mushroom known for growing in pine forests. The name emphasizes the natural habitat of the matsutake, which is often found among pine trees.
- **examples:**
  - 松茸是一种(種)名贵(貴)的食用菌。
    - sōng róng shì yī zhǒng míng guì de shí yòng jūn.
    - Matsutake mushroom is a prized edible fungus.
  - 松茸在深山中生长(長)，被誉(譽)为(為)珍稀食品。
    - sōng róng zài shēn shān zhōng shēng zhǎng, bèi yù wéi zhēn xī shí pǐn.
    - Matsutake mushrooms grow in deep mountains and are revered as a rare delicacy.
### 松茸 → 松(鬆)
- **traditional:** 鬆
- **definition:** pine
- **pinyin:** sōng
- **components:**
  - 髟
    - biāo
    - hair
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 髟 ("hair") + phonetic 松 (sōng) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** 鬆 (sōng, "loose") combines 髟 (biāo, "hair") as the semantic element expressing the idea of looseness or something flowing freely, similar to hair, with 松 (sōng, "pine") as the phonetic element. This links to the concept of being loose or relaxed, as hair can freely flow and pine branches are not tightly bound.
  - **simplification:** The simplified form 松(鬆) (sōng, "pine") retains 毛 (máo, "fur") as a reduced element replacing 髟 (biāo, "hair") and removing excess components for simplicity.
- **examples:**
  - 院子里(裡)有一棵高大的松(鬆)树(樹)。
    - Yuànzi lǐ yǒu yī kē gāodà de sōngshù.
    - There is a tall pine tree in the yard.
  - 那片森林以松(鬆)树(樹)闻(聞)名。
    - Nà piàn sēnlín yǐ sōngshù wénmíng.
    - That forest is famous for its pine trees.
  - 他躺在松(鬆)针(針)覆盖(蓋)的地面上。
    - Tā tǎng zài sōngzhēn fùgài de dìmiàn shàng.
    - He lay on the ground covered with pine needles.
### 松茸 → 松(鬆) → 髟
- **definition:** hair
- **pinyin:** biāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person with long hair ->
    - represents long hair
  - **interpretation:** The character 髟(biāo, "hair") is a pictogram, symbolizing a person adorned with long hair, emphasizing its characteristic texture and appearance.
- **examples:**
  - 她的髟柔顺(順)如丝(絲)。
    - Tā de biāo róushùn rú sī.
    - Her hair is as smooth as silk.
  - 他每天早上花时(時)间(間)整理髟，保持整洁(潔)。
    - Tā měitiān zǎoshang huā shíjiān zhěnglǐ biāo, bǎochí zhěngjié.
    - He spends time every morning tidying his hair, keeping it neat.
  - 这(這)本字典详(詳)细(細)介绍(紹)了髟的历(歷)史。
    - Zhè běn zìdiǎn xiángxì jièshào le biāo de lìshǐ.
    - This dictionary details the history of the hair radical.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 髟](@media/glyph9adf.png)
### 松茸 → 茸
- **definition:** mushroom; fungi; soft growth
- **pinyin:** róng
- **components:**
  - 艸
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 聰
    - cōng
    - intelligent
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艸 ('grass') + phonetic abbreviation of 聰 ('intelligent') ->
    - fungi/mushroom
  - **interpretation:** The character 茸(róng) ('mushroom; fungi; soft growth') combines 艸 (cǎo, 'grass') as the semantic component, indicating the natural plant-like or soft qualities of fungi, with a phonetic abbreviation from 聰 (cōng, 'intelligent'). The phonetic part contributes the sound, while the semantic part relates to the character's meaning of something growing among or resembling grass, like fungi or soft growth.
- **examples:**
  - 草原上长(長)满(滿)了茸草。
    - Cǎoyuán shàng zhǎng mǎn le róngcǎo.
    - The grassland is covered with soft grass.
  - 她的玩具熊有茸茸的表面。
    - Tā de wánjù xióng yǒu róngróng de biǎomiàn.
    - Her teddy bear has a fluffy surface.
  - 树(樹)林里(裡)充满(滿)了各种(種)各样(樣)的茸。
    - Shùlín lǐ chōngmǎn le gè zhǒng gè yàng de róng.
    - The forest is filled with various types of fungi.
### 松茸 → 茸 → 艸
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - grass
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts grass blades ->
    - duplication of 屮 (chè, 'grass') ->
    - grass imagery
  - **interpretation:** The character 艸(cǎo, 'grass') is a pictorial representation of grass blades. It is essentially a duplication of the character 屮 (chè, 'grass'), visually suggesting the appearance of grass tufts through repetition, emphasizing the concept of grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 公园(園)里(裡)绿(綠)艸茵茵。
    - Gōngyuán lǐ lǜ cǎo yīn yīn.
    - The park is filled with lush grass.
  - 晨露滋润(潤)艸丛(叢)，微风(風)使它们(們)起舞。
    - Chénlù zīrùn cǎo cóng, wēifēng shǐ tāmen qǐwǔ.
    - The morning dew nourishes the cluster of grass, and the breeze makes them dance.
  - 秋天时(時)艸变(變)黄(黃)，冬天它又枯萎。
    - Qiūtiān shí cǎo biàn huáng, dōngtiān tā yòu kūwěi.
    - In autumn, the grass turns yellow, and in winter, it withers.
- **historical forms:**

### 松茸 → 茸 → 艸 → 屮
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润(潤)后(後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屮](@media/glyph5c6e.png)
### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰
- **definition:** intelligent
- **pinyin:** cōng
- **components:**
  - 耳
    - ěr
    - ear
  - 悤
    - cōng
    - intelligent
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 耳 (ěr, "ear") + phonetic 悤 (cōng) ->
    - listening ear leading to intelligence
  - **interpretation:** The character 聰(cōng, "clever") represents the concept of intelligence through sensitivity to sound and willingness to listen. The semantic component 耳 (ěr, "ear") signifies listening, while the phonetic component 悤 (cōng) helps convey the sound. Together, they depict someone who is keen at understanding and learning via hearing, reflecting cleverness.
- **examples:**
  - 他很聪(聰)明，总(總)是能找到解决(決)问(問)题(題)的方法。
    - Tā hěn cōngmíng, zǒng shì néng zhǎodào jiějué wèntí de fāngfǎ.
    - He is very clever and always finds ways to solve problems.
  - 聰明的人通常很有創意。
    - Cōngmíng de rén tōngcháng hěn yǒu chuàngyì.
    - Clever people are often very creative.
  - 这(這)本书(書)适(適)合聪(聰)明的学(學)生阅(閱)读(讀)。
    - Zhè běn shū shìhé cōngmíng de xuéshēng yuèdú.
    - This book is suitable for clever students to read.
### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰 → 耳
- **definition:** ear
- **pinyin:** ěr
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an ear
  - **interpretation:** The character 耳 (ěr, "ear") is a pictogram that visually represents an ear with its distinctive shape. This straightforward representation made it intuitive for ancient speakers to associate the character directly with the concept of an ear.
- **examples:**
  - 音乐(樂)直入耳。
    - Yīn yuè zhí rù ěr.
    - The music goes straight to the ear.
  - 他亲(親)耳听(聽)到谣(謠)言，心中充满(滿)疑虑(慮)。
    - Tā qīn ěr tīng dào yáo yán, xīn zhōng chōng mǎn yí lǜ.
    - He heard the rumor with his own ears, and his heart was filled with doubt.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 耳](@media/glyph8033.png)
### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰 → 悤
- **definition:** intelligent
- **pinyin:** cōng
- **components:**
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
  - 囪
    - cōng
    - patterned shape
  - 聰
    - cōng
    - intelligent
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 心 (xīn, "heart") + 囪 as a patterned shape in Han dynasty ->
    - evolved from original cleverness ->
    - later indicating haste
  - **interpretation:** The original form of 悤 (cōng, "clever") depicts a heart 心 (xīn, "heart") with a dot indicating a hole, which symbolized intelligence. Over time, the dot evolved into a more complex pattern 囪 during the Han dynasty, transforming the character's meaning to indicate haste, possibly due to the idea of learning quickly or acting with intelligence. This semantic shift is reflected in its derivation to 聰 (cōng, "intelligent") that preserves the original meaning of cleverness.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 悤](@media/glyph60a4.png)
### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰 → 悤 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. Over time, it has become highly stylized, but it continues to convey the notion of the heart as the center of emotions and consciousness.
- **examples:**
  - 她的心一直都在帮(幫)助别(別)人。
    - Tā de xīn yīzhí dōu zài bāngzhù biérén.
    - Her heart is always in helping others.
  - 在城市的中心，有一个(個)美丽(麗)的公园(園)。
    - Zài chéngshì de zhōngxīn, yǒu yí gè měilì de gōngyuán.
    - At the center of the city, there is a beautiful park.
  - 对(對)于(於)许(許)多人来(來)说(說)，家庭是生活的核心。
    - Duìyú xǔduō rén lái shuō, jiātíng shì shēnghuó de héxīn.
    - For many people, family is the core of life.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 心](@media/glyph5fc3.png)
### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰 → 悤 → 囪
- **definition:** patterned shape
- **pinyin:** cōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a window with a shutter ->
    - original representation of an architectural feature
  - **interpretation:** The character 囪(cōng, 'patterned shape') originally depicted a window closed with a shutter, visually representing an architectural feature that provided ventilation and light while maintaining security. This representation suggests the utility and style of such windows, forming the basis for its association with patterns or shapes.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 囪](@media/glyph56ea.png)

## 油条(條)
---
## fried dough stick
### yóu tiáo
---
- **traditional:** 油條
- **definition:** fried dough stick
- **pinyin:** yóu tiáo
- **components:**
  - 油
    - yóu
    - oil
  - 条(條)
    - tiáo
    - strip; streak; item
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 油 (yóu, "oil") + 条(條) (tiáo, "strip") =
    - 油条(條) (yóutiáo, "fried dough stick")
  - **interpretation:** The term refers to a strip of dough that is deep-fried in oil, common in Chinese cuisine as a breakfast item or snack. The name directly describes its preparation method and shape: frying (油) in oil and its oblong, strip-like form (条).
  - **simplification:** Simplified from 油條
- **examples:**
  - 早餐常常配有油条(條)和豆浆(漿)。
    - Zǎocān chángcháng pèiyǒu yóutiáo hé dòujiāng.
    - Breakfast is often served with fried dough sticks and soy milk.
  - 中式早餐里(裡)有油条(條)，口感松软(軟)细(細)腻(膩)。
    - Zhōngshì zǎocān lǐ yǒu yóutiáo, kǒugǎn sōngruǎn xìnì.
    - In Chinese-style breakfasts, fried dough sticks are present, and they have a soft and delicate texture.
  - 唐代的市集常见(見)油条(條)，深受市民喜爱(愛)。
    - Tángdài de shìjí chángjiàn yóutiáo, shēnshòu shìmín xǐ'ài.
    - In the Tang Dynasty markets, fried dough sticks were commonly seen and were much loved by citizens.
### 油条(條) → 油
- **definition:** oil
- **pinyin:** yóu
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 由
    - yóu
    - reason
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵 (shuǐ, 'water') + phonetic 由 (yóu, 'reason') =
    - liquid that flows ->
    - oil, sauce
  - **interpretation:** The character 油(yóu) combines the water radical 氵 (shuǐ, 'water') with the phonetic 由 (yóu, 'reason'). This suggests something liquid, aligning with the meanings 'oil' and 'sauce', both of which flow like water.
- **examples:**
  - 油可以用来(來)炒菜。
    - Yóu kěyǐ yòng lái chǎo cài.
    - Oil can be used for stir-frying dishes.
  - 我喜欢(歡)辣椒油，因为(為)它增加了味道。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān làjiāo yóu, yīnwèi tā zēngjiāle wèidào.
    - I like chili oil because it enhances the flavor.
  - 煎鱼(魚)时(時)可以先在鱼(魚)上抹点(點)油，这(這)样(樣)鱼(魚)更滑嫩。
    - Jiān yú shí kěyǐ xiān zài yú shàng mǒ diǎn yóu, zhèyàng yú gèng huá nèn.
    - When pan-frying fish, you can first spread a little oil on the fish, so that the fish becomes more tender.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 油](@media/glyph6cb9.png)
### 油条(條) → 油 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字中偏旁氵，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快戏(戲)水。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 油条(條) → 油 → 由
- **definition:** reason
- **pinyin:** yóu
- **components:**
  - 十
    - shí
    - ten
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic 十 (needle) + semantic 口 (mouth) ->
    - container with a needle symbolizing an ancient pronunciation
  - **interpretation:** The character 由(yóu, 'cause') depicts a container with a top resembling a needle (十), phonetic for sound with 口 (mouth) for semantic influence, symbolizing something that originates from a cause, just as contents originate from a container.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)问(問)题(題)由他负(負)责(責)。
    - Zhège wèntí yóu tā fùzé.
    - This issue is caused by him to be responsible.
  - 一切的变(變)化都是由时(時)间(間)引起的。
    - Yīqiè de biànhuà dōu shì yóu shíjiān yǐnqǐ de.
    - All changes are caused by the passage of time.
  - 胜(勝)利由努力而来(來)。
    - Shènglì yóu nǔlì ér lái.
    - Victory is caused by effort.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 由](@media/glyph7531.png)
### 油条(條) → 油 → 由 → 十
- **definition:** ten
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original vertical stroke ->
    - later horizontal stroke added ->
    - forms a cross ->
    - represents 'ten'
  - **interpretation:** The character 十(shí, 'ten') represents the number ten with a cross shape that could be seen as tally marks. It evolved from a simple vertical stroke to a cross by adding a horizontal stroke, symbolizing a complete set of ten.
- **examples:**
  - 我有十本书(書)。
    - Wǒ yǒu shí běn shū.
    - I have ten books.
  - 花园(園)里(裡)有十棵树(樹)，景色十分优(優)美。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu shí kē shù, jǐngsè shífēn yōuměi.
    - There are ten trees in the garden, and the scenery is very beautiful.
  - 十年磨一剑(劍)。
    - Shí nián mó yī jiàn.
    - It takes ten years of practice to hone a sword.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 十](@media/glyph5341.png)
### 油条(條) → 油 → 由 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 油条(條) → 条(條)
- **traditional:** 條
- **definition:** strip; streak; item
- **pinyin:** tiáo
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 攸
    - yōu
    - a place far away
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "wood") + phonetic 攸 (yōu) ->
    - originally indicates a small branch or wooden stick
  - **interpretation:** The character 條 (tiáo, "strip; streak; item") combines the semantic 木 (mù, "wood") to suggest something made of wood, and the phonetic 攸 (yōu) to provide the pronunciation. Initially, it referred specifically to a small branch or stick made of wood, which logically leads to the modern extended meanings of a 'strip' or 'item' in more general contexts because of the similar shape and form.
  - **simplification:** 条(條) simplifies 條 by removing the 木 (mù, "wood") component and simplifying 攸 (yōu) to a simpler form, focusing on phonetics rather than semantic resemblance to wood.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)条(條)裙子很好看。
    - Zhè tiáo qúnzi hěn hǎokàn.
    - This dress looks very nice.
  - 河上架了一座长(長)长(長)的桥(橋)。
    - Hé shàng jiàle yī zuò cháng cháng de qiáo.
    - A long bridge was built over the river.
  - 他发(發)送了一条(條)短信，通知朋友聚会(會)时(時)间(間)。
    - Tā fāsòngle yī tiáo duǎnxìn, tōngzhī péngyǒu jùhuì shíjiān.
    - He sent a text message, informing friends of the gathering time.
### 油条(條) → 条(條) → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 油条(條) → 条(條) → 攸
- **definition:** a place far away
- **pinyin:** yōu
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 攴
    - pū
    - strike
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 攴 (pū, "strike" or "hit") ->
    - depiction may include drops of water ->
    - combines to suggest 'warning' or 'purification'
  - **interpretation:** The character 攸 is an ideogrammic compound with 人 (rén, "person") + 攴 (pū, "strike" or "hit"). Two interpretations exist: one posits it as a depiction of a person about to be disciplined, thus suggesting 'warning'; another suggests a ritual washing, connected to ceremonial purification, and thus involves water symbolism. The sense of 'distant' likely emerged as a metaphorical extension from the idea of warning or cleansing, which sets one apart or corrects a path.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 攸](@media/glyph6538.png)
### 油条(條) → 条(條) → 攸 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 油条(條) → 条(條) → 攸 → 攴
- **definition:** strike
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩鼓面，传(傳)递(遞)出节(節)奏的信号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了一下门(門)，唤(喚)起了室内(內)的安静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 攴](@media/glyph6534.png)
### 油条(條) → 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 油条(條) → 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 油条(條) → 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卜](@media/glyph535c.png)

## 海派
---
## Shanghai style
### hǎi pài
---
- **definition:** Shanghai style
- **pinyin:** hǎi pài
- **components:**
  - 海
    - hǎi
    - sea; ocean; maritime; large
  - 派
    - pài
    - style; group; faction; school
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 海 (hǎi, "sea") refers to the coastal and maritime element of Shanghai, a city near the East China Sea, indicating the openness and cosmopolitan nature of the city due to its sea connections. 派 (pài, "style; school; faction") describes a distinct approach or characteristic appearance related to a group or region. Here, it indicates a distinctive style that is associated with Shanghai.
  - **interpretation:** 海 (hǎi, "sea") suggests the openness, trade, and external influences due to Shanghai's maritime location, reflecting a cosmopolitan lifestyle. 派 (pài, "style; school") implies a unique cultural or artistic expression, and in this context, refers to the innovative and avant-garde aspects of Shanghai's culture and lifestyle shaped by its international interactions.
- **examples:**
  - 他的穿着(著)非常海派。
    - Tā de chuānzhuó fēicháng hǎi pài.
    - His clothing style is very Shanghai style.
  - 这(這)种(種)建筑(築)体(體)现(現)了海派风(風)格。
    - Zhè zhǒng jiànzhù tǐxiànle hǎi pài fēnggé.
    - This type of architecture embodies the Shanghai style.
  - 我喜欢(歡)海派的艺(藝)术(術)作品。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān hǎi pài de yìshù zuòpǐn.
    - I love Shanghai style art pieces.
### 海派 → 海
- **definition:** sea; ocean; maritime; large
- **pinyin:** hǎi
- **components:**
  - 氵(水)
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 每
    - měi
    - each
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic 每 (měi) ->
    - sea; ocean
  - **interpretation:** The character 海(hǎi, "sea; ocean") combines the semantic component 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water"), representing water or fluidity, with the phonetic component 每 (měi), which provides the pronunciation. The meaning of 'sea or ocean' naturally extends from the association with water, emphasizing a large body of it.
- **examples:**
  - 孩子们(們)喜欢(歡)去海边(邊)玩耍。
    - Háizimen xǐhuān qù hǎibiān wánshuǎ.
    - Children like to play by the sea.
  - 海洋的蓝(藍)色令人心旷(曠)神怡。
    - Hǎiyáng de lánsè lìng rén xīnkuàngshényí.
    - The blue of the ocean is refreshing.
  - 他梦(夢)想去环(環)游(遊)世界的海洋。
    - Tā mèngxiǎng qù huányóu shìjiè de hǎiyáng.
    - He dreams of traveling around the world's oceans.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 海](@media/glyph6d77.png)
### 海派 → 海 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字中偏旁氵，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快戏(戲)水。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 海派 → 海 → 每
- **definition:** each
- **pinyin:** měi
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
  - 母
    - mǔ
    - mother
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 屮 (sprout) + phonetic 母 (mǔ, "mother") ->
    - adult woman ready for marriage and generation ->
    - each time
  - **interpretation:** The character 每 (měi, "each") combines the semantic element 屮 ("sprout") with the phonetic 母 (mǔ, "mother"). The sprout component implies growth and maturity, suggesting a woman has reached adulthood. This connects to the idea of 'each time' through the readiness for recurring life cycles or activities, such as marriage and childbearing.
- **examples:**
  - 每个(個)人都有自己的梦(夢)想。
    - Měi gèrén dōu yǒu zìjǐ de mèngxiǎng.
    - Each person has their own dreams.
  - 他每天早上锻(鍛)炼(鍊)身体(體)。
    - Tā měitiān zǎoshang duànliàn shēntǐ.
    - He exercises every morning.
  - 每次见(見)到她，我都很开(開)心。
    - Měi cì jiàndào tā, wǒ dōu hěn kāixīn.
    - Each time I see her, I am very happy.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 每](@media/glyph6bcf.png)
### 海派 → 海 → 每 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润(潤)后(後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屮](@media/glyph5c6e.png)
### 海派 → 海 → 每 → 母
- **definition:** mother
- **pinyin:** mǔ
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** differentiated form
  - **description:**
    - 女 (nǚ, "woman") + addition of two dots ->
    - distinguished as 母 (mǔ, "mother")
  - **interpretation:** The character 母 (mǔ, "mother") is a differentiated form of 女 (nǚ, "woman") with the addition of two dots to distinguish it. In early script forms, both 母 (mǔ, "mother") and 女 (nǚ, "woman") were represented by the same form as 女, necessitating the addition of dots to create a visual distinction. The character 毋, originally borrowed from 母, further specialized by changing the dots to a stroke to avoid confusion between the characters.
- **examples:**
  - 母给(給)了我无(無)限的温(溫)暖。
    - mǔ gěi le wǒ wúxiàn de wēnnuǎn
    - Mother has given me endless warmth.
  - 我的母温(溫)柔而坚(堅)毅，培养(養)了我良好的品格。
    - wǒ de mǔ wēnróu ér jiānyì, péiyǎng le wǒ liánghǎo de pǐngé
    - My mother is gentle and strong, nurturing my good character.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 母](@media/glyph6bcd.png)
### 海派 → 海 → 每 → 母 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 女](@media/glyph5973.png)
### 海派 → 派
- **definition:** style; group; faction; school
- **pinyin:** pài
- **components:**
  - 水
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 𠂢
    - mǐ
    - original form
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Pictogram: 𠂢 (original form) ->
    - Phono-semantic: semantic 水 (shuǐ, "water; river") + phonetic 𠂢 =
    - differentiation of original form with water
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted 𠂢 alone. To differentiate and specify meanings related to water or a flowing style, 水 (shuǐ, "water; river") was added as a semantic element.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)研究传(傳)统(統)文人派，注重文化底蕴(蘊)。
    - Wǒmen yánjiū chuántǒng wénrén pài, zhùzhòng wénhuà dǐyùn.
    - We study the traditional literati school, emphasizing cultural depth.
  - 他加入了摇(搖)滚(滾)派，追求自由精神。
    - Tā jiārùle yáogǔn pài, zhuīqiú zìyóu jīngshén.
    - He joined the rock group to pursue a spirit of freedom.
  - 古典音乐(樂)派，具有悠久历(歷)史。
    - Gǔdiǎn yīnyuè pài, jùyǒu yōujiǔ lìshǐ.
    - The classical music school has a long history.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 派](@media/glyph6d3e.png)
### 海派 → 派 → 水
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flowing water
  - **interpretation:** 水 (shuǐ, 'water') is a pictogram that directly represents the appearance of flowing water, making it intuitive and easy to recognize. Its simplicity and direct visual reference to its meaning have allowed it to remain unchanged over millennia.
- **examples:**
  - 水是一种(種)生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì yī zhǒng shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 夏天很热(熱)，喝水能解暑。
    - Xiàtiān hěn rè, hē shuǐ néng jiě shǔ.
    - It is very hot in summer, drinking water can relieve the heat.
  - 河水潺潺，沿岸绿(綠)树(樹)成荫(蔭)。
    - Hé shuǐ chánchán, yán'àn lǜshù chéng yīn.
    - The river flows babbling, and green trees along the bank provide shade.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 水](@media/glyph6c34.png)
### 海派 → 派 → 𠂢
- **definition:** original form
- **pinyin:** mǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a long river with tributaries ->
    - original form
  - **interpretation:** The character 𠂢 is a pictographic representation of a long river with tributaries, symbolizing its original form as it visually attempts to capture the imagery of flowing water and branching paths. It is described as the horizontal flip of 永 (yǒng, meaning 'eternal'), though its depiction clearly relates more to an aquatic landscape than an everlasting concept.

## 点(點)茶
---
## traditional tea whisking method
### diǎn chá
---
- **traditional:** 點茶
- **definition:** traditional tea whisking method
- **pinyin:** diǎn chá
- **components:**
  - 点(點)
    - diǎn
    - point; dot; order
  - 茶
    - chá
    - tea
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 點 (diǎn, "point; dot; order") + 茶 (chá, "tea")
  - **interpretation:** 點 (diǎn, "point; dot; order") originally refers to making a small mark or selecting. In the context of 點茶 (diǎn chá), it refers to the action of whisking or preparing tea, traditionally involving adding water drop by drop while whisking the tea into a frothy mixture. This process mirrors the careful, precise act of 点 (diǎn, "point; dot") where tea is methodically introduced and transformed. 茶 (chá, "tea") brings in the context of the beverage itself, emphasizing the ritualistic and artisanal process involved.
- **examples:**
  - 他喜欢(歡)研究点(點)茶的历(歷)史。
    - Tā xǐhuān yánjiū diǎn chá de lìshǐ.
    - He likes to study the history of traditional tea whisking.
  - 在宋代，点(點)茶是一种(種)流行的艺(藝)术(術)形式。
    - Zài Sòng dài, diǎn chá shì yī zhǒng liúxíng de yìshù xíngshì.
    - During the Song Dynasty, tea whisking was a popular art form.
  - 茶艺(藝)师(師)展示了点(點)茶的技巧。
    - Cháyìshī zhǎnshìle diǎn chá de jìqiǎo.
    - The tea artist demonstrated the technique of traditional tea whisking.
### 点(點)茶 → 点(點)
- **traditional:** 點
- **definition:** point; dot; order
- **pinyin:** diǎn
- **components:**
  - 黑
    - hēi
    - black
  - 占
    - zhān
    - divination
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 黑 (hēi, "black") + phonetic: 占 (zhān, "divination") =
    - black mark indicating a point ->
    - spot, dot
  - **interpretation:** In 點 (diǎn, "dot"), 黑 (hēi, "black") represents the concept of a mark or dot in its dark color, while 占 (zhān, "divination") provides the phonetic spelling. Together, the components denote a small dark mark or point.
  - **simplification:** 点(點) simplifies 點 by removing the upper components of 黑 (hēi, "black"), forming a more straightforward symbol for a dot or small point.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)在图(圖)上点(點)出目标(標)。
    - Qǐng zài tú shàng diǎn chū mùbiāo。
    - Please mark the target on the map.
  - 她用粉笔(筆)在黑板上点(點)了点(點)，指明答案。
    - Tā yòng fěnbǐ zài hēibǎn shàng diǎn le diǎn, zhǐmíng dá'àn。
    - She lightly tapped on the blackboard with chalk to indicate the answer.
  - 网(網)格中的每个(個)点(點)都很重要。
    - Wǎnggé zhōng de měi gè diǎn dōu hěn zhòngyào。
    - Every point in the grid is important.
### 点(點)茶 → 点(點) → 黑
- **definition:** black
- **pinyin:** hēi
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - person
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 大 (dà, "person") with a tattooed face for penal purposes ->
    - ancient punishments ->
    - dots added around 大 representing tattoo marks ->
    - erroneously interpreted as 火 (huǒ, "fire") under a chimney causing blackening ->
    - displaced 玄 (xuán, "black")
  - **interpretation:** The character 黑(hēi) originally represented a person with facial tattoos, symbolizing punishment. Over time, its meaning evolved to represent the color black, replacing 玄 (xuán, "black") which was previously used.
  - **simplification:** The character is not simplified in Chinese. However, in Japanese, the modern form 黒 replaces two dots with one stroke as part of orthographic reform.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)只乌(烏)鸦(鴉)的羽毛非常黑。
    - Zhè zhī wūyā de yǔmáo fēicháng hēi.
    - The crow's feathers are very black.
  - 他的心情因为(為)失落而变(變)得黑，看不出一丝(絲)笑容。
    - Tā de xīnqíng yīnwèi shīluò ér biànde hēi, kànbùchū yīsī xiàoróng.
    - His mood turned dark because of the loss, showing no trace of a smile.
  - 黑色在时(時)尚中代表神秘。
    - Hēisè zài shíshàng zhōng dàibiǎo shénmì.
    - Black represents mystery in fashion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 黑](@media/glyph9ed1.png)
### 点(點)茶 → 点(點) → 黑 → 大
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)房子很大。
    - Zhè ge fángzi hěn dà.
    - This house is very big.
  - 大海波涛(濤)汹(洶)涌(湧)，展现(現)出大自然的力量。
    - Dàhǎi bōtāo xiōngyǒng, zhǎnxiàn chū dàzìrán de lìliàng.
    - The vast ocean waves surge, showcasing the power of nature.
  - 大人物登场(場)，留下传(傳)奇。
    - Dà rénwù dēngchǎng, liúxià chuánqí.
    - Great figures make an appearance, leaving behind legends.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 大](@media/glyph5927.png)
### 点(點)茶 → 点(點) → 黑 → 大 → 夫
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a variant form of 大 (dà, "big") representing an adult man with a hairpin ->
    - became associated with 夫 (fū, "man").
  - **interpretation:** 夫 (fū, "man") was visually similar to 大 (dà, "big") and was originally interchangeable. The addition of the horizontal stroke was interpreted as a hairpin, symbolizing adulthood for men.
- **examples:**
  - 此夫心怀(懷)大志。
    - Cǐ fū xīn huái dà zhì.
    - This man has lofty aspirations.
  - 他勤劳(勞)努力，堪称(稱)良夫。
    - Tā qín láo nǔ lì, kān chēng liáng fū.
    - He works diligently and is regarded as an exemplary man.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夫](@media/glyph592b.png)
### 点(點)茶 → 点(點) → 黑 → 火
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火在壁炉(爐)中熊熊燃烧(燒)。
    - Huǒ zài bìlú zhōng xióngxióng ránshāo.
    - The fire burns fiercely in the fireplace.
  - 野外露营(營)时(時)，火能驱(驅)走寒冷。
    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇到火灾(災)时(時)，迅速疏散最为(為)重要。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.
    - In case of a fire, evacuating quickly is of utmost importance.

### 点(點)茶 → 点(點) → 占
- **definition:** divination
- **pinyin:** zhān
- **components:**
  - 卜
    - bǔ

  - 口
    - kǒu

  - **description:**
    - 卜 (bǔ, "divination") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") =
    - speaking about divination ->
    - divination
  - **interpretation:** The character 占 (zhān, "divination") represents the act of divination, combining the symbol for divination itself with the mouth, which may imply speaking or chanting during the divinatory practice.
- **examples:**
  - 古人借占，测(測)定吉凶。
    - Gǔ rén jiè zhān, cè dìng jí xiōng.

  - 他占了一卦。
    - Tā zhānle yī guà.
    - He performed a divination.
  - 他运(運)用占，预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Tā yùnyòng zhān, yùcè wèilái.

### 点(點)茶 → 点(點) → 占 → 卜
- **definition:** divination
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
