## 起床
---
## to get out of bed; to wake up
### qǐ chuáng
---
- **definition:** to get out of bed; to wake up
- **pinyin:** qǐ chuáng
- **components:**
  - 起
    - qǐ
    - to rise; to start; to get up from
  - 床
    - chuáng
    - bed
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 起 (qǐ, "to rise; to start; to get up from") combined with 床 (chuáng, "bed") refers to the action of getting up from a bed, embodying the process of transitioning from a lying position to standing.
  - **interpretation:** 起 (qǐ, "to rise") conveys the action of moving upward or beginning an action. In this context, it refers explicitly to starting the day by getting up. When paired with 床 (chuáng, "bed"), it specifies the exact place from which one rises, thus directly invoking the act of getting out of bed. The sense of 'to wake up' derives from this physical action as waking is the mental state accompanying rising.
- **examples:**
  - 我每天早上六点(點)起床。
    - Wǒ měitiān zǎoshang liù diǎn qǐ chuáng.
    - I wake up at six every morning.
  - 天气(氣)冷时(時)，我不想起床。
    - Tiānqì lěng shí, wǒ bù xiǎng qǐ chuáng.
    - When the weather is cold, I don't want to get out of bed.
  - 他迟(遲)到了因为(為)起床太晚。
    - Tā chídào le yīnwèi qǐ chuáng tài wǎn.
    - He was late because he got out of bed too late.
### 起床 → 起
- **definition:** to rise; to start; to get up from
- **pinyin:** qǐ
- **components:**
  - 走
    - zǒu
    - walk
  - 巳
    - sì
    - sixth of the Twelve Earthly Branches
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 走 (zǒu, "walk") + phonetic 巳 (sì) ->
    - rise; lift; begin; get up
  - **interpretation:** The semantic component 走 (zǒu, "walk") suggests movement or action, fitting with the meaning of rising or getting up. The phonetic component 巳 (sì) was chosen for its sound, contributing to the pronunciation without directly affecting the meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 太阳(陽)升起，天边(邊)染上橘色。
    - Tàiyáng shēng qǐ, tiānbiān rǎn shàng jú sè.
    - The sun rises, painting the sky with orange.
  - 我们(們)要起床了。
    - Wǒmen yào qǐchuáng le.
    - We need to get up.
  - 新的一天开(開)始了，大家都充满(滿)活力。
    - Xīn de yī tiān kāishǐ le, dàjiā dōu chōngmǎn huólì.
    - A new day begins, and everyone is full of energy.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 起](@media/glyph8d77.png)
### 起床 → 起 → 走
- **definition:** walk
- **pinyin:** zǒu
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 夭
    - yāo
    - young
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 龰
    - yuè
    - walking
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Running man (original depiction) + 止 (zhǐ, "foot") added later ->
    - top 夭 (yāo, "young") simplified to 土 (tǔ, "earth"), bottom stylized as 龰 ->
    - modern 走
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted a man running, with an added foot to emphasize movement. Over time, elements like the top 夭 were simplified to 土, and the bottom was stylized to 龰, although they are unrelated to the original meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 看到前方火光时(時)，他急忙走向安全地带(帶)。
    - Kàndào qiánfāng huǒguāng shí, tā jímáng zǒu xiàng ānquán dìdài.
    - When he saw the firelight ahead, he hurriedly ran toward safety.
  - 比赛(賽)开(開)始后(後)，选(選)手们(們)奋(奮)力走向终(終)点(點)。
    - Bǐsài kāishǐ hòu, xuǎnshǒu men fènlì zǒu xiàng zhōngdiǎn.
    - After the race began, the contestants ran towards the finish line.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 走](@media/glyph8d70.png)
### 起床 → 起 → 走 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 起床 → 起 → 走 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 起床 → 起 → 走 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)后(後)，他的足不能动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小明打球时(時)，不小心扭伤(傷)了足。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我每天锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足部。
    - wǒ měitiān duànliàn zúbù。
    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 足](@media/glyph8db3.png)
### 起床 → 起 → 走 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 起床 → 起 → 走 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

### 起床 → 起 → 走 → 夭
- **definition:** young
- **pinyin:** yāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a figure leaning forward, presumably running ->
    - energetic, young
  - **interpretation:** The character 夭(yāo) ("young") visually represents someone leaning forward in a motion that suggests energy and vitality associated with youthfulness. This imagery aligns with the concept of being lively or young.
- **examples:**
  - 他还夭，意气(氣)风(風)发(發)。
    - Tā hái yāo, yìqì fēngfā。
    - He is still young, full of youthful vigor.
  - 小女孩还夭，充满(滿)无(無)限活力。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái hái yāo, chōngmǎn wúxiàn huólì。
    - The little girl is still young, filled with boundless energy.

### 起床 → 起 → 走 → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院子里(裡)的土，适(適)合种(種)花。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
- **historical forms:**

### 起床 → 起 → 巳
- **definition:** sixth of the Twelve Earthly Branches
- **pinyin:** sì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a fetus or snake.
  - **interpretation:** The character 巳(sì, "fetus") likely represents the shape of a fetus curled in the womb or possibly the sinuous form of a snake. This ambiguity is due to its pictographic origin, imitating the curves and forms seen in nature.
- **examples:**
  - 那小小的巳在温(溫)暖的子宫(宮)中悄然成长(長)。
    - Nà xiǎoxiǎo de sì zài wēnnuǎn de zǐgōng zhōng qiǎorán chéngzhǎng.
    - The tiny fetus is growing quietly in the warm womb.
  - 医(醫)生发(發)现(現)巳异(異)常，提醒家长(長)早期注意。
    - Yīshēng fāxiàn sì yìcháng, tíxǐng jiāzhǎng zǎoqī zhùyì.
    - The doctor found an abnormality in the fetus and urged the parents to pay early attention.
  - 母亲(親)感受到巳微弱的心跳伴随(隨)着(著)温(溫)柔的希望。
    - Mǔqīn gǎnshòudào sì wēiruò de xīntiào bànsuízhe wēnróu de xīwàng.
    - The mother felt the fetus's faint heartbeat accompanied by a gentle hope.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 巳](@media/glyph5df3.png)
### 起床 → 床
- **definition:** bed
- **pinyin:** chuáng
- **components:**
  - 广(廣)
    - guǎng
    - house
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 广(廣) (guǎng, "house") + 木 (mù, "tree/wood") =
    - wooden furniture (bed) in a house
  - **interpretation:** The character 床 (chuáng, "bed") signifies a piece of wooden furniture located within a house. The inclusion of 木, meaning 'wood,' intuitively aligns with beds being made from wooden materials, while 广(廣) represents the enclosing structure of a house, emphasizing the indoor placement of furniture.
- **examples:**
  - 我睡在床上。
    - Wǒ shuì zài chuáng shàng.
    - I sleep on the bed.
  - 买(買)了新床，感觉(覺)睡眠更好。
    - Mǎile xīn chuáng, gǎnjué shuìmián gèng hǎo.
    - I bought a new bed, and I feel my sleep is better.
  - 孩子在床上玩耍，笑声(聲)充满(滿)房间(間)。
    - Háizi zài chuáng shàng wánshuǎ, xiàoshēng chōngmǎn fángjiān.
    - The child plays on the bed, and laughter fills the room.
### 起床 → 床 → 广(廣)
- **traditional:** 廣
- **definition:** house
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 廣
    - guǎng
    - broad
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广(廣) (guǎng, "broad") + phonetic 黃 (huáng, "yellow") ->
    - broad
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, "broad") combines the semantic element 广(廣), depicting a broad area or structure, with the phonetic element 黃 (huáng), which lends its sound. This combination signifies the idea of something wide or expansive.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by removing the 黃 (huáng, "yellow") phonetic component, leaving only the semantic element.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)条(條)河非常广(廣)阔(闊)。
    - Zhè tiáo hé fēicháng guǎngkuò.
    - This river is very broad.
  - 他的知识(識)面很广(廣)，总(總)是能解决(決)问(問)题(題)。
    - Tā de zhīshì miàn hěn guǎng, zǒng shì néng jiějué wèntí.
    - His knowledge is broad, and he is always able to solve problems.
  - 在学(學)校里(裡)，他参(參)加了许(許)多广(廣)泛的活动(動)。
    - Zài xuéxiào lǐ, tā cānjiāle xǔduō guǎngfàn de huódòng.
    - At school, he participated in many broad activities.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 广](@media/glyph5e7f.png)
### 起床 → 床 → 广(廣) → 廣
- **definition:** broad
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 广
    - guǎng
    - roof; shelter
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 (roof; shelter) + phonetic 黃 (huáng, sound) ->
    - shelter
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, 'shelter') combines the semantic component 广, which suggests the idea of covering or enclosure like a roof, with the phonetic component 黃 (huáng). The enclosure aspect of 广 underlines the meaning of providing shelter or an expansive space.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by retaining the roof radical but removing 黃, simplifying the structure considerably.
- **examples:**
  - 我们正在寻找一个可以提供广(廣)的地方。
    - Wǒmen zhèngzài xúnzhǎo yī gè kěyǐ tígōng guǎng de dìfāng.
    - We are looking for a place that can provide shelter.
  - 那里的广(廣)设施非常完善，适合长时间停留。
    - Nàlǐ de guǎng shèshī fēicháng wánshàn, shìhé cháng shíjiān tíngliú.
    - The shelter facilities there are very complete, suitable for long stays.
  - 如果有恶劣天气，我们需要一个广(廣)来保护自己。
    - Rúguǒ yǒu èliè tiānqì, wǒmen xūyào yī gè guǎng lái bǎohù zìjǐ.
    - If there is bad weather, we need a shelter to protect ourselves.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廣](@media/glyph5ee3.png)
### 起床 → 床 → 广(廣) → 廣 → 黃
- **definition:** yellow
- **pinyin:** huáng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally a pictogram depicting a disabled person or man with a ring of jade on the chest ->
    - phonetically borrowed for 'yellow' ->
    - 黃
  - **interpretation:** The character 黃 (huáng, 'yellow') originated from a pictogram representing either a disabled person or a man with a jade ring, showing a connection to cultural rituals or symbols of status. It was later phonetically borrowed to represent the color 'yellow' without semantic connection to its original depiction. In modern Chinese, its primary use is to denote the color yellow, disconnecting entirely from its debated pictographic origins.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)朵花是黄(黃)色的。
    - Zhè duǒ huā shì huángsè de.
    - This flower is yellow.
  - 秋天来(來)临(臨)时(時)，树(樹)叶(葉)变(變)成金黄(黃)色。
    - Qiūtiān láilín shí, shùyè biàn chéng jīnhuáng sè.
    - When autumn arrives, the leaves turn golden yellow.
  - 他穿了一件黄(黃)色的外套。
    - Tā chuānle yī jiàn huángsè de wàitào.
    - He wore a yellow jacket.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 黃](@media/glyph9ec3.png)
### 起床 → 床 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)

## 酒单(單)
---
## drinks menu
### jiǔ dān
---
- **traditional:** 酒單
- **definition:** drinks menu
- **pinyin:** jiǔ dān
- **components:**
  - 酒
    - jiǔ
    - alcohol; liquor; spirits; wine
  - 单(單)
    - dān
    - list; bill; form; single
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 酒 (jiǔ, "alcohol") refers to alcoholic beverages in general. 單 (dān, "list") signifies a list or menu of items.
  - **interpretation:** 酒 (jiǔ, "alcohol") names the main content of interest, while 單 (dān, "list") provides the format, resulting in a 'drinks menu' — a list specifically for alcoholic beverages.
- **examples:**
  - 我想看看酒单(單)。
    - Wǒ xiǎng kàn kàn jiǔ dān.
    - I would like to see the drinks menu.
  - 酒单(單)上有很多选(選)择(擇)。
    - Jiǔ dān shàng yǒu hěn duō xuǎnzé.
    - There are many options on the drinks menu.
  - 我们(們)决(決)定从(從)酒单(單)上点(點)红(紅)酒。
    - Wǒmen juédìng cóng jiǔ dān shàng diǎn hóngjiǔ.
    - We decided to order red wine from the drinks menu.
### 酒单(單) → 酒
- **definition:** alcohol; liquor; spirits; wine
- **pinyin:** jiǔ
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 酉
    - yǒu
    - complete cycle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 氵 (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic: 酉 (yǒu, "complete cycle") =
    - a liquid associated with 酉 (fermentation/vessels) ->
    - alcohol
  - **interpretation:** The character 酒 (jiǔ, "alcohol") uses 氵 (shuǐ, "water") to indicate a liquid, and 酉 (yǒu, "complete cycle") to suggest fermentation or storage vessels, representing alcoholic beverages.
- **examples:**
  - 他喝了太多酒。
    - Tā hēle tài duō jiǔ.
    - He drank too much alcohol.
  - 夜深人静(靜)时(時)，他独(獨)自品酒。
    - Yè shēn rén jìng shí, tā dúzì pǐn jiǔ.
    - In the quiet of the night, he savored his drink alone.
  - 那杯香醇的酒，令他回味无(無)穷(窮)。
    - Nà bēi xiāngchún de jiǔ, lìng tā huíwèi wúqióng.
    - That glass of aromatic alcohol left him with an unforgettable aftertaste.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 酒](@media/glyph9152.png)
### 酒单(單) → 酒 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字中偏旁氵，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快戏(戲)水。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 酒单(單) → 酒 → 酉
- **definition:** complete cycle
- **pinyin:** yǒu
- **components:**
  - 酒
    - jiǔ
    - alcohol
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a wine vessel with a pointed bottom ->
    - original character for 酒 (jiǔ, "alcohol")
  - **interpretation:** 酉 (yǒu, "complete cycle") originally depicted a wine vessel, indicating the integral role of alcohol in traditional cycles, such as moon phases or ceremonial events. It is the original character for 酒 (jiǔ, "alcohol"), highlighting its use in fermentation processes.
- **examples:**
  - 每一次回望旧(舊)地，都仿(彷)佛(彿)见(見)证(證)了一个(個)酉的完结(結)。
    - Měi yīcì huíwàng jiùdì, dōu fǎngfú jiànzhèngle yīgè yǒu de wánjié.
    - Every time I look back, it seems to witness a complete cycle coming to an end.
  - 日落黄(黃)昏后(後)，大地经(經)历(歷)了一个(個)酉的循环(環)。
    - Rìluò huánghūn hòu, dàdì jīnglìle yīgè yǒu de xúnhuán.
    - After sunset, the land has undergone a complete cycle.
### 酒单(單) → 单(單)
- **traditional:** 單
- **definition:** list; bill; form; single
- **pinyin:** dān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Y-shaped wooden stick with stones ->
    - hunting or war weapon ->
    - resemblance to 中 ->
    - stylized to 田
  - **interpretation:** Initially depicting a Y-shaped weapon with stones suggesting a hunting tool, the character evolved visually, resembling a pole or stick (中), later taking a form similar to 田. This innovative stylization reveals its original purpose as a practical tool for warfare or hunting, thereby informing its association with tasks and lists in the modern sense.
  - **simplification:** 单(單): The character was simplified by removing the complex elements within 田, reducing it to a more direct form that still suggests the idea of a singular, straightforward entity akin to a list.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)给(給)我一张(張)清单(單)。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī zhāng qīngdān.
    - Please give me a list.
  - 他列出了需要购(購)买(買)的物品清单(單)。
    - Tā liè chūle xūyào gòumǎi de wùpǐn qīngdān.
    - He made a list of items to purchase.
  - 她准(準)备(備)了一份客人的名单(單)。
    - Tā zhǔnbèi le yī fèn kèrén de míngdān.
    - She prepared a list of guests.

## 金竹果

## jinzhu fruit
### jīn zhú guǒ
---
- **definition:** jinzhu fruit
- **pinyin:** jīn zhú guǒ
- **components:**
  - 金
    - jīn
    - gold; metal
  - 竹果
    - zhú guǒ
    - jinzhu fruit
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** The word 金竹果 (jīn zhú guǒ) combines references to color, form, and nature. 金 (jīn, "gold") indicates a golden color; 竹果 (zhú guǒ, "jinzhu fruit") refers directly to a specific fruit, though details about it might be more colloquial or regional knowledge.
  - **interpretation:** 金 (jīn, "gold") suggests the golden color of the fruit, possibly its appearance or value. The term 竹果 (zhú guǒ, "jinzhu fruit") is a direct reference to a specific fruit; however, in this context, it serves primarily to name the fruit rather than describe it.
### 金竹果 → 金
- **definition:** gold; metal
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 士
    - shì
    - upside-down ritual axe
  - 呂
    - lǚ
    - two blocks of metal
  - 亼
    - jí
    - open mouth upside down
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 士 (upside-down ritual axe) + 呂 (two blocks of metal) + phonetic 亼 (open mouth upside down) ->
    - original pronunciation; no earth pictogram in ancient forms ->
    - metal, later gold
  - **interpretation:** Initially representing copper, due to its use in the Copper Age, the character 金 (jīn, "metal") evolved to refer broadly to metal as technological progress made various metals crucial in society. The extension to gold reflects its value and prominence. The phonetic 亼 indicates the character's pronunciation, with semantic elements showing early associations with precious materials.
- **examples:**
  - 金是一种(種)重要的工业(業)原料。
    - Jīn shì yī zhǒng zhòngyào de gōngyè yuánliào.
    - Metal is an important industrial material.
  - 她的项(項)链(鍊)是纯(純)金的。
    - Tā de xiàngliàn shì chún jīn de.
    - Her necklace is made of pure gold.
  - 每个(個)国(國)家都有自己的金矿(礦)。
    - Měi gè guójiā dōu yǒu zìjǐ de jīnkuàng.
    - Every country has its own gold mines.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 金](@media/glyph91d1.png)
### 金竹果 → 金 → 士
- **definition:** upside-down ritual axe
- **pinyin:** shì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a ritual axe, possibly made of jade ->
    - symbolized soldier ->
    - intellectual or officer over time
  - **interpretation:** The character 士(shì, 'scholar') originally depicted a ritual axe used in ceremonies, implying a person of a certain rank or status who could wield such symbols. This connection to ceremonial authority evolved to mean 'soldier' and later 'intellectual' or 'officer', roles associated with leadership and knowledge in societal hierarchies.
- **examples:**
  - 历(歷)史上，士被视(視)为(為)一种(種)权(權)力的象征(徵)。
    - Lìshǐ shàng, shì bèi shì wéi yī zhǒng quánlì de xiàngzhēng.
    - Historically, the 'shi' was seen as a symbol of power.
  - 在古代，只有贵(貴)族才拥(擁)有士。
    - Zài gǔdài, zhǐyǒu guìzú cái yǒngyǒu shì.
    - In ancient times, only nobles possessed the 'shi'.
  - 士的制(製)作材料可能是珍贵(貴)的金属(屬)。
    - Shì de zhìzuò cáiliào kěnéng shì zhēnguì de jīnshǔ.
    - The materials used to make the 'shi' might have been precious metals.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 士](@media/glyph58eb.png)
### 金竹果 → 金 → 呂
- **definition:** two blocks of metal
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two disconnected blocks of metal, later connected in seal script ->
    - Original form of 鋁 (lǚ, 'ingot') ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'spine' and 'music notes'
  - **interpretation:** The character 呂(lǚ) ('two blocks of metal') visually represents two separate blocks aligned vertically. In its earliest forms, these blocks were disconnected, symbolizing distinct metal segments, which aligns with its early use for 'ingot'. Over time, as seen in seal script, a connecting line was added to form the modern appearance. This visual interpretation supports its original meaning related to metal. It was later phonetically borrowed to convey concepts like 'spine' and 'music notes', where no direct semantic link exists with metal, but the sound similarity allowed its reuse in these contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 他用两(兩)个(個)大的金属(屬)块(塊)铸(鑄)造了一个(個)雕像。
    - Tā yòng liǎng gè dà de jīnshǔ kuài zhùzào le yī gè diāoxiàng.
    - He cast a statue using two large blocks of metal.
  - 现(現)代工业(業)中，金属(屬)块(塊)常用于(於)制(製)造重型设(設)备(備)。
    - Xiàndài gōngyè zhōng, jīnshǔ kuài cháng yòng yú zhìzào zhòngxíng shèbèi.
    - In modern industry, metal blocks are often used for manufacturing heavy equipment.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)师(師)用金属(屬)块(塊)建造了一个(個)现(現)代化建筑(築)。
    - Zhège shèjì shī yòng jīnshǔ kuài jiànzào le yī gè xiàndàihuà jiànzhù.
    - The designer built a modern structure using metal blocks.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 呂](@media/glyph5442.png)
### 金竹果 → 金 → 亼
- **definition:** open mouth upside down
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 金竹果 → 金 → 亼 → 入
- **definition:** enter
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入座。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生走入校园(園)，开(開)始新学(學)期。
    - Xuéshēng zǒu rù xiàoyuán, kāishǐ xīn xuéqī.
    - The students enter the campus and start a new semester.
  - 游(遊)客走入古城，探索历(歷)史。
    - Yóukè zǒu rù gǔchéng, tànsuǒ lìshǐ.
    - The tourists enter the ancient city and explore its history.

### 金竹果 → 金 → 亼 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

### 金竹果 → 金 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今天的天气(氣)不错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在是吃晚饭(飯)的时(時)候。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她今天特别(別)忙，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 金竹果 → 金 → 亼 → 今 → 曰
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)曰：勤奋(奮)是成功之母。
    - Lǎoshī yuē：qínfèn shì chénggōng zhī mǔ。
    - The teacher said, 'Diligence is the mother of success.'
  - 孔子曰，学(學)而不思则(則)罔。
    - Kǒngzǐ yuē, xué ér bù sī zé wǎng。
    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无(無)为(為)而治。
    - Lǎozǐ yuē, wúwéi ér zhì。
    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'

### 金竹果 → 竹果
- **definition:** jinzhu fruit
- **pinyin:** zhú guǒ
- **components:**
  - 竜
    - zhú
    - pipal tree
  - 果
    - guǒ
    - fruit
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 竜 (zhú, "pipal tree") + 果 (guǒ, "fruit") =
    - refers to the fruit known as jinzhu. The word combines the concept of a specific type of tree with the idea of its fruit, indicating a product that comes from the pipal tree, commonly referred to as jinzhu fruit.
  - **interpretation:** 竜 (zhú, "pipal tree") represents the type of tree associated with the jinzhu fruit, hinting at its significance or origin. 果 (guǒ, "fruit") indicates it is the fruit of this particular tree, creating a specific botanical reference.
### 金竹果 → 竹果 → 竜
- **definition:** pipal tree
- **pinyin:** zhú
- **components:**
  - 龍
    - lóng
    - dragon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Ancient form of 龍 (lóng, "dragon") used in Japan ->
    - recorded in early Chinese dictionaries resembling a stylized dragon form, incorporating mythical creature imagery
  - **interpretation:** The character 竜 (lóng, "dragon") is used in Japan and stylistically represents the ancient depiction of a dragon, a sacred composite creature in Chinese culture. This depiction included elements resembling snakes, crocodiles, and other animals, embodying divine and powerful symbolism.
- **examples:**
  - 竜在古代被认(認)为(為)是神圣(聖)的树(樹)。
    - Zhú zài gǔdài bèi rènwéi shì shénshèng de shù.
    - The pipal tree was considered a sacred tree in ancient times.
  - 在热(熱)带(帶)地区(區)，竜常常被用作遮阳(陽)树(樹)。
    - Zài rèdài dìqū, zhú chángcháng bèi yòng zuò zhēyáng shù.
    - In tropical regions, the pipal tree is often used as a shade tree.
  - 很多人认(認)为(為)在竜下冥想可以增强(強)精神力量。
    - Hěnduō rén rènwéi zài zhú xià míngxiǎng kěyǐ zēngqiáng jīngshén lìliàng.
    - Many people believe that meditating under a pipal tree can enhance spiritual strength.
### 金竹果 → 竹果 → 竜 → 龍
- **definition:** dragon
- **pinyin:** lóng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a sacred composite creature with features of snake, crocodile, fish, deer, etc. ->
    - Large-mouthed beast head, S-shaped body, possibly scale-like patterns ->
    - Head ornament elements resemble antlers or clan emblems ->
    - Evolved into separate head (left) and body (right) parts in writing
  - **interpretation:** The character 龍 (lóng, 'dragon') is a pictogram representing a mythical creature combining attributes like scales, a beast head, and an elongated body. Its depiction included antler-like ornaments or clan symbols, suggesting its status as a sacred animal in ancient China. The evolution of the character involved separating the head and body elements, reflecting practical adaptations in script forms over time.
- **examples:**
  - 在中国(國)文化中，龙(龍)象征(徵)着(著)权(權)力和幸运(運)。
    - Zài Zhōngguó wénhuà zhōng, lóng xiàngzhēng zhe quánlì hé xìngyùn.
    - In Chinese culture, the dragon symbolizes power and luck.
  - 龙(龍)年被认(認)为(為)是特别(別)吉祥的一年。
    - Lóngnián bèi rènwéi shì tèbié jíxiáng de yī nián.
    - The Year of the Dragon is considered especially auspicious.
  - 传(傳)说(說)中的龙(龍)能够(夠)呼风(風)唤(喚)雨。
    - Chuánshuō zhōng de lóng nénggòu hū fēng huàn yǔ.
    - Legendary dragons have the ability to call forth wind and rain.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 龍](@media/glyph9f8d.png)
### 金竹果 → 竹果 → 果
- **definition:** fruit
- **pinyin:** guǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts fruits on a tree
  - **interpretation:** The character 果 (guǒ) vividly depicts fruits hanging from a tree, encapsulating the concrete image of a tree bearing fruit, which directly leads to the meaning of 'fruit.' The tree and the fruit form an intuitive visual association with the concept of bearing or producing fruits.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)吃苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī píngguǒ.
    - I like to eat apples.
  - 这(這)个(個)果汁很新鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhège guǒzhī hěn xīnxiān.
    - This juice is very fresh.
  - 水果摊(攤)上有很多种(種)类(類)的水果。
    - Shuǐguǒ tān shàng yǒu hěnduō zhǒnglèi de shuǐguǒ.
    - There are many varieties of fruit at the fruit stand.
- **historical forms:**

## 鼓楼(樓)
---
## drum tower
### gǔ lóu
---
- **traditional:** 鼓樓
- **definition:** drum tower
- **pinyin:** gǔ lóu
- **components:**
  - 鼓
    - gǔ
    - drum
  - 楼(樓)
    - lóu
    - tower; building with multiple floors
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 鼓 (gǔ, "drum") + 楼(樓) (lóu, "tower") refers to a traditional structure often found in Chinese cities, where drums were used to signal time or events.
  - **interpretation:** A 鼓 (gǔ, "drum") is placed in a 楼(樓) (lóu, "tower") and used to signal time in ancient China. Drum towers were central to city life, serving as public timekeepers and ceremonial spaces.
  - **simplification:** 楼 is simplified from 樓
- **examples:**
  - 到北京旅游一定要去看看鼓楼(樓)。
    - Dào Běijīng lǚyóu yīdìng yào qù kànkàn gǔ lóu.
    - When traveling to Beijing, you must visit the Drum Tower.
  - 傍晚时(時)分，鼓楼(樓)散发(發)出古老的韵(韻)味。
    - Bàngwǎn shí fēn, gǔ lóu sànfā chū gǔlǎo de yùnwèi.
    - In the evening, the Drum Tower exudes an ancient charm.
### 鼓楼(樓) → 鼓
- **definition:** drum
- **pinyin:** gǔ
- **components:**
  - 壴
    - zhù
    - drum
  - 支
    - zhī
    - hand holding drumstick
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 壴 (zhù, "drum") + 支 (zhī, "hand holding drumstick") =
    - drum being played ->
    - drum
  - **interpretation:** The character 鼓(gǔ) combines a depiction of a drum 壴 with a hand holding a drumstick 支. This intuitive combination directly represents the act of drumming.
- **examples:**
  - 他敲鼓。
    - Tā qiāo gǔ.
    - He beats the drum.
  - 音乐(樂)会(會)开(開)始时(時)，乐(樂)手敲鼓。
    - Yīnyuèhuì kāishǐ shí, yuèshǒu qiāo gǔ.
    - When the concert begins, the musician beats the drum.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 鼓](@media/glyph9f13.png)
### 鼓楼(樓) → 鼓 → 壴
- **definition:** drum
- **pinyin:** zhù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a drum 壴, with a base and feathers 土 on top ->
    - stylized in the Kangxi radical 鼓
  - **interpretation:** The character 壴 (zhù, "drum") visually represents a drum with two ends, with elements contributing to its structure, such as a base and feathers. It was later incorporated into characters like 鼓 (gǔ, "drum") by adding elements that illustrate additional actions like hands holding a drumstick.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)面壴声(聲)震天动(動)地。
    - Zhè miàn zhù shēng zhèn tiān dòng dì.
    - The sound of this drum shakes the heavens and the earth.
  - 战(戰)士敲响(響)壴，示警敌(敵)人。
    - Zhànshì qiāo xiǎng zhù, shì jǐng dírén.
    - The soldier beats the drum to warn the enemy.
  - 庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式上，祭司击(擊)打壴，宣告传(傳)统(統)。
    - Zhuāngyán yíshì shàng, jìsī jī dǎ zhù, xuānguò chuántǒng.
    - At the solemn ceremony, the priest beats the drum to proclaim tradition.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 壴](@media/glyph58f4.png)
### 鼓楼(樓) → 鼓 → 支
- **definition:** hand holding drumstick
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand holding a drumstick
  - **interpretation:** The character 支 (zhī, 'hand holding drumstick') visually represents a hand grasping a stick-like object, suggesting support or physical action, which aligns with its meanings related to branching or supporting.
- **examples:**
  - 他支鼓槌，敲响(響)大鼓。
    - Tā zhī gǔchuí, qiāo xiǎng dà gǔ.
    - He holds the drumstick and strikes the big drum.
  - 鼓手支着(著)鼓槌，打出动(動)人节(節)奏。
    - Gǔshǒu zhī zhe gǔchuí, dǎ chū dòngrén jiézòu.
    - The drummer holds the drumstick and produces a captivating rhythm.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 支](@media/glyph652f.png)
### 鼓楼(樓) → 楼(樓)
- **traditional:** 樓
- **definition:** tower; building with multiple floors
- **pinyin:** lóu
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 婁
    - lóu
    - a constellation; tangle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, 'tree') + phonetic 婁 (lóu) ->
    - building/structure made of wood
  - **interpretation:** The character 樓(lóu) represents a 'building with multiple floors'. The semantic component 木 (mù, 'tree') suggests a structure made of wood, referring to traditional building materials. The phonetic component 婁 (lóu) provides the pronunciation without contributing directly to the meaning.
  - **simplification:** Simplified as 楼 by replacing the complex phonetic 婁 with its simplified form 娄(婁).
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)座楼(樓)非常高。
    - Zhè zuò lóu fēicháng gāo.
    - This building is very tall.
  - 学(學)校后(後)面有一栋(棟)新楼(樓)。
    - Xuéxiào hòumiàn yǒu yī dòng xīn lóu.
    - There is a new building behind the school.
  - 他住在五楼(樓)，每天都要爬楼(樓)梯。
    - Tā zhù zài wǔ lóu, měitiān dōu yào pá lóutī.
    - He lives on the fifth floor and has to climb the stairs every day.
### 鼓楼(樓) → 楼(樓) → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 鼓楼(樓) → 楼(樓) → 婁
- **definition:** a constellation; tangle
- **pinyin:** lóu
- **components:**
  - 爪
    - zhǎo
    - hands
  - 角
    - jiǎo
    - horn
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 母
    - mǔ
    - mother
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Original: 爪(爪, "hands") + 角(角, "horn") + 女(女, "woman") ->
    - Later form: 母(母, "mother") + 中 + 女(女, "daughter")
  - **interpretation:** The character 婁(lóu) likely originated as a phono-semantic compound, combining 爪(爪, "hands") to depict manipulation or bundling, with the phonetic support of 角, and 女(女, "woman") as another semantic component. Over time, its representation evolved into an ideogrammic compound with 母(母, "mother"), 中 suggesting centrality or encompassing, and 女(女, "daughter"), potentially symbolizing the concept of bringing things together or bundling, which fits its meaning as 'bundle'.
### 鼓楼(樓) → 楼(樓) → 婁 → 爪
- **definition:** hands
- **pinyin:** zhǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand grabbing from above, resembles a claw ->
    - stylized to represent claws
  - **interpretation:** The character 爪 (zhǎo, "claw") originally depicted a hand grabbing from above, stylized to resemble the form of claws.
- **examples:**
  - 猫(貓)的爪非常敏捷。
    - Māo de zhǎo fēicháng mǐnjié.
    - The cat's claws are very agile.
  - 狗的爪稳(穩)固，使它轻(輕)松(鬆)爬山。
    - Gǒu de zhǎo wěngù, shǐ tā qīngsōng páshān.
    - The dog's claws are sturdy, allowing it to climb mountains easily.
  - 鹰(鷹)的爪锋(鋒)利，能牢牢抓住猎(獵)物。
    - Yīng de zhǎo fēnglì, néng láoláo zhuā zhù lièwù.
    - The eagle's claws are sharp, enabling it to firmly grasp its prey.
- **historical forms:**

### 鼓楼(樓) → 楼(樓) → 婁 → 角
- **definition:** horn
- **pinyin:** jiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an animal horn
  - **interpretation:** The character 角 (jiǎo, "horn") visually represents the distinctive shape of an animal's horn.
- **examples:**
  - 牛角是一种(種)坚(堅)固的天然武器。
    - niú jiǎo shì yī zhǒng jiān gù de tiān rán wǔ qì。
    - Cow horns are sturdy natural weapons.
  - 鹿角丰(豐)富了森林的传(傳)说(說)，象征(徵)着(著)自由与(與)力量。
    - lù jiǎo fēng fù le sēn lín de chuán shuō, xiàng zhēng zhe zì yóu yǔ lì liàng。
    - Deer antlers enrich the legends of the forest and symbolize freedom and strength.
  - 犀牛角在古代被视(視)作珍贵(貴)药(藥)材。
    - xī niú jiǎo zài gǔ dài bèi shì zuò zhēn guì yào cái。

### 鼓楼(樓) → 楼(樓) → 婁 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 女](@media/glyph5973.png)
### 鼓楼(樓) → 楼(樓) → 婁 → 母
- **definition:** mother
- **pinyin:** mǔ
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** differentiated form
  - **description:**
    - 女 (nǚ, "woman") + addition of two dots ->
    - distinguished as 母 (mǔ, "mother")
  - **interpretation:** The character 母 (mǔ, "mother") is a differentiated form of 女 (nǚ, "woman") with the addition of two dots to distinguish it. In early script forms, both 母 (mǔ, "mother") and 女 (nǚ, "woman") were represented by the same form as 女, necessitating the addition of dots to create a visual distinction. The character 毋, originally borrowed from 母, further specialized by changing the dots to a stroke to avoid confusion between the characters.
- **examples:**
  - 母给(給)了我无(無)限的温(溫)暖。
    - mǔ gěi le wǒ wúxiàn de wēnnuǎn
    - Mother has given me endless warmth.
  - 我的母温(溫)柔而坚(堅)毅，培养(養)了我良好的品格。
    - wǒ de mǔ wēnróu ér jiānyì, péiyǎng le wǒ liánghǎo de pǐngé
    - My mother is gentle and strong, nurturing my good character.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 母](@media/glyph6bcd.png)
### 鼓楼(樓) → 楼(樓) → 婁 → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)

## 同城
---
## Chinese online classifieds platform
### Wǔ Bā Tóngchéng
---
- **definition:** Chinese online classifieds platform
- **pinyin:** Wǔ Bā Tóngchéng
- **components:**
  - 同
    - tóng
    - same; together
  - 城
    - chéng
    - city; town
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 同 (tóng, "same; together") signifies unity or being alike, while 城 (chéng, "city") refers to a town or urban area. Combined, 同城 (tóngchéng) intuitively represents 'within the same city', suggesting locality or community.
  - **interpretation:** 同 (tóng, "same; together") evokes the idea of uniformity or being in unison. 城 (chéng, "city") conveys the physical space of an urban area. Thus, the combination refers to the concept of being in the same urban space, highlighting a shared locality or community context.
- **examples:**
  - 我在同城网(網)上找到了一个好工作。
    - Wǒ zài Tóngchéng wǎng shàng zhǎodào le yī gè hǎo gōngzuò.
    - I found a good job on the 58.com site.
  - 同城平台提供了许(許)多租房信息。
    - Tóngchéng píngtái tígōng le xǔduō zūfáng xìnxī.
    - The 58.com platform provides a lot of rental information.
  - 我们(們)利用同城发(發)布了二手物品的广(廣)告。
    - Wǒmen lìyòng Tóngchéng fābù le èrshǒu wùpǐn de guǎnggào.
    - We used 58.com to post advertisements for second-hand items.
### 同城 → 同
- **definition:** same; together
- **pinyin:** tóng
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - "mouth"
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally depicted as a pipe 筒 (tǒng, "pipe") ->
    - 口 added as decoration ->
    - interpreted as mouth 口 (kǒu, "mouth") giving orders ->
    - evolved to mean togetherness and unity
  - **interpretation:** The character 同 (tóng, "same; unity; together; common") originally depicted a pipe but later took on the symbolic meaning of unity, possibly influenced by the shared cooperation in activities like music or rigid group tasks. The addition of 口 (kǒu, "mouth") emphasizes communication and collaboration.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)同心协(協)力。
    - Wǒmen tóngxīn xiélì.
    - We work together with one heart and mind.
  - 他们(們)穿着(著)同款衣服，看起来(來)十分整齐(齊)。
    - Tāmen chuānzhe tóng kuǎn yīfú, kàn qǐlái shífēn zhěngqí.
    - They are wearing the same style of clothes and look very orderly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 同](@media/glyph540c.png)
### 同城 → 同 → 口
- **definition:** "mouth"
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 同城 → 城
- **definition:** city; town
- **pinyin:** chéng
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - soil
  - 成
    - chéng
    - complete
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 土 (tǔ, "soil") + phonetic 成 (chéng, "complete") =
    - city walls made of stamped earth ->
    - wall; city wall
  - **interpretation:** The character 城 (chéng, "wall; city wall") combines the meaning of 土 (tǔ, "soil") with the sound of 成 (chéng, "complete"), reflecting the construction of city walls using compacted earth.
- **examples:**
  - 城外有护(護)城河，城内(內)居住百姓。
    - Chéng wài yǒu hùchénghé, chéng nèi jūzhù bǎixìng。
    - Outside the city wall there is a moat, and inside the city wall many people live.
  - 古城历(歷)经(經)岁(歲)月。
    - Gǔ chéng lìjīng suìyuè。
    - The ancient city wall has endured the passage of time.
  - 高耸(聳)的城令敌(敵)人畏惧(懼)。
    - Gāosǒng de chéng lìng dírén wèijù。
    - The towering city wall strikes fear into the hearts of enemies.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 城](@media/glyph57ce.png)
### 同城 → 城 → 土
- **definition:** soil
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院子里(裡)的土，适(適)合种(種)花。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.

### 同城 → 城 → 成
- **definition:** complete
- **pinyin:** chéng
- **components:**
  - 戊
    - wù
    - weapon
  - 丁
    - dīng
    - fourth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 戊 (depicts a weapon) + phonetic 丁 (sound) ->
    - meaning related to protection or completion
  - **interpretation:** Originally related to 'city walls', protected by a weapon (戊), which conveys the idea of completeness or fortification. The sound provided by 丁 reinforces this association. This concept of protection leads to the general sense of something being complete or finished.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)本书(書)终(終)于(於)写(寫)成了。
    - Zhè běn shū zhōngyú xiě chéng le.
    - This book is finally completed.
  - 他成功地解决(決)了这(這)个(個)问(問)题(題)。
    - Tā chénggōng de jiějué le zhège wèntí.
    - He successfully solved this problem.
  - 我的梦(夢)想是成为(為)一名医(醫)生。
    - Wǒ de mèngxiǎng shì chéngwéi yī míng yīshēng.
    - My dream is to become a doctor.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 成](@media/glyph6210.png)
### 同城 → 城 → 成 → 戊
- **definition:** weapon
- **pinyin:** wù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a halberd.
  - **interpretation:** The character 戊(wù, "weapon") depicts a halberd, which is a traditional Chinese pole weapon with an axe blade and spike. Originally, the character visually represented the weapon and was used to denote its image and function in ancient contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 戊是古代军(軍)队(隊)的重要装(裝)备(備)。
    - Wù shì gǔdài jūnduì de zhòngyào zhuāngbèi.
    - Weapons were essential equipment for ancient armies.
  - 随(隨)着(著)科技的发(發)展，现(現)代戊的种(種)类(類)越来(來)越多。
    - Suízhe kējì de fāzhǎn, xiàndài wù de zhǒnglèi yuèláiyuè duō.
    - With the development of technology, the varieties of modern weapons have increased.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 戊](@media/glyph620a.png)
### 同城 → 城 → 成 → 丁
- **definition:** fourth
- **pinyin:** dīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of a nail ->
    - 丁
  - **interpretation:** The character 丁 originally depicted the head of a nail, emphasizing simplicity and directness. While it has developed other interpretations over time, such as a head or city wall, these relate to similar shapes and functions. Today, 釘 (dīng, 'nail') reflects this meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 工人熟练(練)地把丁敲进(進)了墙(牆)壁。
    - Gōngrén shúliàn de bǎ dīng qiāng jìnle qiángbì.
    - The worker skillfully hammered the nail into the wall.
  - 他精心挑选(選)了铁(鐵)质(質)丁，确(確)保家(傢)具(俱)稳(穩)固。
    - Tā jīngxīn tiāoxuǎnle tiě zhì dīng, quèbǎo jiājù wěngù.
    - He carefully selected the iron nail to ensure the furniture was stable.
  - 请(請)把散落的丁收好。
    - Qǐng bǎ sànluò de dīng shōuhǎo.
    - Please gather the scattered nails.
- **historical forms:**

## 买(買)完了
---
## finished buying
### mǎi wán le
---
- **traditional:** 買完了
- **definition:** finished buying
- **pinyin:** mǎi wán le
- **components:**
  - 买(買)
    - mǎi
    - buy
  - 完
    - wán
    - finish; complete
  - 了
    - le
    - completed action; particle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 買 (mǎi, "buy") + 完 (wán, "finish") + 了 (le, "completed action") combine to express the completion of a buying action.
  - **interpretation:** 買 (mǎi, "buy") indicates the action of purchasing goods, while 完 (wán, "finish") suggests that the action reaches its end. 了 (le, "completed action") is a particle that marks the completion, indicating finality.
- **examples:**
  - 她买(買)完了食材。
    - Tā mǎi wán le shícái.
    - She finished buying groceries.
  - 我已经(經)买(買)完了所有需要的东(東)西。
    - Wǒ yǐjīng mǎi wán le suǒyǒu xūyào de dōngxī.
    - I have finished buying everything I need.
  - 他们(們)不久前就买(買)完了票。
    - Tāmen bùjiǔ qián jiù mǎi wán le piào.
    - They finished buying the tickets shortly ago.
### 买(買)完了 → 买(買)
- **traditional:** 買
- **definition:** buy
- **pinyin:** mǎi
- **components:**
  - 网(網)
    - wǎng
    - net
  - 貝
    - bèi
    - money cowrie
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 网 (wǎng, "net") + 貝 (bèi, "money cowrie") =
    - capturing with a net and valuables ->
    - buy
  - **interpretation:** The traditional character 買 (mǎi, "buy") depicts a net used to capture valuable items, represented by the cowrie shell, indicating the exchange process of purchasing. This combines physical capture with the notion of economic transaction, effectively illustrating the concept of buying.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 買 (mǎi, "buy") was simplified to 买(買) by removing the 财(財) (cái, "wealth") radical and using a modified net component.
- **examples:**
  - 我去超市，买(買)水果。
    - Wǒ qù chāoshì, mǎi shuǐguǒ.
    - I go to the supermarket to buy fruits.
  - 她想买(買)新衣服。
    - Tā xiǎng mǎi xīn yīfú.
    - She wants to buy new clothes.
  - 他们(們)准(準)备(備)买(買)票，去看电(電)影。
    - Tāmen zhǔnbèi mǎi piào, qù kàn diànyǐng.
    - They are ready to buy tickets to go watch a movie.
### 买(買)完了 → 买(買) → 网(網)
- **traditional:** 網
- **definition:** net
- **pinyin:** wǎng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a net with crossing lines or mesh ->
    - symbol for 'net'
  - **interpretation:** The character 网(網) (wǎng, 'net') visually represents a net with lines intersecting to form a grid, making it intuitive as a symbol for a net or mesh.
  - **simplification:** The simplified character 网 (wǎng) retains the essential visual structure of intersecting lines to depict a net. It conveys the idea of a net through a simplified representation without additional semantic or phonetic elements.
- **examples:**
  - 他用网(網)捕鱼(魚)，快乐(樂)满(滿)怀(懷)。
    - Tā yòng wǎng bǔ yú, kuàilè mǎn huái.
    - He fishes with a net and is full of joy.
  - 很多信息通过(過)网(網)传(傳)播，速度惊(驚)人。
    - Hěn duō xìnxī tōngguò wǎng chuánbō, sùdù jīngrén.
    - A lot of information spreads through the net with astonishing speed.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 网](@media/glyph7f51.png)
### 买(買)完了 → 买(買) → 貝
- **definition:** money cowrie
- **pinyin:** bèi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cowrie shell ->
    - used as currency in ancient China ->
    - stylized as 貝
  - **interpretation:** The character 貝(bèi, 'shell/money') visually represents a cowrie shell, which was used as a form of currency in ancient China. This explains why it is associated with money or valuables.
  - **simplification:** 贝 is a cursive script simplification of 貝, transforming the character into a more streamlined form while retaining its essence.
- **examples:**
  - 他把贝(貝)当作护(護)身符，放在口袋里(裡)。
    - Tā bǎ bèi dāng zuò hùshēn fú, fàng zài kǒudài lǐ.
    - He uses shells as a talisman, placing them in his pocket.
  - 古代人用贝(貝)作为(為)货(貨)币(幣)。
    - Gǔdài rén yòng bèi zuòwéi huòbì.
    - In ancient times, people used shells as currency.
### 买(買)完了 → 完
- **definition:** finish; complete
- **pinyin:** wán
- **components:**
  - 宀
    - mián
    - roof
  - 元
    - yuán
    - origin
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 宀 (roof) + phonetic 元 (sound) ->
    - finished; intact
  - **interpretation:** The character 完 (wán, "finished; intact") combines the semantic element 宀 (mián, "roof"), suggesting a protective or structural component, and the phonetic element 元 (yuán, "origin"), indicating the pronunciation. Together, they imply a structure that is completed and covered, hence the sense of something being "finished" or "intact."
- **examples:**
  - 他终(終)于(於)完成任务(務)了。
    - Tā zhōngyú wánchéng rènwù le.
    - He finally finished the task.
  - 晚餐做好了，可以开(開)饭(飯)了。
    - Wǎncān zuò hǎo le, kěyǐ kāifàn le.
    - Dinner is finished and ready to be served.
  - 我的工作还(還)没(沒)完，需要加班。
    - Wǒ de gōngzuò hái méi wán, xūyào jiābān.
    - My work is not finished yet and I need to work overtime.
### 买(買)完了 → 完 → 宀
- **definition:** roof
- **pinyin:** mián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with four walls ->
    - roof
  - **interpretation:** 宀(mián, "roof") is a pictogram representing a house with four walls. It emphasizes an enclosed space, distinguishing it from similar structures like 广(guǎng, "broad") which depicts a building with three walls. This makes 宀 a logical choice for representing a roof in various characters.
- **examples:**
  - 含有宀的汉(漢)字代表家的温(溫)暖。
    - Hán yǒu mián de hànzì dàibiǎo jiā de wēnnuǎn.
    - Chinese characters that include the radical '宀' represent the warmth of home.
  - 屋顶(頂)遮风(風)挡(擋)雨，家园(園)散发(發)温(溫)馨。
    - Wūdǐng zhē fēng dǎng yǔ, jiāyuán sànfā wēnxīn.
    - The roof shields from wind and rain, and the home radiates warmth.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 宀](@media/glyph5b80.png)
### 买(買)完了 → 完 → 元
- **definition:** origin
- **pinyin:** yuán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a human head above a horizontal line, symbolizing the origin or the head of something
  - **interpretation:** 元 (yuán, 'origin') represents the head, which is often considered the starting point or leader, aligning with the concept of 'origin'. This setup also connects metaphorically to beginnings or first principles.
- **examples:**
  - 万(萬)物之元来(來)自于(於)混沌。
    - Wànwù zhī yuán láizì yú húndùn.
    - The origin of all things comes from chaos.
  - 道家的理念追寻(尋)心灵(靈)的元。
    - Dàojiā de lǐniàn zhuīxún xīnlíng de yuán.
    - Taoist philosophy seeks the origin of the soul.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 元](@media/glyph5143.png)
### 买(買)完了 → 了
- **definition:** completed action; particle
- **pinyin:** le
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a baby without arms (compare 子 with arms) ->
    - entangled legs ->
    - sound loan for 'finish'
  - **interpretation:** The original depiction is of a baby shape illustrating a state of vulnerability or incompleteness. Over time, the idea of 'entangled legs' metaphorically transitioned into 'something tied or completed.' 'Finish' likely arose from a sound loan rather than semantic combination, as 'entangled' implies coming to an end or conclusion in a motion.
- **examples:**
  - 事情已经(經)结(結)束了。
    - Shìqíng yǐjīng jiéshù le.
    - The matter has already ended.
  - 他终(終)于(於)明白了。
    - Tā zhōngyú míngbái le.
    - He finally understood.
  - 她在一小时(時)内(內)完成了这(這)项(項)任务(務)。
    - Tā zài yī xiǎoshí nèi wánchéng le zhè xiàng rènwù.
    - She completed this task within an hour.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 了](@media/glyph4e86.png)

## 冰糖雪梨
---
## rock sugar pear drink
### bīng táng xuě lí
---
- **definition:** rock sugar pear drink
- **pinyin:** bīng táng xuě lí
- **components:**
  - 冰
    - bīng
    - ice; frost; chill; cold
  - 糖
    - táng
    - sugar; candy; sweet
  - 雪
    - xuě
    - snow; snowy; wipe away
  - 梨
    - lí
    - pear
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 冰 (bīng, "ice") + 糖 (táng, "sugar") + 雪 (xuě, "snow") + 梨 (lí, "pear")
  - **interpretation:** 冰 (bīng, "ice") suggests coldness or something refreshing, setting the context for a chilled drink. 糖 (táng, "sugar") refers to sweetness, specifically the use of rock sugar which is less refined and often used in traditional Chinese cuisine for milder sweetness. 雪 (xuě, "snow") symbolizes purity and the idea of freshness, aligning with the cooling effect of the drink. 梨 (lí, "pear") provides the main flavor component, indicating that the drink is pear-based. Combining these elements, 冰糖雪梨 refers to a refreshing beverage made of pear, typically sweetened with rock sugar, served cold to enhance its cooling effect.
- **examples:**
  - 冰糖雪梨是一种(種)清凉(涼)的饮(飲)品。
    - Bīngtáng xuělí shì yī zhǒng qīngliáng de yǐnpǐn.
    - Rock sugar pear drink is a refreshing beverage.
  - 我喜欢(歡)在夏天喝冰糖雪梨。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān zài xiàtiān hē bīngtáng xuělí.
    - I like to drink rock sugar pear drink in the summer.
  - 冰糖雪梨常用于(於)润(潤)喉止咳。
    - Bīngtáng xuělí cháng yòng yú rùn hóu zhǐ ké.
    - Rock sugar pear drink is often used to soothe the throat and relieve coughing.
### 冰糖雪梨 → 冰
- **definition:** ice; frost; chill; cold
- **pinyin:** bīng
- **components:**
  - 水
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 冫
    - bīng
    - ice
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 水 (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic 冫(bīng) ->
    - water that is frozen ->
    - ice
  - **interpretation:** The character 冰(bīng, "ice") combines the semantic element 水 (shuǐ, "water") indicating the substance and the phonetic element 冫, which provides the sound. Together they represent water that has frozen into ice.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)在夏天吃冰淇淋。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān zài xiàtiān chī bīngqílín.
    - I like eating ice cream in the summer.
  - 湖面上结(結)了一层(層)厚厚的冰。
    - Hú miàn shàng jié le yī céng hòu hòu de bīng.
    - A thick layer of ice formed on the surface of the lake.
  - 冬天时(時)，河里(裡)的水会(會)结(結)冰。
    - Dōngtiān shí, hé lǐ de shuǐ huì jié bīng.
    - In winter, the water in the river will freeze.
- **historical forms:**

### 冰糖雪梨 → 冰 → 水
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flowing water
  - **interpretation:** 水 (shuǐ, 'water') is a pictogram that directly represents the appearance of flowing water, making it intuitive and easy to recognize. Its simplicity and direct visual reference to its meaning have allowed it to remain unchanged over millennia.
- **examples:**
  - 水是一种(種)生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì yī zhǒng shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 夏天很热(熱)，喝水能解暑。
    - Xiàtiān hěn rè, hē shuǐ néng jiě shǔ.
    - It is very hot in summer, drinking water can relieve the heat.
  - 河水潺潺，沿岸绿(綠)树(樹)成荫(蔭)。
    - Hé shuǐ chánchán, yán'àn lǜshù chéng yīn.
    - The river flows babbling, and green trees along the bank provide shade.

### 冰糖雪梨 → 冰 → 冫
- **definition:** ice
- **pinyin:** bīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts two stylized blocks of ice, suggesting the concept of cold or freezing.
  - **interpretation:** The character 冫(piān, "cold") depicts two compressed and stylized blocks of ice, representing the idea of cold. This radical is commonly used in characters related to ice or coldness, capturing the visual simplicity and fundamental concept of ice in visual form.
- **examples:**
  - 冬天时(時)，河水都结(結)成冰。
    - Dōngtiān shí, hé shuǐ dōu jié chéng bīng.
    - In winter, the river water freezes into ice.
  - 他的手像冰一样(樣)冷。
    - Tā de shǒu xiàng bīng yīyàng lěng.
    - His hands are as cold as ice.
  - 打开(開)冰箱，可以感觉(覺)到冷气(氣)扑(撲)面而来(來)。
    - Dǎkāi bīngxiāng, kěyǐ gǎnjué dào lěngqì pūmiàn ér lái.
    - When you open the refrigerator, you can feel the cold air rush out.
- **historical forms:**

### 冰糖雪梨 → 糖
- **definition:** sugar; candy; sweet
- **pinyin:** táng
- **components:**
  - 米
    - mǐ
    - rice
  - 唐
    - táng
    - Tang dynasty
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 米 (mǐ, "rice") + phonetic 唐 (táng, "Tang dynasty") =
    - rice-based sweetener ->
    - sugar
  - **interpretation:** The character 糖(táng) combines 米 (mǐ, "rice"), indicating that sugar can be derived from grain-based sources like rice, with 唐 (táng), which provides the sound. This reflects the historical use of grain in sweeteners.
- **examples:**
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)在烘焙时(時)用糖调(調)味。
    - Māmā zài hōngbèi shí yòng táng tiáowèi.
    - Mom uses sugar to flavor the baked goods.
  - 他煮咖啡时(時)放了糖，使味道更加浓(濃)郁。
    - Tā zhǔ kāfēi shí fàng le táng, shǐ wèidào gèngjiā nóngyù.
    - He added sugar when brewing the coffee, which made the flavor richer.
  - 秋天的时(時)候有人卖(賣)糖，这(這)种(種)糖在节(節)日里(裡)很受欢(歡)迎。
    - Qiūtiān de shíhòu yǒurén mài táng, zhèzhǒng táng zài jiérì lǐ hěn shòu huānyíng.
    - In autumn, someone sells sugar, and this kind of sugar is very popular during festivals.

### 冰糖雪梨 → 糖 → 米
- **definition:** rice
- **pinyin:** mǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts rice kernels ->
    - 米(mǐ, 'rice')
  - **interpretation:** The character 米(mǐ, 'rice') visually represents dehusked rice kernels to differentiate it from 粟. The horizontal stroke may symbolize a bamboo sieve, emphasizing the process of separating grains from their husks.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)吃米饭(飯)。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī mǐfàn.
    - I like to eat rice.

    - Tā cóng nóngcūn dài huí yī dài mǐ, yòng lái zhǔ fàn.
    - She brought a bag of rice from the countryside to cook.
  - 市场(場)上有新米出售。
    - Shìchǎng shàng yǒu xīn mǐ chūshòu.
    - New rice is available in the market.

### 冰糖雪梨 → 糖 → 唐
- **definition:** Tang dynasty
- **pinyin:** táng
- **components:**
  - 庚
    - gēng
    - standard; fifth of the ten heavenly stems
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 庚 ->
    - integrative element ->
    - final form was 唐
  - **interpretation:** The character 唐(táng) originally referred to 'exaggerate, boast' with the mouth being the indicative semantic component 口 (kǒu, "mouth") and 庚 serving as the phonetic element. The transformation of the phonetic component indicates a shift over time from its more complete original form to the current contracted version. In the historical context, this base sense was related to expressions considered grand or impressive, leading to the Tang Dynasty being associated with grandness or magnificence, such as in 唐诗 ('Tang poetry'), distinguished for its literary excellence.
- **examples:**
  - 唐朝是一個文化繁榮的時期。
    - Tángcháo shì yī gè wénhuà fánróng de shíqí.
    - The Tang dynasty was a period of cultural prosperity.
  - 唐代詩歌極富創意，許多詩人留下不朽之作。
    - Tángdài shīgē jí fù chuàngyì, xǔduō shīrén liúxià bùxiǔ zhī zuò.
    - Poetry from the Tang dynasty was extremely creative, and many poets left behind immortal works.
  - 許多留學生對唐文化感興趣，因為它影響了整個東亞地區。
    - Xǔduō liúxuéshēng duì Táng wénhuà gǎn xìngqù, yīnwèi tā yǐngxiǎngle zhěng gè Dōng Yà dìqū.
    - Many international students are interested in Tang culture because it influenced the entire East Asian region.
- **historical forms:**

### 冰糖雪梨 → 糖 → 唐 → 庚
- **definition:** standard; fifth of the ten heavenly stems
- **pinyin:** gēng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a flail and a threshing device
  - **interpretation:** The character 庚 (gēng, "standard; fifth of the ten heavenly stems") originally depicted a flail and a threshing device used in agriculture, illustrating its role connected to the cycles and standards in agricultural work, which were fundamental in traditional Chinese calendars and reckoning systems.
- **examples:**
  - 庚是天干的第五位。
    - Gēng shì tiāngān de dì wǔ wèi.
    - Geng is the fifth of the ten heavenly stems.
  - 在古代历(曆)法中，庚被用作记(記)录(錄)年份的符号(號)。
    - Zài gǔdài lìfǎ zhōng, gēng bèi yòng zuò jìlù niánfèn de fúhào.
    - In ancient calendars, Geng was used as a symbol to record the year.
  - 庚日适(適)合举(舉)办(辦)婚礼(禮)，因为(為)它象征(徵)着(著)新开(開)始。
    - Gēng rì shìhé jǔbàn hūnlǐ, yīnwèi tā xiàngzhēngzhe xīn kāishǐ.
    - The Geng day is suitable for holding weddings because it symbolizes a new beginning.
### 冰糖雪梨 → 糖 → 唐 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 冰糖雪梨 → 雪
- **definition:** snow; snowy; wipe away
- **pinyin:** xuě
- **components:**
  - 雨
    - yǔ
    - rain
  - 彗
    - huì
    - broom
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 雨 (yǔ, "rain") + phonetic 彗 (huì, "broom") ->
    - snow
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 雨 (yǔ, "rain") for the semantic idea of precipitation and 彗 (huì, "broom") for its phonetic value. The image of rain light and fluffy as a broom sweep implies the specific type of precipitation: snow.
- **examples:**
  - 冬天的时(時)候，我们(們)经(經)常去山上滑雪。
    - Dōngtiān de shíhòu, wǒmen jīngcháng qù shānshàng huáxuě.
    - In winter, we often go to the mountains to ski.
  - 昨天晚上下了很多雪。
    - Zuótiān wǎnshàng xiàle hěnduō xuě.
    - It snowed a lot last night.
  - 雪花在阳(陽)光下闪(閃)闪(閃)发(發)光。
    - Xuěhuā zài yángguāng xià shǎnshǎn fāguāng.
    - The snowflakes sparkle under the sunlight.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 雪](@media/glyph96ea.png)

    - rain

### 冰糖雪梨 → 雪 → 彗

  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand

  - **description:**

    - holding a broom
  - **interpretation:** The character 彗 (huì, "broom") combines 甡 (shēn, "broom") with 又 (yòu, "hand") to depict the action of holding a broom. This emphasizes the function and use of a broom, suggesting an object specifically designed to be held by hand for sweeping.
- **examples:**

    - The old craftsman uses the broom to meticulously clean the workshop.

    - Zài hán dōng yè wǎn, tā mò mò ná qǐ huì, qīng sǎo mén qián.
    - On a cold winter night, he silently picked up the broom and swept the front door.

  - **interpretation:** The character 甡 contains the semantic component 生 (shēng, "life") which may suggest something related to production or generation, combined with the phonetic 辛 (xīn), which contributes the sound. The character's connection to 'broom' is through borrowing for phonetic purposes and does not derive directly from its parts.

  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.

### 冰糖雪梨 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 辛
- **definition:** bitter; toilsome
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a tool—chisel or awl—used to mark slaves and criminals ->
    - 辛
  - **interpretation:** The character 辛 (xīn) originally depicted a tool such as a chisel, used for marking or branding. The association with a sharp tool helps explain its extended meaning of 'spice,' as spices can have a pungent, sharp quality reminiscent of a tool's point or effect.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)菜有一种(種)辛辣的味道。
    - Zhège cài yǒu yī zhǒng xīnlà de wèidào.
    - This dish has a spicy taste.
  - 他喜欢(歡)在食物里(裡)添加辛香料。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài shíwù lǐ tiānjiā xīn xiāngliào.
    - He likes to add spices to the food.
  - 这(這)种(種)辛口的调(調)料非常受欢(歡)迎。
    - Zhè zhǒng xīnkǒu de tiáoliào fēicháng shòu huānyíng.
    - This type of spicy seasoning is very popular.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 辛](@media/glyph8f9b.png)
### 冰糖雪梨 → 雪 → 彗 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.

### 冰糖雪梨 → 梨

    - lì

  - **description:**

    - pear tree
  - **interpretation:** The character 梨 (lí, "pear") is a phono-semantic compound where 木 (mù, "wood") provides the semantic element, indicating a tree or something related to wood, and 利 (lì) contributes the phonetic component, suggesting the sound 'lí'. This combination forms the meaning of a 'pear tree,' which aligns with its wooden trunk characteristic.
- **examples:**
