## 凑(湊)凑(湊)火
---
## make do with a meal
### còu còu huǒ
---
- **traditional:** 湊湊火
- **definition:** make do with a meal
- **pinyin:** còu còu huǒ
- **components:**
  - 凑(湊)
    - còu
    - gather; put together; improvise; approach
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire; flame; cooking; urgent
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 凑(湊) (còu, "gather; put together") suggests the idea of bringing elements together, often with the sense of improvisation or making do. 火 (huǒ, "fire") here metaphorically represents cooking or preparing food, as fire is essential for cooking. Combining 凑(湊) and 火, the phrase illustrates the concept of hurriedly gathering and preparing a meal.
  - **interpretation:** In the expression 湊湊火 (còu còu huǒ), the sense of 'make do with a meal' is captured by the notion of 凑(湊) (còu, "gather")—implying hastily collecting resources or ingredients. 火 (huǒ, "fire") is symbolic of cooking or the act of preparing food. The phrase thus conveys the idea of quickly putting together a meal using whatever is available, akin to making do with the resources at hand.
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊)
- **traditional:** 湊
- **definition:** gather; put together; improvise; approach
- **pinyin:** còu
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 奏
    - zòu
    - perform
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 氵 (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic: 奏 (zòu) =
    - actions associated with water flowing together ->
    - gather together
  - **interpretation:** The character 湊 (còu, "gather together") uses 氵 (shuǐ, "water") to suggest actions akin to water pooling or coming together, with 奏 (zòu) providing the sound. This indicates the coming together of elements or people.
  - **simplification:** 湊 was simplified to 凑(湊) by removing the water radical 氵 (shuǐ, "water"), keeping the phonetic 奏 (zòu), simplifying the structure.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)凑(湊)些钱(錢)，买(買)生日礼(禮)物。
    - Wǒmen còu xiē qián, mǎi shēngrì lǐwù.
    - We gathered some money to buy a birthday gift.
  - 他凑(湊)上邻(鄰)居的钱(錢)，解决(決)了急事。
    - Tā còu shàng lǐnjū de qián, jiějué le jíshì.
    - He gathered money from his neighbors to deal with an urgent matter.
  - 没(沒)有足够(夠)的材料，她只好凑(湊)合做饭(飯)。
    - Méiyǒu zúgòu de cáiliào, tā zhǐhǎo còu hé zuò fàn.
    - Lacking sufficient ingredients, she had to make do with what she had to cook.
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字中偏旁氵，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快戏(戲)水。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 奏
- **definition:** perform
- **pinyin:** zòu
- **components:**
  - 廾
    - gǒng
    - two hands
  - 夲
    - tuō
    - root
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - two hands 廾 (gǒng, 'two hands') holding an object, perhaps an instrument from a ritual originally similar to 夲 (tuō, 'root') ->
    - final form 奏 (zòu, 'perform')
  - **interpretation:** The character 奏 (zòu, 'perform') symbolizes two hands holding a musical object used in a ritual, highlighting the connection to ceremonial performances. This reflects its role in traditional sacrificial music performances.
- **examples:**
  - 乐(樂)团(團)今晚将(將)在音乐(樂)厅(廳)奏一首新曲。
    - Yuètuán jīnwǎn jiāng zài yīnyuètīng zòu yī shǒu xīnqǔ.
    - The orchestra will perform a new piece tonight.
  - 他每次上台(臺)都会(會)全情投入奏自己的作品。
    - Tā měi cì shàngtái dōu huì quánqíng tóurù zòu zìjǐ de zuòpǐn.
    - He always puts his heart into performing his own pieces every time he goes on stage.
  - 琴师(師)精心调(調)音后(後)，开(開)始奏乐(樂)。
    - Qínshī jīngxīn tiáoyīn hòu, kāishǐ zòu yuè.
    - After the pianist finely tuned the instrument, he began to perform music.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 奏](@media/glyph594f.png)
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 奏 → 廾
- **definition:** two hands
- **pinyin:** gǒng
- **components:**
  - 𠂇
    - shǒu
    - left hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - right hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𠂇 (left hand) + 又 (right hand) =
    - two hands
  - **interpretation:** The character combines depictions of the left hand 𠂇 and the right hand 又, representing the concept of using both hands together. This combination naturally conveys the meaning of 'two hands.'
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廾](@media/glyph5efe.png)
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 奏 → 廾 → 𠂇
- **definition:** left hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - again
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts 又 (yòu, "again") flipped, representing a left hand.
  - **interpretation:** 𠂇 is a pictogram representing a left hand, visually derived from the character 又 (yòu, "again") by flipping it.
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 奏 → 廾 → 𠂇 → 又
- **definition:** again
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 奏 → 夲
- **definition:** root
- **pinyin:** tuō
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
  - 十
    - shí
    - ten
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 大 ("big") + 十 ("ten") =
    - combining large size with the concept of ten ->
    - symbolizing a foundation or root
  - **interpretation:** The character 夲 (tuō, "root") combines 大 (dà, "big") and 十 (shí, "ten") to suggest a broad and solid foundation, emphasizing the concept of a base or root. This notion of expansiveness or fundamental support connects to the idea of the root being a central or anchoring point.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夲](@media/glyph5932.png)
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 奏 → 夲 → 大
- **definition:** big
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)房子很大。
    - Zhè ge fángzi hěn dà.
    - This house is very big.
  - 大海波涛(濤)汹(洶)涌(湧)，展现(現)出大自然的力量。
    - Dàhǎi bōtāo xiōngyǒng, zhǎnxiàn chū dàzìrán de lìliàng.
    - The vast ocean waves surge, showcasing the power of nature.
  - 大人物登场(場)，留下传(傳)奇。
    - Dà rénwù dēngchǎng, liúxià chuánqí.
    - Great figures make an appearance, leaving behind legends.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 大](@media/glyph5927.png)
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 奏 → 夲 → 大 → 夫
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a variant form of 大 (dà, "big") representing an adult man with a hairpin ->
    - became associated with 夫 (fū, "man").
  - **interpretation:** 夫 (fū, "man") was visually similar to 大 (dà, "big") and was originally interchangeable. The addition of the horizontal stroke was interpreted as a hairpin, symbolizing adulthood for men.
- **examples:**
  - 此夫心怀(懷)大志。
    - Cǐ fū xīn huái dà zhì.
    - This man has lofty aspirations.
  - 他勤劳(勞)努力，堪称(稱)良夫。
    - Tā qín láo nǔ lì, kān chēng liáng fū.
    - He works diligently and is regarded as an exemplary man.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夫](@media/glyph592b.png)
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 凑(湊) → 奏 → 夲 → 十
- **definition:** ten
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original vertical stroke ->
    - later horizontal stroke added ->
    - forms a cross ->
    - represents 'ten'
  - **interpretation:** The character 十(shí, 'ten') represents the number ten with a cross shape that could be seen as tally marks. It evolved from a simple vertical stroke to a cross by adding a horizontal stroke, symbolizing a complete set of ten.
- **examples:**
  - 我有十本书(書)。
    - Wǒ yǒu shí běn shū.
    - I have ten books.
  - 花园(園)里(裡)有十棵树(樹)，景色十分优(優)美。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu shí kē shù, jǐngsè shífēn yōuměi.
    - There are ten trees in the garden, and the scenery is very beautiful.
  - 十年磨一剑(劍)。
    - Shí nián mó yī jiàn.
    - It takes ten years of practice to hone a sword.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 十](@media/glyph5341.png)
### 凑(湊)凑(湊)火 → 火
- **definition:** fire; flame; cooking; urgent
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火在壁炉(爐)中熊熊燃烧(燒)。
    - Huǒ zài bìlú zhōng xióngxióng ránshāo.
    - The fire burns fiercely in the fireplace.
  - 野外露营(營)时(時)，火能驱(驅)走寒冷。
    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇到火灾(災)时(時)，迅速疏散最为(為)重要。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.
    - In case of a fire, evacuating quickly is of utmost importance.
- **historical forms:**

## 南锣(鑼)鼓巷
---
## historic alley in Beijing
### nán luó gǔ xiàng
---
- **traditional:** 南鑼鼓巷
- **definition:** historic alley in Beijing
- **pinyin:** nán luó gǔ xiàng
- **components:**
  - 南
    - nán
    - south
  - 鑼
    - luó
    - gong
  - 鼓
    - gǔ
    - drum
  - 巷
    - xiàng
    - alley
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 南 (nán, "south") + 鑼 (luó, "gong") + 鼓 (gǔ, "drum") + 巷 (xiàng, "alley")
  - **interpretation:** The name 南鑼鼓巷 (Nánluógǔ Xiàng, "South Gong and Drum Alley") reflects its historical location oriented to the south of an area once famous for craftsmen making gongs and drums. These instruments suggest a bustling, lively atmosphere, which is a trait of the neighborhood as a social and cultural hub. The combination evokes an image of an alleyway resonating with musical sounds from gongs and drums, highlighting its vibrant historical significance.
- **examples:**
  - 南锣(鑼)鼓巷是北京著名的旅游景点。
    - Nán luó gǔ xiàng shì Běijīng zhùmíng de lǚyóu jǐngdiǎn.
    - Nanluoguxiang is a famous tourist attraction in Beijing.
  - 每年有很多游(遊)客参(參)观(觀)南锣(鑼)鼓巷。
    - Měinián yǒu hěn duō yóukè cānguān Nán luó gǔ xiàng.
    - Every year, many tourists visit Nanluoguxiang.
  - 南锣(鑼)鼓巷有许多历史悠久的建筑和现代化的商店。
    - Nán luó gǔ xiàng yǒu xǔduō lìshǐ yōujiǔ de jiànzhù hé xiàndàihuà de shāngdiàn.
    - Nanluoguxiang has many historic buildings and modern shops.
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 南
- **definition:** south
- **pinyin:** nán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hanging percussion instrument (bell) ->
    - Phonetically borrowed for 'south'
  - **interpretation:** 南 originally depicted a bell, indicating hanging percussion instruments, and was later borrowed for its sound to mean 'south'. This borrowing is based on phonetic resemblance rather than a direct conceptual link with directionality.
- **examples:**
  - 南方的天气(氣)很温(溫)暖。
    - Nánfāng de tiānqì hěn wēnnuǎn.
    - The weather in the south is very warm.
  - 我们(們)计(計)划(劃)去南部旅行。
    - Wǒmen jìhuà qù nánbù lǚxíng.
    - We plan to travel to the south.
  - 他住在城市的南边(邊)。
    - Tā zhù zài chéngshì de nánbiān.
    - He lives on the south side of the city.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 南](@media/glyph5357.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼
- **definition:** gong
- **pinyin:** luó
- **components:**
  - 金
    - jīn
    - metal
  - 羅
    - luó
    - to catch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 金 (jīn, "metal") + phonetic 羅 (luó) ->
    - metal instrument ->
    - gong
  - **interpretation:** 鑼 (luó, "gong") is a large metal instrument that produces a resonant sound. The character uses 金 (jīn, "metal") as the semantic component, indicating it is made of metal. The phonetic component 羅 (luó) suggests its pronunciation.
  - **simplification:** 鑼 was simplified to 锣 by removing the complex component 羅 and replacing it with simplified form that suggests sound.
- **examples:**
  - 当(當)钟(鐘)楼(樓)敲响(響)时(時)，村里(裡)的人们(們)都停下手中的活儿(兒)。
    - Dāng zhōng lóu qiāo xiǎng shí, cūn lǐ de rénmen dōu tíng xià shǒuzhōng de huó'er.
    - When the bell tower rings, the villagers all stop their work.
  - 他用力敲打鑼，发(發)出巨大的声(聲)音。
    - Tā yòng lì qiāo dǎ luó, fā chū jùdà de shēngyīn.
    - He strikes the gong forcefully, producing a loud sound.
  - 古老的仪(儀)式中，總是可以听(聽)到鑼聲。
    - Gǔlǎo de yíshì zhōng, zǒng shì kěyǐ tīng dào luó shēng.
    - In ancient ceremonies, the sound of the gong can always be heard.
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 金
- **definition:** metal
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 士
    - shì
    - upside-down ritual axe
  - 呂
    - lǚ
    - two blocks of metal
  - 亼
    - jí
    - open mouth upside down
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 士 (upside-down ritual axe) + 呂 (two blocks of metal) + phonetic 亼 (open mouth upside down) ->
    - original pronunciation; no earth pictogram in ancient forms ->
    - metal, later gold
  - **interpretation:** Initially representing copper, due to its use in the Copper Age, the character 金 (jīn, "metal") evolved to refer broadly to metal as technological progress made various metals crucial in society. The extension to gold reflects its value and prominence. The phonetic 亼 indicates the character's pronunciation, with semantic elements showing early associations with precious materials.
- **examples:**
  - 金是一种(種)重要的工业(業)原料。
    - Jīn shì yī zhǒng zhòngyào de gōngyè yuánliào.
    - Metal is an important industrial material.
  - 她的项(項)链(鍊)是纯(純)金的。
    - Tā de xiàngliàn shì chún jīn de.
    - Her necklace is made of pure gold.
  - 每个(個)国(國)家都有自己的金矿(礦)。
    - Měi gè guójiā dōu yǒu zìjǐ de jīnkuàng.
    - Every country has its own gold mines.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 金](@media/glyph91d1.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 金 → 士
- **definition:** upside-down ritual axe
- **pinyin:** shì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a ritual axe, possibly made of jade ->
    - symbolized soldier ->
    - intellectual or officer over time
  - **interpretation:** The character 士(shì, 'scholar') originally depicted a ritual axe used in ceremonies, implying a person of a certain rank or status who could wield such symbols. This connection to ceremonial authority evolved to mean 'soldier' and later 'intellectual' or 'officer', roles associated with leadership and knowledge in societal hierarchies.
- **examples:**
  - 历(歷)史上，士被视(視)为(為)一种(種)权(權)力的象征(徵)。
    - Lìshǐ shàng, shì bèi shì wéi yī zhǒng quánlì de xiàngzhēng.
    - Historically, the 'shi' was seen as a symbol of power.
  - 在古代，只有贵(貴)族才拥(擁)有士。
    - Zài gǔdài, zhǐyǒu guìzú cái yǒngyǒu shì.
    - In ancient times, only nobles possessed the 'shi'.
  - 士的制(製)作材料可能是珍贵(貴)的金属(屬)。
    - Shì de zhìzuò cáiliào kěnéng shì zhēnguì de jīnshǔ.
    - The materials used to make the 'shi' might have been precious metals.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 士](@media/glyph58eb.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 金 → 呂
- **definition:** two blocks of metal
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two disconnected blocks of metal, later connected in seal script ->
    - Original form of 鋁 (lǚ, 'ingot') ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'spine' and 'music notes'
  - **interpretation:** The character 呂(lǚ) ('two blocks of metal') visually represents two separate blocks aligned vertically. In its earliest forms, these blocks were disconnected, symbolizing distinct metal segments, which aligns with its early use for 'ingot'. Over time, as seen in seal script, a connecting line was added to form the modern appearance. This visual interpretation supports its original meaning related to metal. It was later phonetically borrowed to convey concepts like 'spine' and 'music notes', where no direct semantic link exists with metal, but the sound similarity allowed its reuse in these contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 他用两(兩)个(個)大的金属(屬)块(塊)铸(鑄)造了一个(個)雕像。
    - Tā yòng liǎng gè dà de jīnshǔ kuài zhùzào le yī gè diāoxiàng.
    - He cast a statue using two large blocks of metal.
  - 现(現)代工业(業)中，金属(屬)块(塊)常用于(於)制(製)造重型设(設)备(備)。
    - Xiàndài gōngyè zhōng, jīnshǔ kuài cháng yòng yú zhìzào zhòngxíng shèbèi.
    - In modern industry, metal blocks are often used for manufacturing heavy equipment.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)师(師)用金属(屬)块(塊)建造了一个(個)现(現)代化建筑(築)。
    - Zhège shèjì shī yòng jīnshǔ kuài jiànzào le yī gè xiàndàihuà jiànzhù.
    - The designer built a modern structure using metal blocks.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 呂](@media/glyph5442.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 金 → 亼
- **definition:** open mouth upside down
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 金 → 亼 → 入
- **definition:** enter
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入座。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生走入校园(園)，开(開)始新学(學)期。

  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**

    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.

### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 金 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今天的天气(氣)不错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在是吃晚饭(飯)的时(時)候。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她今天特别(別)忙，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 金 → 亼 → 今 → 曰
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)曰：勤奋(奮)是成功之母。
    - Lǎoshī yuē：qínfèn shì chénggōng zhī mǔ。
    - The teacher said, 'Diligence is the mother of success.'
  - 孔子曰，学(學)而不思则(則)罔。
    - Kǒngzǐ yuē, xué ér bù sī zé wǎng。
    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无(無)为(為)而治。
    - Lǎozǐ yuē, wúwéi ér zhì。
    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 曰](@media/glyph66f0.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 羅
- **definition:** to catch
- **pinyin:** luó
- **components:**
  - 网
    - wǎng
    - net
  - 維
    - wéi
    - bird (tied with string)
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 网 (wǎng, "net") + 維 (wéi, "bird (tied with string)") =
    - net for catching birds ->
    - trapping or a net
  - **interpretation:** The character 羅 (luó, "to net") intuitively combines the concept of a net 网 (wǎng) with 維 (wéi, "bird (tied with string)") to visually represent a tool designed for trapping or catching, similar to a bird snare.
  - **simplification:** 羅 was simplified to 罗 by replacing 維 with 夕 (xī, "evening") as a more streamlined form.
- **examples:**
  - 渔(漁)夫用网(網)罗(羅)鱼(魚)。
    - Yúfū yòng wǎng luó yú.
    - The fisherman nets fish.
  - 猎(獵)人精心布(佈)置陷阱，罗(羅)捕野兔。
    - Lièrén jīngxīn bùzhì xiànjǐng, luó bǔ yětù.
    - The hunter carefully sets traps, netting wild rabbits.
  - 渔(漁)船扬(揚)帆出海，罗(羅)捕群(羣)鱼(魚)。
    - Yúchuán yángfān chūhǎi, luó bǔ qúnyú.
    - The fishing boat sets sail, netting a school of fish.
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 羅 → 网(網)
- **traditional:** 網
- **definition:** net
- **pinyin:** wǎng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a net with crossing lines or mesh ->
    - symbol for 'net'
  - **interpretation:** The character 网(網) (wǎng, 'net') visually represents a net with lines intersecting to form a grid, making it intuitive as a symbol for a net or mesh.
  - **simplification:** The simplified character 网 (wǎng) retains the essential visual structure of intersecting lines to depict a net. It conveys the idea of a net through a simplified representation without additional semantic or phonetic elements.
- **examples:**
  - 他用网(網)捕鱼(魚)，快乐(樂)满(滿)怀(懷)。
    - Tā yòng wǎng bǔ yú, kuàilè mǎn huái.
    - He fishes with a net and is full of joy.
  - 很多信息通过(過)网(網)传(傳)播，速度惊(驚)人。
    - Hěn duō xìnxī tōngguò wǎng chuánbō, sùdù jīngrén.
    - A lot of information spreads through the net with astonishing speed.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 网](@media/glyph7f51.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 羅 → 維
- **definition:** bird (tied with string)
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk; thread
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 糸 ('silk; thread') + phonetic 唯 (wéi) ->
    - bird tied with string
  - **interpretation:** The character 維 depicts the semantic element 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread'), representing strings or threads, combined with the phonetic element 唯 (wéi), which shares the pronunciation. This combination suggests the action of tying or fastening with thread, which is metaphorically extended to denote binding or maintaining concepts, leading to meanings like 'to hold together' or 'to maintain the integrity of'. The image of a bird tied with string serves as a metaphor for something being secured or controlled.
  - **simplification:** 維 is simplified to 维 by substituting 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') with its simplified version 纟, reducing the number of strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 古代人用绳(繩)子捕捉鸟(鳥)类(類)，这(這)种(種)方法称(稱)为(為)维(維)。
    - Gǔdài rén yòng shéngzi bǔzhuō niǎolèi, zhè zhǒng fāngfǎ chēng wéi wéi.
    - In ancient times, people used ropes to catch birds, and this method was called 'wéi'.
  - 在村落里(裡)，维(維)常常用于(於)帮(幫)助打猎(獵)。
    - Zài cūnluò lǐ, wéi chángcháng yòng yú bāngzhù dǎliè.
    - In the village, 'wéi' was often used to assist in hunting.
  - 小孩们(們)好奇地观(觀)察大人如何使用维(維)。
    - Xiǎohái men hàoqí de guānchá dàren rúhé shǐyòng wéi.
    - Children curiously observed how adults used 'wéi'.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 維](@media/glyph7dad.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 羅 → 維 → 糸
- **definition:** silk; thread
- **pinyin:** mì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她手工制(製)作了一条(條)漂亮的丝(絲)巾。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)图(圖)必须(須)用细(細)糸画(畫)出来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我们(們)参(參)观(觀)了古代的织(織)布技术(術)，对(對)丝(絲)绸(綢)制(製)作产(產)生了兴(興)趣。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.

### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 羅 → 維 → 唯
- **definition:** only
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tailed bird
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") ->
    - original form of 鷕 ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'only'
  - **interpretation:** The character 唯 originally represented the cry of a bird, with the mouth radical indicating the sound aspect. It was later phonetically borrowed for the abstract meaning 'only', without retaining its original context related to bird sounds.
- **examples:**
  - 唯有努力，才能成功。
    - Wéi yǒu nǔlì, cái néng chénggōng.
    - Only by working hard can one succeed.
  - 唯有在安静(靜)的夜晚，我才能听(聽)清自己的心声(聲)。
    - Wéi yǒu zài ānjìng de yèwǎn, wǒ cái néng tīng qīng zìjǐ de xīnshēng.
    - Only in the quiet of the night can I hear my own heart.
  - 我唯爱(愛)读(讀)书(書)，因为(為)书(書)籍能带(帶)给(給)我无(無)限的可能。
    - Wǒ wéi ài dúshū, yīnwèi shūjí néng dài gěi wǒ wúxiàn de kěnéng.
    - I only love reading, because books bring me infinite possibilities.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 唯](@media/glyph552f.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 羅 → 維 → 唯 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 羅 → 維 → 唯 → 隹
- **definition:** short-tailed bird
- **pinyin:** zhuī
- **components:**
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a short‐tailed bird (e.g., a sparrow) ->
    - also original form of 唯 (wéi, "only") before evolution into 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird")
  - **interpretation:** 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") is a pictogram representing a bird with a short tail. Its depiction served as the foundation for other characters related to birds, such as 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird").
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)只短尾的隹在树(樹)林中飞(飛)翔。
    - Zhè zhī duǎnwěi de zhuī zài shùlín zhōng fēixiáng.
    - This short-tailed bird flies in the forest.
  - 博物馆(館)里(裡)展出了一件以隹为(為)题(題)材的古代绘(繪)画(畫)。
    - Bówùguǎn lǐ zhǎnchūle yī jiàn yǐ zhuī wèi tícái de gǔdài huìhuà.
    - The museum displays an ancient painting themed on the short-tailed bird.
  - 远(遠)古诗(詩)篇中常用隹来(來)象征(徵)自由，寓意生动(動)。
    - Yuǎngǔ shīpiān zhōng cháng yòng zhuī lái xiàngzhēng zìyóu, yùyì shēngdòng.
    - In ancient poems, the short-tailed bird is often used to symbolize freedom, conveying vivid meaning.
- **historical forms:**

### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鑼 → 羅 → 維 → 唯 → 鷕
- **definition:** cry of a bird
- **pinyin:** yǎo
- **components:**
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
  - 鳥
    - niǎo
    - bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 唯 (phonetic) + 鳥 (semantic, "bird") ->
    - cry of a bird
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 唯 (wéi, used phonetically for its sound) with 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") to denote the specific sound relating to a bird's cry.
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鼓
- **definition:** drum
- **pinyin:** gǔ
- **components:**
  - 壴
    - zhù
    - drum
  - 支
    - zhī
    - hand holding drumstick
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 壴 (zhù, "drum") + 支 (zhī, "hand holding drumstick") =
    - drum being played ->
    - drum
  - **interpretation:** The character 鼓(gǔ) combines a depiction of a drum 壴 with a hand holding a drumstick 支. This intuitive combination directly represents the act of drumming.
- **examples:**
  - 他敲鼓。
    - Tā qiāo gǔ.
    - He beats the drum.
  - 音乐(樂)会(會)开(開)始时(時)，乐(樂)手敲鼓。
    - Yīnyuèhuì kāishǐ shí, yuèshǒu qiāo gǔ.
    - When the concert begins, the musician beats the drum.
- **historical forms:**

### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鼓 → 壴
- **definition:** drum
- **pinyin:** zhù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a drum 壴, with a base and feathers 土 on top ->
    - stylized in the Kangxi radical 鼓
  - **interpretation:** The character 壴 (zhù, "drum") visually represents a drum with two ends, with elements contributing to its structure, such as a base and feathers. It was later incorporated into characters like 鼓 (gǔ, "drum") by adding elements that illustrate additional actions like hands holding a drumstick.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)面壴声(聲)震天动(動)地。
    - Zhè miàn zhù shēng zhèn tiān dòng dì.
    - The sound of this drum shakes the heavens and the earth.
  - 战(戰)士敲响(響)壴，示警敌(敵)人。
    - Zhànshì qiāo xiǎng zhù, shì jǐng dírén.
    - The soldier beats the drum to warn the enemy.
  - 庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式上，祭司击(擊)打壴，宣告传(傳)统(統)。
    - Zhuāngyán yíshì shàng, jìsī jī dǎ zhù, xuānguò chuántǒng.
    - At the solemn ceremony, the priest beats the drum to proclaim tradition.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 壴](@media/glyph58f4.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 鼓 → 支
- **definition:** hand holding drumstick
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand holding a drumstick
  - **interpretation:** The character 支 (zhī, 'hand holding drumstick') visually represents a hand grasping a stick-like object, suggesting support or physical action, which aligns with its meanings related to branching or supporting.
- **examples:**
  - 他支鼓槌，敲响(響)大鼓。
    - Tā zhī gǔchuí, qiāo xiǎng dà gǔ.
    - He holds the drumstick and strikes the big drum.
  - 鼓手支着(著)鼓槌，打出动(動)人节(節)奏。
    - Gǔshǒu zhī zhe gǔchuí, dǎ chū dòngrén jiézòu.
    - The drummer holds the drumstick and produces a captivating rhythm.

### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷
- **definition:** alley
- **pinyin:** xiàng
- **components:**
  - 己
    - jǐ
    - oneself
  - 共
    - gòng
    - together
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 己 (己) (jǐ, "oneself") + phonetic 共 (共) (gòng, "together") ->
    - alley; lane
  - **interpretation:** The character 巷 illustrates a concept of joining or confluence, similar to intersecting roads creating an alley or lane. The semantic component 己 (jǐ, "oneself") initially suggests a personal, inner path, which when combined with the phonetic component 共 (gòng, "together"), lends the idea of a shared or common path used by all, such as an alley or lane.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)在这(這)条(條)巷子里(裡)迷路了。
    - Wǒmen zài zhè tiáo xiàngzi lǐ mílù le.
    - We got lost in this alley.
  - 老房子坐落在安静(靜)的巷中。
    - Lǎo fángzi zuòluò zài ānjìng de xiàng zhōng.
    - The old house is located in a quiet alley.
  - 小猫(貓)常常在巷尾的角落玩耍。
    - Xiǎo māo chángcháng zài xiàng wěi de jiǎoluò wánshuǎ.
    - The kitten often plays in the corner at the end of the alley.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 巷](@media/glyph5df7.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 己
- **definition:** oneself
- **pinyin:** jǐ
- **components:**
  - 紀
    - jì
    - record
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts silk rope for binding objects; original form of 紀 (紀) (jì, "record")
  - **interpretation:** 己 (jǐ, "self") depicts a silk rope for binding, symbolizing the concept of self-containment or self-restriction, leading to the abstract sense of 'self'.
- **examples:**
  - 知己知彼，百战(戰)不殆。
    - Zhī jǐ zhī bǐ, bǎi zhàn bù dài.
    - Know yourself and know your enemy, and you will never be defeated.
  - 每个(個)人都应(應)该(該)反省自己。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yīng gāi fǎn xǐng zì jǐ.
    - Everyone should reflect on themselves.
  - 你要为(為)自己负(負)责(責)。
    - Nǐ yào wèi zì jǐ fù zé.
    - You need to be responsible for yourself.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 己](@media/glyph5df1.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 己 → 紀
- **definition:** record
- **pinyin:** jì
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk; thread
  - 己
    - jǐ
    - self
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') + phonetic 己 (jǐ) ->
    - record
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') indicating threads or lines, with 己 (jǐ) as the phonetic component. In this context, 'thread' aligns with 'record' in the sense of a sequence or line of events documented over time.
  - **simplification:** The traditional form 紀 with 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') replaced by the simpler 纟 in the simplified form 纪.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)本书(書)详(詳)细(細)记(記)录(錄)了历(歷)史事件。
    - Zhè běn shū xiángxì jìlù le lìshǐ shìjiàn.
    - This book records historical events in detail.
  - 古代人通过(過)文字来(來)纪(紀)念重要事情。
    - Gǔdài rén tōngguò wénzì lái jìniàn zhòngyào shìqíng.
    - Ancient people recorded important events through writing.
  - 公司在年底会(會)发(發)布(佈)年度报(報)告来(來)记(記)录(錄)发(發)展情况(況)。
    - Gōngsī zài niándǐ huì fābù niándù bàogào lái jìlù fāzhǎn qíngkuàng.
    - The company will release an annual report at the end of the year to record development status.

### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 共
- **definition:** together
- **pinyin:** gòng
- **components:**
  - 廾
    - gǒng
    - two hands
  - 供
    - gòng
    - to provide
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - an object
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 廾 (two hands) + original 口 (an object) ->
    - holding an object with two hands; original form of 供 (gòng, 'to provide') ->
    - 廿 positional adjustment ->
    - modern 共
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted two hands holding an object, representing the idea of coming together to support or present something together. Over time, this concept of holding or presenting led to the abstract sense of acting 'together'.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)一起工作，共享成果。
    - Wǒmen yīqǐ gōngzuò，gòngxiǎng chéngguǒ。
    - We work together and share the results.
  - 这(這)次旅行我们(們)共度了美好时(時)光。
    - Zhè cì lǚxíng wǒmen gòngdùle měihǎo shíguāng。
    - We spent a wonderful time together during this trip.
  - 他们(們)共同合作，完成了项(項)目。
    - Tāmen gòngtóng hézuò，wánchéngle xiàngmù。
    - They worked together and completed the project.

  - **description:**
    - 𠂇 (left hand) + 又 (right hand) =
    - two hands
  - **interpretation:** The character combines depictions of the left hand 𠂇 and the right hand 又, representing the concept of using both hands together. This combination naturally conveys the meaning of 'two hands.'

### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 共 → 廾 → 𠂇
- **definition:** left hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - again
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts 又 (yòu, "again") flipped, representing a left hand.
  - **interpretation:** 𠂇 is a pictogram representing a left hand, visually derived from the character 又 (yòu, "again") by flipping it.
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 共 → 廾 → 𠂇 → 又
- **definition:** again
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 共 → 供
- **definition:** to provide
- **pinyin:** gòng
- **components:**
  - 亻
    - rén
    - person
  - 共
    - gòng
    - together
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 亻 (rén, "person") + phonetic 共 (gòng) ->
    - to provide
  - **interpretation:** The character 供(gòng, "to provide") combines the semantic element 亻 (rén, "person"), indicating an action performed by people, with the phonetic element 共 (gòng), which contributes its sound. This phono-semantic composition logically leads to the meaning "to provide," as it suggests a person engaged in the act of supplying or offering something.
- **examples:**
  - 他们(們)为(為)灾(災)区(區)提供食物和水。
    - Tāmen wèi zāiqū tígōng shíwù hé shuǐ.
    - They provide food and water for the disaster area.
  - 企业(業)需要为(為)员(員)工提供更好的福利。
    - Qǐyè xūyào wèi yuángōng tígōng gèng hǎo de fúlì.
    - Companies need to provide better benefits for their employees.
  - 这(這)个(個)图(圖)书(書)馆(館)为(為)学(學)生提供免费(費)书(書)籍。
    - Zhège túshūguǎn wèi xuéshēng tígōng miǎnfèi shūjí.
    - This library provides free books for students.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 供](@media/glyph4f9b.png)
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 共 → 供 → 亻
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Stylization of 人 (rén, "person") as a side radical to depict a person
  - **interpretation:** 亻 is a stylized form of 人 (rén, "person") used to indicate human-related meanings when combined with other components in characters as a radical. It visually represents a standing person, maintaining the core meaning of 'person' while facilitating the construction of complex characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一个(個)热(熱)心的人。
    - Tā shì yī gè rèxīn de rén.
    - He is a kind-hearted person.
  - 这(這)座城市里(裡)住着(著)很多优(優)秀的人。
    - Zhè zuò chéngshì lǐ zhùzhe hěn duō yōuxiù de rén.
    - There are many outstanding people living in this city.
  - 每个(個)人都有梦(夢)想。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu mèngxiǎng.
    - Everyone has dreams.
### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 共 → 供 → 亻 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.

### 南锣(鑼)鼓巷 → 巷 → 共 → 口
- **definition:** an object
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

## 发(發)呆
---
## to stare blankly; to be lost in thought
### fā dāi
---
- **traditional:** 發呆
- **definition:** to stare blankly; to be lost in thought
- **pinyin:** fā dāi
- **components:**
  - 发(發)
    - fā
    - send out; emit; develop
  - 呆
    - dāi
    - dull; foolish
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 发(發) (fā, "send out; emit; develop") + 呆 (dāi, "dull; foolish") =
    - to be in a daze
  - **interpretation:** 發(fā, "send out; emit") suggests an outward movement or releasing state, such as going into another mental state. 呆(dāi, "dull; foolish") indicates a state of being mentally unresponsive or stupefied. Together, 發呆(fādāi) refers to being in a mental state where one 'emits' or transitions into dullness or unresponsiveness, hence being 'in a daze'.
- **examples:**
  - 他坐在椅子上发(發)呆。
    - Tā zuò zài yǐzi shàng fādāi.
    - He sits in a chair in a daze.
  - 天气(氣)这(這)么(麼)好，为(為)什么(麼)你还(還)在发(發)呆？
    - Tiānqì zhème hǎo, wèishéme nǐ hái zài fādāi?
    - The weather is so nice, why are you still in a daze?
  - 她喜欢(歡)在黄(黃)昏时(時)分对(對)着(著)天空发(發)呆。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài huánghūn shífēn duìzhe tiānkōng fādāi.
    - She likes to be in a daze staring at the sky during dusk.
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發)
- **traditional:** 發
- **definition:** send out; emit; develop
- **pinyin:** fā
- **components:**
  - 攴
    - pū
    - hand
  - 癹
    - bā
    - foot steps, radical
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Pictogram of bow firing arrow ->
    - hand 攴 added ->
    - hand evolved to 癹 (phonetic) ->
    - final form 發
  - **interpretation:** 發 initially depicted a bow firing an arrow, symbolizing the idea of emitting or releasing. The added hand component indicated an action, aligning with the sense of 'issuing or emitting'. With 癹 serving the phonetic purpose, it unified into the character 發, emphasizing the concept of sending forth or dispatching, as in 'emit' or 'issue'.
  - **simplification:** 发 is the simplified form of 發, reducing the complex 癹 component into a simpler structure while retaining pronunciation.
- **examples:**
  - 公司明天会(會)发(發)布新产(產)品。
    - Gōngsī míngtiān huì fābù xīn chǎnpǐn.
    - The company will issue a new product tomorrow.
  - 她的表演发(發)出耀眼的光芒。
    - Tā de biǎoyǎn fāchū yàoyǎn de guāngmáng.
    - Her performance emitted a dazzling light.
  - 请(請)尽(盡)快发(發)送邮(郵)件。
    - Qǐng jǐnkuài fāsòng yóujiàn.
    - Please send the email as soon as possible.
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 攴
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩鼓面，传(傳)递(遞)出节(節)奏的信号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了一下门(門)，唤(喚)起了室内(內)的安静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 攴](@media/glyph6534.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 攴 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crack in an oracle bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜 (bǔ, 'divination') directly depicts a crack being used in oracle bones to divine future events. This literal representation naturally extends to the concept of divination.
- **examples:**
  - 在古代，人们(們)常用龟(龜)甲进(進)行卜卦。
    - Zài gǔdài, rénmen cháng yòng guījiǎ jìnxíng bǔguà.
    - In ancient times, people often used turtle shells for divination.
  - 他对(對)未来(來)充满(滿)疑虑(慮)，所以决(決)定找人卜卦。
    - Tā duì wèilái chōngmǎn yílǜ, suǒyǐ juédìng zhǎo rén bǔguà.
    - He was full of doubts about the future, so he decided to find someone for divination.
  - 在占星术(術)中，卜法常被用来(來)预(預)测(測)未来(來)。
    - Zài zhānxīngshù zhōng, bǔfǎ cháng bèi yòng lái yùcè wèilái.
    - In astrology, divination methods are often used to predict the future.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卜](@media/glyph535c.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 癹
- **definition:** foot steps, radical
- **pinyin:** bā
- **components:**
  - 癶
    - bō
    - two outstretched feet
  - 殳
    - shū
    - hand with stick
  - 撥
    - bō
    - to shift
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound and phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 癶 (bō, "two outstretched feet") + 殳 (shū, "hand with stick") =
    - to beat or cut grass ->
    - original form of 撥 (bō, "to shift")
  - **interpretation:** The character 癹 combines the pictogram of two outstretched feet with the image of a hand holding a stick. This represents an action involved in striking or cutting grass, linking it to actions of sorting or moving, hence its relationship to the concept behind 撥 (bō, "to shift"). As a phono-semantic compound, 癶 provides the sound and the notion of spreading or stretching, while 殳 emphasizes the action-related meaning.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 癹](@media/glyph7679.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 癹 → 癶
- **definition:** two outstretched feet
- **pinyin:** bō
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 止 (zhǐ, "foot") + 止 (zhǐ, "foot") =
    - two outstretched feet diverging ->
    - diverging direction
  - **interpretation:** The character 癶(bá) represents two feet moving in opposite directions, symbolizing divergence and movement. It contrasts with 舛 (chuǎn, "contradict"), which depicts convergent feet, highlighting different types of movement orientations.
- **examples:**
  - 古文字中有癶，象征(徵)着(著)两(兩)只(隻)伸出的脚(腳)。
    - Gǔ wénzì zhōng yǒu bá, xiàngzhēngzhe liǎng zhǐ shēnchū de jiǎo.
    - In ancient scripts, bá appears, symbolizing two outstretched feet.
  - 汉(漢)字构(構)造中含有癶，展现(現)出足部迅猛伸展的形态(態)。
    - Hànzì gòuzào zhōng hányǒu bá, zhǎnxiàn chū zúbù xùnměng shēnzhǎn de xíngtài.
    - Within the structure of Chinese characters, bá is incorporated, revealing the form of swiftly outstretched feet.
  - 癶象征(徵)着(著)两(兩)只(隻)外伸的脚(腳)。
    - Bá xiàngzhēngzhe liǎng zhǐ wài shēn de jiǎo.
    - Bá symbolizes two outstretched feet.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 癶](@media/glyph7676.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 癹 → 癶 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 癹 → 癶 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 癹 → 癶 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 癹 → 殳
- **definition:** hand with stick
- **pinyin:** shū
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - tool
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 𠘧 (hand) + 又 (tool) =
    - depicts hand holding a tool ->
    - borrowed meaning of bamboo halberd
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted a hand holding a tool, suggesting the action of beating. It was later borrowed to refer to a specific type of weapon, a bamboo halberd.
- **examples:**
  - 古代战(戰)场(場)上，殳曾被视(視)为(為)关(關)键(鍵)武器。
    - Gǔdài zhànchǎng shàng, shū céng bèi shì wéi guānjiàn wǔqì.
    - On ancient battlefields, the shū was once considered a crucial weapon.
  - 兵器展览(覽)中，殳闪(閃)耀着(著)历(歷)史的光芒。
    - Bīngqì zhǎnlǎn zhōng, shū shǎnyào zhe lìshǐ de guāngmáng.
    - In the arms exhibition, the shū shone with the brilliance of history.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 殳](@media/glyph6bb3.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 癹 → 撥
- **definition:** to shift
- **pinyin:** bō
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 發
    - fā
    - emit
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, "hand") + 發 (fā, "emit") =
    - hand action represented by a related sound ->
    - to push aside
  - **interpretation:** The character 撥(bō, "to push aside") combines 手 (shǒu, "hand") as a semantic element suggesting an action performed by hand with 發 (fā, "emit") to indicate the pronunciation. Together, they evoke the idea of using the hand to move something aside.
  - **simplification:** 撥 (bō, "to push aside") was simplified to 拨(撥) by retaining the hand radical 扌 (an abbreviated form of 手 (shǒu, "hand")) while preserving overall meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 他撥開桌上的雜物，露出光滑的桌面。
    - Tā bō kāi zhuō shàng de záwù, lù chū guānghuá de zhuōmiàn.
    - He pushed aside the clutter on the table, revealing the smooth tabletop.
  - 請撥開那塊大布，看看下面隱藏的秘密。
    - Qǐng bō kāi nà kuài dà bù, kàn kàn xiàmiàn yǐncáng de mìmì.
    - Please push aside that large cloth to see the hidden secret underneath.
### 发(發)呆 → 发(發) → 癹 → 撥 → 發
- **definition:** emit
- **pinyin:** fā
- **components:**
  - 癶
    - bó
    - stretch out
  - 殳
    - shū
    - a type of weapon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 癶 (stretch out) + phonetic 殳 (a type of weapon) ->
    - to issue
  - **interpretation:** The character 發(fā, "issue") combines the semantic element 癶(bó, "stretch out") representing action or movement, with the phonetic element 殳(shū, "a type of weapon") which provides the sound. The idea of stretching out or moving forward aligns with the notion of issuing or sending forth, whether it be an object, action, or command.
  - **simplification:** In the simplified form 发, the component 殳 (shū, "a type of weapon") was replaced with another element that retains the phonetic sound to reduce the number of strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 公司今天发(發)布(佈)了新的政策。
    - Gōngsī jīntiān fābù le xīn de zhèngcè.
    - The company issued a new policy today.
  - 他发(發)了一封邀请(請)函給我。
    - Tā fāle yī fēng yāoqǐng hán gěi wǒ.
    - He issued an invitation letter to me.
  - 老师(師)决(決)定不对(對)这(這)个(個)错(錯)误(誤)发(發)言。
    - Lǎoshī juédìng bù duì zhège cuòwù fāyán.
    - The teacher decided not to issue a comment on this mistake.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 發](@media/glyph767c.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 呆
- **definition:** dull; foolish
- **pinyin:** dāi
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant form of 保
  - **description:** Originally designated as a combination of 口 (kǒu, "mouth") and 木 (mù, "tree"), depicting a person standing still with an astonished mouth open under a tree, the character 呆 evolved as a variant of 保 (bǎo, "to protect") in historical contexts.
  - **interpretation:** The character 呆 conveys a sense of being motionless or stagnant, akin to a tree. Over time, it developed to express feelings of being dazed or dull, illustrating a motionless or blank state of mind.
- **examples:**
  - 他看起来很呆。
    - Tā kànqǐlái hěn dāi.
    - He looks very dazed.
  - 小明呆住了，眼神迷茫。
    - Xiǎomíng dāi zhù le, yǎnshén mímáng.
    - Xiaoming was stunned, his eyes were vacant.
  - 她发(發)呆了。
    - Tā fā dāi le.
    - She was lost in thought.
### 发(發)呆 → 呆 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 发(發)呆 → 呆 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)

## 呷哺呷哺

## Xiabu Xiabu hot pot chain
### xiā bǔ xiā bǔ
---
- **definition:** Xiabu Xiabu hot pot chain
- **pinyin:** xiā bǔ xiā bǔ
- **components:**
  - 呷哺
    - xiā bǔ
    - sip; nourish
  - 呷哺
    - xiā bǔ
    - sip; nourish
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 呷 (xiā, "sip") 哺 (bǔ, "nourish") 呷 (xiā, "sip") 哺 (bǔ, "nourish")
  - **interpretation:** The repetition of 呷 (xiā, "sip") and 哺 (bǔ, "nourish") suggests the act of savoring and being nourished by food, which perfectly encapsulates the dining experience at this hot pot chain. It reflects the social and communal aspect of sharing a meal in Chinese culture.
- **examples:**
  - 呷哺呷哺是一个(個)非常受欢(歡)迎的连(連)锁(鎖)火锅(鍋)店。
    - xiā bǔ xiā bǔ shì yīgè fēicháng shòu huānyíng de liánsuǒ huǒguō diàn.
    - Xiabu Xiabu is a very popular hot pot chain.
  - 我和朋友喜欢(歡)去呷哺呷哺，尝(嘗)试(試)各种(種)新口味。
    - wǒ hé péngyǒu xǐhuān qù xiā bǔ xiā bǔ, chángshì gè zhǒng xīn kǒuwèi.
    - My friends and I like to go to Xiabu Xiabu to try various new flavors.
  - 每次去呷哺呷哺，都能品尝(嚐)到独(獨)特的火锅(鍋)风(風)味。
    - měi cì qù xiā bǔ xiā bǔ, dōu néng pǐncháng dào dútè de huǒguō fēngwèi.
    - Every time I go to Xiabu Xiabu, I can taste a unique hot pot flavor.
### 呷哺呷哺 → 呷哺
- **definition:** sip; nourish
- **pinyin:** xiā bǔ
- **components:**
  - 呷
    - xiā
    - sip; take a sip
  - 哺
    - bǔ
    - nourish; feed; give breast milk
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 呷 (xiā, "sip") + 哺 (bǔ, "nourish") - combining to convey the meaning of 'sipping to nourish' as associated with consuming liquids or soft foods.
  - **interpretation:** The character 呷 (xiā, "sip") evokes the action of taking small amounts of liquid or food into the mouth, which is commonly done to savor or ease the digestion process. 哺 (bǔ, "nourish") involves feeding or providing sustenance, typically through gentle or care-filled means. Together, they construct an image of nurturing oneself or others by sipping, highlighting the delicate manner in which nourishment is obtained.
### 呷哺呷哺 → 呷哺 → 呷
- **definition:** sip; take a sip
- **pinyin:** xiā
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 甲
    - jiǎ
    - armor; shell; first
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 甲 (jiǎ)
  - **interpretation:** Combines 口 (kǒu, "mouth"), indicating an action involving the mouth, with 甲 (jiǎ) for its sound, to represent the action of sipping or drinking a small amount.
- **examples:**
  - 他轻(輕)轻(輕)地呷了一口茶。
    - Tā qīngqīng de xiā le yī kǒu chá.
    - He took a gentle sip of tea.
  - 她呷了一口咖啡，然后(後)继(繼)续(續)阅(閱)读(讀)。
    - Tā xiā le yī kǒu kāfēi, ránhòu jìxù yuèdú.
    - She took a sip of coffee, then continued reading.
  - 这(這)汤(湯)太烫(燙)了，只能呷一小口。
    - Zhè tāng tài tàng le, zhǐ néng xiā yī xiǎo kǒu.
    - This soup is too hot, can only sip a little.
- **historical forms:**

### 呷哺呷哺 → 呷哺 → 哺
- **definition:** nourish; feed; give breast milk
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 甫
    - fǔ
    - beginning
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 甫 (fǔ) ->
    - nourish; feed
  - **interpretation:** 哺 (bǔ, "nourish; feed") combines 口 (kǒu, "mouth"), indicating the act of feeding or nourishment through the mouth, with 甫 (fǔ) serving as the phonetic component, providing the sound. The meaning relates to using the mouth to provide sustenance or nourishment, thus evolving the sense of 'feed.'
- **examples:**
  - 母鸟(鳥)给(給)小鸟(鳥)哺食。
    - Mǔniǎo gěi xiǎoniǎo bǔshí.
    - The mother bird feeds the baby birds.
  - 父母哺育孩子成长(長)。
    - Fùmǔ bǔyù háizi chéngzhǎng.
    - Parents nourish and raise the children to grow.
  - 奶牛哺乳的小牛非常可爱(愛)。
    - Nǎiniú bǔrǔ de xiǎoniú fēicháng kě'ài.
    - The calves being nursed by the cows are very cute.
### 呷哺呷哺 → 呷哺 → 哺 → 甫
- **definition:** beginning
- **pinyin:** fǔ
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - vegetation
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
  - 父
    - fù
    - father
  - 用
    - yòng
    - to use
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 ('vegetation') + 田 ('field') =
    - garden ->
    - corrupted into 父 ('father') + 用 ('to use') ->
    - phono-semantic: 父 for sound
  - **interpretation:** Originally, 甫 depicted a piece of land or garden through the combination of vegetation (屮) and a field (田). Over time, the components evolved in script, with 父 becoming the phonetic element, contributing the sound. While originally referring to gardens, its phonetic role led to its modern use related to men or gentlemen.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小村庄(莊)只有一个(個)男子甫。
    - Zhège xiǎo cūnzhuāng zhǐyǒu yīgè nánzǐ fǔ.
    - This small village has only one man named Fu.
  - 甫是一位出色的画(畫)家。
    - Fǔ shì yī wèi chūsè de huàjiā.
    - Fu is an outstanding painter.
  - 他们(們)在讨(討)论(論)甫的生平。
    - Tāmen zài tǎolùn fǔ de shēngpíng.
    - They are discussing Fu's life.

  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润(潤)后(後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。

## 大栅(柵)栏(欄)
---
## historic commercial street in Beijing
### dà shí làn
---
- **traditional:** 大柵欄
- **definition:** historic commercial street in Beijing
- **pinyin:** dà shí làn
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big; great
  - 栅(柵)栏(欄)
    - shí lán
    - fence; barrier
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 大 (dà, "big; great") is used to signify importance or size. 柵(栅) (zhà, "fence; barrier") and 欄(栏) (lán, "rail; fence") together can form the sense of a barricade or structural barrier. Historically, this area in Beijing served as a bustling commercial hub, often characterized by notable structures and barriers.
  - **interpretation:** The combination 大 (dà, "big; great") with 柵(栅)欄(栏) (shí lán, "fence; barrier") suggests a significant place bounded or defined by notable structures, fitting for a prominent area like a major commercial street in Beijing which was well-established and recognizable by such features. It indicates both the historical significance and the structural aspect of this area.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)今天要去大栅(柵)栏(欄)。
    - Wǒmen jīntiān yào qù dà shí làn.
    - Today, we are going to Dàshílàn.
  - 大栅(柵)栏(欄)是一个(個)充满(滿)历(歷)史风(風)情的地方。
    - Dà shí làn shì yī gè chōngmǎn lìshǐ fēngqíng de dìfāng.
    - Dàshílàn is a place full of historical charm.
  - 游(遊)览(覽)完天安门(門)，我们(們)可以去大栅(柵)栏(欄)逛逛。
    - Yóulǎn wán tiānānmén, wǒmen kěyǐ qù dà shí làn guàng guàng.
    - After touring Tiananmen, we can visit Dàshílàn.
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 大
- **definition:** big; great
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)房子很大。
    - Zhè ge fángzi hěn dà.
    - This house is very big.
  - 大海波涛(濤)汹(洶)涌(湧)，展现(現)出大自然的力量。
    - Dàhǎi bōtāo xiōngyǒng, zhǎnxiàn chū dàzìrán de lìliàng.
    - The vast ocean waves surge, showcasing the power of nature.
  - 大人物登场(場)，留下传(傳)奇。
    - Dà rénwù dēngchǎng, liúxià chuánqí.
    - Great figures make an appearance, leaving behind legends.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 大](@media/glyph5927.png)
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 大 → 夫
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a variant form of 大 (dà, "big") representing an adult man with a hairpin ->
    - became associated with 夫 (fū, "man").
  - **interpretation:** 夫 (fū, "man") was visually similar to 大 (dà, "big") and was originally interchangeable. The addition of the horizontal stroke was interpreted as a hairpin, symbolizing adulthood for men.
- **examples:**
  - 此夫心怀(懷)大志。
    - Cǐ fū xīn huái dà zhì.
    - This man has lofty aspirations.
  - 他勤劳(勞)努力，堪称(稱)良夫。
    - Tā qín láo nǔ lì, kān chēng liáng fū.
    - He works diligently and is regarded as an exemplary man.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夫](@media/glyph592b.png)
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄)
- **traditional:** 柵欄
- **definition:** fence; barrier
- **pinyin:** shí lán
- **components:**
  - 栅(柵)
    - shàn
    - fence; palisade
  - 栏(欄)
    - lán
    - railing; bar; fence; pen
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 柵 (shàn, "fence") indicates a fence as a physical barrier, while 欄 (lán, "railing") emphasizes the structural support aspect. While these involve different semantic elements and might involve alternative readings, each pertains to physical boundary structures.
  - **interpretation:** 柵 (shàn, "fence") represents the protective function of a boundary structure, physically denoting a barrier for containment or defense. 欄 (lán, "railing") provides the sense of bars or support, further specifying the form or use, such as in rows or pen areas. Together, they imply a constructed boundary like those found in urban environments to enclose or guide movement.
- **examples:**
  - 那只(隻)猴子正在攀爬栅(柵)栏(欄)。
    - Nà zhī hóuzi zhèngzài pān pá shílàn.
    - The monkey is climbing the fence.
  - 他们(們)在花园(園)周围(圍)建了一个(個)新的栅(柵)栏(欄)。
    - Tāmen zài huāyuán zhōuwéi jiànle yī gè xīn de shílàn.
    - They built a new fence around the garden.
  - 孩子们(們)正在栅(柵)栏(欄)旁边(邊)玩耍。
    - Háizimen zhèngzài shílàn pángbiān wánshuǎ.
    - The children are playing near the fence.
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)
- **traditional:** 柵
- **definition:** fence; palisade
- **pinyin:** shàn
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree; wood
  - 冊
    - cè
    - a form made by lining up pieces of wood and binding them together
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "tree; wood") + phonetic 冊 (cè, "a form made by lining up pieces of wood and binding them together") ->
    - fence
  - **interpretation:** The character 柵 is composed of 木 (mù, "tree; wood"), suggesting materials made of wood, combined with the phonetic 冊 (cè, "a form made by lining up pieces of wood and binding them together"), which conveys the sense of arranging wood in a linear order. This fittingly describes a structure like a fence or palisade, which is essentially wood sections lined together.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)场(場)周围(圍)有一道高高的栅(柵)栏(欄)。
    - Nóngchǎng zhōuwéi yǒu yīdào gāogāo de zhàlán.
    - There is a high fence surrounding the farm.
  - 小路的尽(盡)头(頭)是一扇古老的木栅(柵)门(門)。
    - Xiǎolù de jìntóu shì yī shàn gǔlǎo de mù zhàmén.
    - At the end of the path lies an old wooden gate.
  - 工人正在修理受损(損)的栅(柵)栏(欄)。
    - Gōngrén zhèngzài xiūlǐ shòusǔn de zhàlán.
    - The worker is repairing the damaged fence.
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵) → 木
- **definition:** tree; wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵) → 冊
- **definition:** a form made by lining up pieces of wood and binding them together
- **pinyin:** cè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts bamboo slips strung together ->
    - books; documents
  - **interpretation:** The character 冊(cè, 'a form made by lining up pieces of wood and binding them together') represents bamboo slips tied together with string, symbolizing early forms of books or documents compiled in this manner.
  - **simplification:** 冊 was simplified to 册 by removing interior strokes, forming a more straightforward and less intricate version.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)本书(書)共有五冊。
    - Zhè běn shū gòngyǒu wǔ cè.
    - This book consists of five volumes.
  - 古代的册(冊)子是用竹片制作的。
    - Gǔdài de cèzi shì yòng zhúpiàn zhìzuò de.
    - Ancient booklets were made using bamboo strips.
  - 他在研究一件古老的册(冊)。
    - Tā zài yánjiū yī jiàn gǔlǎo de cè.
    - He is studying an ancient tome.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 冊](@media/glyph518a.png)
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栏(欄)
- **traditional:** 欄
- **definition:** railing; bar; fence; pen
- **pinyin:** lán
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 闌
    - lán
    - block
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 木 (mù, "wood") + 闌 (lán, "block") =
    - wood structure ->
    - railing
  - **interpretation:** The character 栏(欄) (lán, "railing") combines 木 (mù, "wood") for its structural material and the phonetic 闌 (lán, "block"). This indicates a barrier or partition made of wood, like a railing or fence.
  - **simplification:** Simplified 栏(欄) (lán, "railing") uses 兰 (lán, "orchid") from 闌 (lán) for phonetic similarity. This created a simpler form by reducing strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 楼(樓)梯旁的栏(欄)，防止了跌倒。
    - Lóutī páng de lán, fángzhǐ le diēdǎo.
    - The railing beside the stairs prevents falls.
  - 阳(陽)台(臺)外的栏(欄)，提供了安全保护(護)。
    - Yángtái wài de lán, tígōng le ānquán bǎohù.
    - The railing outside the balcony provides safety.
  - 城墙(牆)边(邊)的栏(欄)，俨(儼)然形成一道屏障。
    - Chéngqiáng biān de lán, yǎnrán xíngchéng yīdào píngzhàng.
    - The railing by the city wall forms a clear barrier.
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栏(欄) → 闌
- **definition:** block
- **pinyin:** lán
- **components:**
  - 門
    - mén
    - door
  - 柬
    - jiǎn
    - card
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 門 (mén, "door") + phonetic 柬 (jiǎn, "card") ->
    - block
  - **interpretation:** The character 闌(lán, "block") combines the semantic component 門 (mén, "door") with the phonetic component 柬 (jiǎn, "card"). The semantic element suggests a gateway or passage that can be closed or blocked, while the phonetic element contributes its sound. This reflects the idea of a barrier or closure, hence the meaning "block."
- **examples:**
  - 河水拦(攔)住了我们(們)的去路。
    - Héshuǐ lán zhùle wǒmen de qùlù.
    - The river blocked our way.
  - 警察在道路上设(設)立了拦(攔)截点(點)。
    - Jǐngchá zài dàolù shàng shèlìle lánjié diǎn.
    - The police set up a blockade on the road.
  - 他的计(計)划(劃)被家人拦(攔)下来(來)了。
    - Tā de jìhuà bèi jiārén lán xiàláile.
    - His plan was blocked by his family.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 闌](@media/glyph95cc.png)
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栏(欄) → 闌 → 門
- **definition:** door
- **pinyin:** mén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a double-door gate
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a pair of doors, visually representing the concept of a door or gate, which is fundamental in indicating entrance and exit points in structures.
- **examples:**
  - 我走到门(門)口。
    - Wǒ zǒu dào ménkǒu.
    - I walk to the door.
  - 门(門)轻(輕)轻(輕)打开(開)，房客进(進)来(來)了。
    - Mén qīngqīng dǎkāi, fángkè jìn láile.
    - The door opened gently, and the tenant came in.

### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栏(欄) → 闌 → 柬
- **definition:** card
- **pinyin:** jiǎn
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 音
    - yīn
    - sound
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 木 (mù, "wood") + 音 (yīn, "sound") =
    - phonetic element 音 with semantic 木(木, "wood") ->
    - card or written announcement on wood
  - **interpretation:** The character 柬 (jiǎn, "card") is a combination of 木 (mù, "wood") indicating material, and 音 (yīn, "sound") for phonetic purposes. Historically, messages and cards were written on wooden tablets.
- **examples:**
  - 我收到了一张(張)柬，邀请(請)我参(參)加聚会(會)。
    - Wǒ shōu dào le yī zhāng jiǎn, yāo qǐng wǒ cān jiā jù huì。
    - I received a card inviting me to attend a party.
  - 柬上写(寫)着(著)精美的图(圖)案，使人印象深刻。
    - Jiǎn shàng xiě zhe jīngměi de tú àn, shǐ rén yìnxiàng shēnkè。
    - The card is adorned with exquisite designs, which leave a deep impression.
  - 这(這)是一张(張)精致(緻)的柬。
    - Zhè shì yī zhāng jīngzhì de jiǎn。
    - This is an exquisite card.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 柬](@media/glyph67ec.png)
### 大栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栅(柵)栏(欄) → 栏(欄) → 闌 → 柬 → 音
- **definition:** sound
- **pinyin:** yīn
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - word
  - 甘
    - gān
    - sweet
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to say
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 言 (yán, "word") with 甘 (gān, "sweet") ->
    - a depiction of sound emanating from the mouth ->
    - 甘 stylized as 曰 (yuē) ->
    - final form 音
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a word or sound (言) coming from the mouth, initially represented by 甘 as the body of the tongue, which transforms into 曰. This evolution symbolizes the emergence of sound from the mouth, capturing the essence of 'sound' and 'tone.'
- **examples:**
  - 我最喜欢(歡)听(聽)大提琴的声(聲)音。
    - Wǒ zuì xǐhuān tīng dàtíqín de shēngyīn.
    - I love the sound of the cello the most.
  - 她的声(聲)音很悦(悅)耳。
    - Tā de shēngyīn hěn yuè'ěr.
    - Her voice is very pleasant.
  - 音乐(樂)可以抚(撫)慰人心，给(給)生活增添色彩。
    - Yīnyuè kěyǐ fǔwèi rénxīn, gěi shēnghuó zēngtiān sècǎi.
    - Music can soothe the soul and add color to life.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 音](@media/glyph97f3.png)
